# 2. DEVELOPMENT STAGES

## 2.1 Stage Documentation

```markdown
# NEXUS OS Development Roadmap

## Stage 1: Foundation (Months 1-3)
### Phase 1.1: Boot Infrastructure
- [x] UEFI/BIOS bootloader
- [x] Multiboot2 compliance
- [x] Initial kernel loading
- [x] Basic console output

### Phase 1.2: Core Kernel
- [x] GDT/IDT setup (x86_64)
- [x] Exception handling
- [x] Basic memory detection
- [x] Serial debugging

### Phase 1.3: Memory Management
- [x] Physical memory manager
- [x] Virtual memory (paging)
- [x] Kernel heap allocator
- [x] Memory mapping

## Stage 2: Process Management (Months 4-6)
### Phase 2.1: Scheduling
- [x] Process structures
- [x] Context switching
- [x] Basic round-robin scheduler
- [x] Priority scheduling

### Phase 2.2: Threading
- [x] Kernel threads
- [x] User threads
- [x] Thread local storage
- [x] SMP support

### Phase 2.3: Synchronization
- [x] Spinlocks
- [x] Mutexes
- [x] Semaphores
- [x] Read-write locks

## Stage 3: Hardware Abstraction (Months 7-9)
### Phase 3.1: HAL Core
- [ ] CPU abstraction
- [ ] Interrupt abstraction
- [ ] Timer abstraction
- [ ] DMA abstraction

### Phase 3.2: Driver Framework
- [ ] Driver model
- [ ] Bus enumeration
- [ ] Plug and play
- [ ] Power management

## Stage 4: Virtualization (Months 10-12)
### Phase 4.1: Hypervisor
- [ ] VMX/SVM detection
- [ ] VCPU management
- [ ] Memory virtualization
- [ ] I/O virtualization

### Phase 4.2: VM Management
- [ ] VM creation/destruction
- [ ] VM snapshots
- [ ] Live migration
- [ ] Resource allocation

## Stage 5: File Systems (Months 13-15)
### Phase 5.1: VFS Layer
- [ ] VFS core
- [ ] Inode management
- [ ] Directory operations
- [ ] File operations

### Phase 5.2: Native FS (NexFS)
- [ ] Disk layout
- [ ] Journaling
- [ ] Encryption
- [ ] Compression

## Stage 6: Networking (Months 16-18)
### Phase 6.1: Network Stack
- [ ] Socket layer
- [ ] TCP/IP implementation
- [ ] UDP implementation
- [ ] DNS resolver

### Phase 6.2: Advanced Networking
- [ ] Firewall
- [ ] VPN support
- [ ] Network virtualization
- [ ] QoS

## Stage 7: GUI System (Months 19-22)
### Phase 7.1: Graphics
- [ ] Framebuffer driver
- [ ] Hardware acceleration
- [ ] Compositor
- [ ] Window manager

### Phase 7.2: UI Framework
- [ ] Widget toolkit
- [ ] Theme engine
- [ ] Font rendering
- [ ] Animations

## Stage 8: AI/ML Integration (Months 23-25)
### Phase 8.1: AI Core
- [ ] Neural engine
- [ ] Model runtime
- [ ] NPU support
- [ ] GPU compute

### Phase 8.2: AI Services
- [ ] Voice recognition
- [ ] Image processing
- [ ] Predictive services
- [ ] On-device learning

## Stage 9: IoT & Mobile (Months 26-28)
### Phase 9.1: IoT Support
- [ ] IoT protocols
- [ ] Edge computing
- [ ] Device management
- [ ] Low-power modes

### Phase 9.2: Mobile Features
- [ ] Telephony
- [ ] Sensors
- [ ] Camera
- [ ] Battery management

## Stage 10: Polish & Release (Months 29-30)
### Phase 10.1: Testing
- [ ] Unit testing
- [ ] Integration testing
- [ ] Performance testing
- [ ] Security auditing

### Phase 10.2: Release
- [ ] Documentation
- [ ] SDK release
- [ ] Image creation
- [ ] Distribution
```

# 3. CORE KERNEL

## 3.1 Kernel Header (kernel/include/kernel.h)

```c
/*
 * NEXUS OS - Universal Operating System
 * Copyright (c) 2024 NEXUS Development Team
 * 
 * kernel.h - Core Kernel Definitions
 */

#ifndef _NEXUS_KERNEL_H
#define _NEXUS_KERNEL_H

#include "types.h"
#include "config.h"
#include "version.h"

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                            KERNEL CONFIGURATION                           */
/*===========================================================================*/

#define NEXUS_VERSION_MAJOR     1
#define NEXUS_VERSION_MINOR     0
#define NEXUS_VERSION_PATCH     0
#define NEXUS_VERSION_STRING    "1.0.0-alpha"
#define NEXUS_CODENAME          "Genesis"

/* Kernel Memory Layout */
#define KERNEL_VIRTUAL_BASE     0xFFFFFFFF80000000ULL
#define KERNEL_PHYSICAL_BASE    0x0000000000100000ULL
#define KERNEL_STACK_SIZE       (64 * 1024)             /* 64 KB */
#define KERNEL_HEAP_START       0xFFFFFFFF90000000ULL
#define KERNEL_HEAP_SIZE        (1024 * 1024 * 1024)    /* 1 GB */

/* Page Sizes */
#define PAGE_SIZE_4K            0x1000
#define PAGE_SIZE_2M            0x200000
#define PAGE_SIZE_1G            0x40000000
#define PAGE_SIZE               PAGE_SIZE_4K
#define PAGE_SHIFT              12

/* Maximum Limits */
#define MAX_CPUS                256
#define MAX_PROCESSES           65536
#define MAX_THREADS_PER_PROCESS 4096
#define MAX_OPEN_FILES          65536
#define MAX_MEMORY_REGIONS      1024

/* Scheduling */
#define SCHED_PRIORITY_MIN      0
#define SCHED_PRIORITY_DEFAULT  50
#define SCHED_PRIORITY_MAX      99
#define SCHED_TIME_SLICE_MS     10

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                              KERNEL TYPES                                 */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Basic Types */
typedef signed char         s8;
typedef unsigned char       u8;
typedef signed short        s16;
typedef unsigned short      u16;
typedef signed int          s32;
typedef unsigned int        u32;
typedef signed long long    s64;
typedef unsigned long long  u64;

typedef u64                 size_t;
typedef s64                 ssize_t;
typedef u64                 uintptr_t;
typedef s64                 intptr_t;
typedef s64                 ptrdiff_t;
typedef s64                 off_t;

typedef u64                 phys_addr_t;
typedef u64                 virt_addr_t;
typedef u64                 dma_addr_t;

typedef u32                 pid_t;
typedef u32                 tid_t;
typedef u32                 uid_t;
typedef u32                 gid_t;
typedef u32                 mode_t;
typedef s64                 time_t;

typedef int                 bool;
#define true                1
#define false               0
#define NULL                ((void*)0)

/* Atomic Types */
typedef struct {
    volatile s32 counter;
} atomic_t;

typedef struct {
    volatile s64 counter;
} atomic64_t;

/* Result Type */
typedef enum {
    NEXUS_OK                = 0,
    NEXUS_ERROR             = -1,
    NEXUS_ENOMEM            = -2,
    NEXUS_EINVAL            = -3,
    NEXUS_ENOENT            = -4,
    NEXUS_EBUSY             = -5,
    NEXUS_EACCES            = -6,
    NEXUS_EIO               = -7,
    NEXUS_ETIMEDOUT         = -8,
    NEXUS_ENOSYS            = -9,
    NEXUS_EEXIST            = -10,
    NEXUS_EAGAIN            = -11,
    NEXUS_ENODEV            = -12,
    NEXUS_ENOTSUPP          = -13,
} nexus_result_t;

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                           KERNEL STRUCTURES                               */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* List Structure */
struct list_head {
    struct list_head *next, *prev;
};

/* RB-Tree Node */
struct rb_node {
    unsigned long __rb_parent_color;
    struct rb_node *rb_right;
    struct rb_node *rb_left;
};

struct rb_root {
    struct rb_node *rb_node;
};

/* Reference Counter */
typedef struct {
    atomic_t refcount;
} kref_t;

/* Spinlock */
typedef struct {
    volatile u32 lock;
#ifdef CONFIG_DEBUG_SPINLOCK
    const char *name;
    void *owner;
    unsigned long flags;
#endif
} spinlock_t;

/* Mutex */
typedef struct {
    atomic_t count;
    spinlock_t wait_lock;
    struct list_head wait_list;
#ifdef CONFIG_DEBUG_MUTEX
    void *owner;
    const char *name;
#endif
} mutex_t;

/* RW Lock */
typedef struct {
    atomic_t readers;
    spinlock_t write_lock;
} rwlock_t;

/* Semaphore */
typedef struct {
    s32 count;
    spinlock_t lock;
    struct list_head wait_list;
} semaphore_t;

/* Wait Queue */
typedef struct {
    spinlock_t lock;
    struct list_head head;
} wait_queue_t;

typedef struct wait_queue_entry {
    struct list_head list;
    struct thread *thread;
    int flags;
} wait_queue_entry_t;

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                           CPU INFORMATION                                 */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* CPU Features */
typedef struct {
    /* Vendor Info */
    char vendor_string[16];
    char brand_string[64];
    
    /* Basic Info */
    u32 family;
    u32 model;
    u32 stepping;
    
    /* Feature Flags */
    u64 features;
    
    /* Cache Info */
    u32 l1_dcache_size;
    u32 l1_icache_size;
    u32 l2_cache_size;
    u32 l3_cache_size;
    u32 cache_line_size;
    
    /* Topology */
    u32 physical_cores;
    u32 logical_cores;
    u32 numa_nodes;
    
    /* Virtualization */
    bool has_vmx;           /* Intel VT-x */
    bool has_svm;           /* AMD-V */
    bool has_ept;           /* Extended Page Tables */
    bool has_npt;           /* Nested Page Tables */
    
    /* Security */
    bool has_smep;
    bool has_smap;
    bool has_pku;
    
    /* Performance */
    u32 max_frequency_mhz;
    u32 base_frequency_mhz;
} cpu_features_t;

/* Per-CPU Data */
typedef struct percpu_data {
    u32 cpu_id;
    u32 apic_id;
    u32 numa_node;
    
    /* Current Execution Context */
    struct thread *current_thread;
    struct process *current_process;
    
    /* Idle Thread */
    struct thread *idle_thread;
    
    /* Run Queue */
    struct run_queue *runqueue;
    
    /* Statistics */
    u64 context_switches;
    u64 interrupts;
    u64 idle_time;
    u64 busy_time;
    
    /* Timestamp */
    u64 last_tick;
    
    /* Stack */
    void *kernel_stack;
    void *irq_stack;
    void *nmi_stack;
    
    /* Preemption */
    s32 preempt_count;
    
    /* Architecture Specific */
    void *arch_data;
} percpu_data_t;

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                           KERNEL MACROS                                   */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Compiler Attributes */
#define __packed            __attribute__((packed))
#define __aligned(x)        __attribute__((aligned(x)))
#define __section(x)        __attribute__((section(x)))
#define __unused            __attribute__((unused))
#define __noreturn          __attribute__((noreturn))
#define __weak              __attribute__((weak))
#define __pure              __attribute__((pure))
#define __const             __attribute__((const))
#define __always_inline     inline __attribute__((always_inline))
#define __noinline          __attribute__((noinline))
#define __hot               __attribute__((hot))
#define __cold              __attribute__((cold))

/* Likely/Unlikely Branch Prediction */
#define likely(x)           __builtin_expect(!!(x), 1)
#define unlikely(x)         __builtin_expect(!!(x), 0)

/* Memory Barriers */
#define barrier()           __asm__ __volatile__("" ::: "memory")
#define mb()                __asm__ __volatile__("mfence" ::: "memory")
#define rmb()               __asm__ __volatile__("lfence" ::: "memory")
#define wmb()               __asm__ __volatile__("sfence" ::: "memory")

/* Utility Macros */
#define ARRAY_SIZE(arr)     (sizeof(arr) / sizeof((arr)[0]))
#define ALIGN(x, a)         (((x) + (a) - 1) & ~((a) - 1))
#define ALIGN_DOWN(x, a)    ((x) & ~((a) - 1))
#define IS_ALIGNED(x, a)    (((x) & ((a) - 1)) == 0)

#define MIN(a, b)           ((a) < (b) ? (a) : (b))
#define MAX(a, b)           ((a) > (b) ? (a) : (b))
#define CLAMP(x, lo, hi)    MIN(MAX(x, lo), hi)

#define BIT(n)              (1ULL << (n))
#define BITS_PER_LONG       64
#define BITS_PER_BYTE       8

#define KB(x)               ((x) * 1024ULL)
#define MB(x)               ((x) * 1024ULL * 1024ULL)
#define GB(x)               ((x) * 1024ULL * 1024ULL * 1024ULL)
#define TB(x)               ((x) * 1024ULL * 1024ULL * 1024ULL * 1024ULL)

/* Container Of */
#define container_of(ptr, type, member) ({                      \
    const typeof(((type *)0)->member) *__mptr = (ptr);          \
    (type *)((char *)__mptr - offsetof(type, member)); })

#define offsetof(type, member) ((size_t)&((type *)0)->member)

/* List Operations */
#define LIST_HEAD_INIT(name) { &(name), &(name) }
#define LIST_HEAD(name) struct list_head name = LIST_HEAD_INIT(name)

static inline void INIT_LIST_HEAD(struct list_head *list) {
    list->next = list;
    list->prev = list;
}

static inline void list_add(struct list_head *new, struct list_head *head) {
    head->next->prev = new;
    new->next = head->next;
    new->prev = head;
    head->next = new;
}

static inline void list_add_tail(struct list_head *new, struct list_head *head) {
    head->prev->next = new;
    new->prev = head->prev;
    new->next = head;
    head->prev = new;
}

static inline void list_del(struct list_head *entry) {
    entry->prev->next = entry->next;
    entry->next->prev = entry->prev;
}

static inline bool list_empty(const struct list_head *head) {
    return head->next == head;
}

#define list_entry(ptr, type, member) container_of(ptr, type, member)

#define list_for_each(pos, head) \
    for (pos = (head)->next; pos != (head); pos = pos->next)

#define list_for_each_safe(pos, n, head) \
    for (pos = (head)->next, n = pos->next; pos != (head); pos = n, n = pos->next)

#define list_for_each_entry(pos, head, member) \
    for (pos = list_entry((head)->next, typeof(*pos), member); \
         &pos->member != (head); \
         pos = list_entry(pos->member.next, typeof(*pos), member))

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                        KERNEL CORE FUNCTIONS                              */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Kernel Initialization */
void kernel_main(void);
void kernel_early_init(void);
void kernel_init(void);
void kernel_start_scheduler(void) __noreturn;

/* Panic and Assert */
void kernel_panic(const char *fmt, ...) __noreturn;
void kernel_oops(const char *msg);
void kernel_assert_failed(const char *expr, const char *file, int line);

#define PANIC(msg)          kernel_panic(msg)
#define BUG()               kernel_panic("BUG at %s:%d", __FILE__, __LINE__)
#define BUG_ON(cond)        do { if (unlikely(cond)) BUG(); } while(0)

#ifdef CONFIG_DEBUG
#define ASSERT(expr)        do { if (unlikely(!(expr))) \
                                kernel_assert_failed(#expr, __FILE__, __LINE__); \
                            } while(0)
#else
#define ASSERT(expr)        ((void)0)
#endif

/* Logging */
typedef enum {
    LOG_EMERG   = 0,    /* System is unusable */
    LOG_ALERT   = 1,    /* Action must be taken immediately */
    LOG_CRIT    = 2,    /* Critical conditions */
    LOG_ERR     = 3,    /* Error conditions */
    LOG_WARNING = 4,    /* Warning conditions */
    LOG_NOTICE  = 5,    /* Normal but significant condition */
    LOG_INFO    = 6,    /* Informational */
    LOG_DEBUG   = 7,    /* Debug-level messages */
} log_level_t;

int printk(const char *fmt, ...);
int vprintk(const char *fmt, __builtin_va_list args);

#define pr_emerg(fmt, ...)   printk("[EMERG] " fmt, ##__VA_ARGS__)
#define pr_alert(fmt, ...)   printk("[ALERT] " fmt, ##__VA_ARGS__)
#define pr_crit(fmt, ...)    printk("[CRIT] " fmt, ##__VA_ARGS__)
#define pr_err(fmt, ...)     printk("[ERROR] " fmt, ##__VA_ARGS__)
#define pr_warn(fmt, ...)    printk("[WARN] " fmt, ##__VA_ARGS__)
#define pr_notice(fmt, ...)  printk("[NOTICE] " fmt, ##__VA_ARGS__)
#define pr_info(fmt, ...)    printk("[INFO] " fmt, ##__VA_ARGS__)

#ifdef CONFIG_DEBUG
#define pr_debug(fmt, ...)   printk("[DEBUG] " fmt, ##__VA_ARGS__)
#else
#define pr_debug(fmt, ...)   ((void)0)
#endif

/* Atomic Operations */
static inline s32 atomic_read(const atomic_t *v) {
    return v->counter;
}

static inline void atomic_set(atomic_t *v, s32 i) {
    v->counter = i;
}

static inline void atomic_inc(atomic_t *v) {
    __asm__ __volatile__("lock; incl %0" : "+m"(v->counter));
}

static inline void atomic_dec(atomic_t *v) {
    __asm__ __volatile__("lock; decl %0" : "+m"(v->counter));
}

static inline bool atomic_dec_and_test(atomic_t *v) {
    unsigned char c;
    __asm__ __volatile__("lock; decl %0; sete %1"
                         : "+m"(v->counter), "=qm"(c) :: "memory");
    return c != 0;
}

static inline s32 atomic_add_return(s32 i, atomic_t *v) {
    return __sync_add_and_fetch(&v->counter, i);
}

static inline s32 atomic_cmpxchg(atomic_t *v, s32 old, s32 new) {
    return __sync_val_compare_and_swap(&v->counter, old, new);
}

/* Time */
u64 get_ticks(void);
u64 get_time_ns(void);
u64 get_time_ms(void);
void delay_ms(u64 ms);
void delay_us(u64 us);

/* Memory */
void *kmalloc(size_t size);
void *kzalloc(size_t size);
void *krealloc(void *ptr, size_t new_size);
void kfree(void *ptr);

void *vmalloc(size_t size);
void vfree(void *ptr);

void *memcpy(void *dest, const void *src, size_t n);
void *memset(void *s, int c, size_t n);
void *memmove(void *dest, const void *src, size_t n);
int memcmp(const void *s1, const void *s2, size_t n);

/* String */
size_t strlen(const char *s);
char *strcpy(char *dest, const char *src);
char *strncpy(char *dest, const char *src, size_t n);
int strcmp(const char *s1, const char *s2);
int strncmp(const char *s1, const char *s2, size_t n);
char *strcat(char *dest, const char *src);
char *strchr(const char *s, int c);
char *strrchr(const char *s, int c);
char *strdup(const char *s);

/* Per-CPU */
percpu_data_t *get_percpu(void);
u32 get_cpu_id(void);
u32 get_num_cpus(void);

#define this_cpu()          get_percpu()
#define current_thread()    (this_cpu()->current_thread)
#define current_process()   (this_cpu()->current_process)

/* Preemption */

void preempt_enable(void);
bool preempt_enabled(void);

#endif /* _NEXUS_KERNEL_H */

## 3.2 Kernel Core (kernel/core/kernel.c)

```c
/*
 * NEXUS OS - Kernel Core
 * kernel/core/kernel.c
 */

#include <kernel.h>
#include <arch/cpu.h>
#include <mm/mm.h>
#include <sched/scheduler.h>
#include <drivers/driver.h>
#include <virt/hypervisor.h>
#include <fs/vfs.h>
#include <net/network.h>
#include <security/security.h>
#include <ai_ml/ai_engine.h>

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                           KERNEL STATE                                    */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Kernel Information */
static struct kernel_info {
    const char *version;
    const char *codename;
    const char *build_date;
    const char *build_time;
    const char *compiler;
    
    /* Boot Information */
    u64 boot_time;
    phys_addr_t kernel_start;
    phys_addr_t kernel_end;
    
    /* System State */
    enum {
        KERNEL_STATE_BOOTING,
        KERNEL_STATE_INITIALIZING,
        KERNEL_STATE_RUNNING,
        KERNEL_STATE_SHUTTING_DOWN,
        KERNEL_STATE_HALTED,
    } state;
    
    /* Configuration */
    struct {
        bool virtualization_enabled;
        bool ai_acceleration_enabled;
        bool iot_mode;
        bool mobile_mode;
        bool server_mode;
        bool debug_mode;
    } config;
    
    /* Statistics */
    struct {
        u64 uptime_seconds;
        u64 context_switches;
        u64 interrupts_handled;
        u64 syscalls_processed;
        u64 page_faults;
    } stats;
    
} kernel_info = {
    .version = NEXUS_VERSION_STRING,
    .codename = NEXUS_CODENAME,
    .build_date = __DATE__,
    .build_time = __TIME__,
#ifdef __clang__
    .compiler = "Clang " __clang_version__,
#else
    .compiler = "GCC " __VERSION__,
#endif
    .state = KERNEL_STATE_BOOTING,
};

/* Boot Parameters */
static struct boot_params {
    char cmdline[1024];
    u64 initrd_start;
    u64 initrd_size;
    u32 framebuffer_addr;
    u32 framebuffer_width;
    u32 framebuffer_height;
    u32 framebuffer_pitch;
    u32 framebuffer_bpp;
    u32 memory_map_entries;
    struct memory_map_entry {
        u64 base;
        u64 length;
        u32 type;
    } memory_map[256];
} boot_params;

/* CPU Information */
static cpu_features_t cpu_features[MAX_CPUS];
static percpu_data_t percpu_data[MAX_CPUS];
static u32 num_cpus = 1;
static u32 boot_cpu_id = 0;

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                     KERNEL INITIALIZATION                                 */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Early Initialization (Before Memory Setup) */
void kernel_early_init(void)
{
    /* Initialize Serial Console for Debugging */
    serial_init();
    
    /* Display Boot Banner */
    printk("\n");
    printk("===============================================\n");
    printk("  NEXUS OS v%s (%s)\n", kernel_info.version, kernel_info.codename);
    printk("  Built: %s %s\n", kernel_info.build_date, kernel_info.build_time);
    printk("  Compiler: %s\n", kernel_info.compiler);
    printk("===============================================\n");
    printk("\n");
    
    /* Parse Boot Parameters */
    parse_boot_params(&boot_params);
    
    /* Initialize Architecture-Specific Early Code */
    arch_early_init();
    
    /* Detect CPU Features */
    pr_info("Detecting CPU...\n");
    detect_cpu_features(&cpu_features[0]);
    pr_info("  Vendor: %s\n", cpu_features[0].vendor_string);
    pr_info("  Brand: %s\n", cpu_features[0].brand_string);
    pr_info("  Cores: %d physical, %d logical\n", 
            cpu_features[0].physical_cores, cpu_features[0].logical_cores);
    
    /* Check Virtualization Support */
    if (cpu_features[0].has_vmx) {
        pr_info("  Virtualization: Intel VT-x supported\n");
        kernel_info.config.virtualization_enabled = true;
    } else if (cpu_features[0].has_svm) {
        pr_info("  Virtualization: AMD-V supported\n");
        kernel_info.config.virtualization_enabled = true;
    }
    
    /* Initialize Basic Memory Management */
    pr_info("Initializing memory...\n");
    pmm_early_init(&boot_params);
    
    pr_info("Early initialization complete.\n");
}

/* Main Kernel Initialization */
void kernel_init(void)
{
    kernel_info.state = KERNEL_STATE_INITIALIZING;
    
    pr_info("Starting kernel initialization...\n");
    
    /*=== Stage 1: Core Systems ===*/
    pr_info("[Stage 1] Core Systems\n");
    
    /* Initialize Interrupt Handling */
    pr_info("  Initializing interrupts...\n");
    irq_init();
    
    /* Initialize Physical Memory Manager */
    pr_info("  Initializing physical memory manager...\n");
    pmm_init();
    
    /* Initialize Virtual Memory Manager */
    pr_info("  Initializing virtual memory manager...\n");
    vmm_init();
    
    /* Initialize Kernel Heap */
    pr_info("  Initializing kernel heap...\n");
    heap_init();
    
    /* Initialize Slab Allocator */
    pr_info("  Initializing slab allocator...\n");
    slab_init();
    
    /*=== Stage 2: Hardware Abstraction ===*/
    pr_info("[Stage 2] Hardware Abstraction\n");
    
    /* Initialize HAL */
    pr_info("  Initializing HAL...\n");
    hal_init();
    
    /* Initialize ACPI/Device Tree */
    pr_info("  Initializing firmware interface...\n");
    acpi_init();
    
    /* Initialize Timer */
    pr_info("  Initializing timer...\n");
    timer_init();
    
    /* Initialize SMP */
    pr_info("  Initializing SMP...\n");
    num_cpus = smp_init(percpu_data, MAX_CPUS);
    pr_info("  Found %d CPUs\n", num_cpus);
    
    /*=== Stage 3: Process Management ===*/
    pr_info("[Stage 3] Process Management\n");
    
    /* Initialize Scheduler */
    pr_info("  Initializing scheduler...\n");
    scheduler_init();
    
    /* Initialize Process Manager */
    pr_info("  Initializing process manager...\n");
    process_init();
    
    /* Initialize IPC */
    pr_info("  Initializing IPC...\n");
    ipc_init();
    
    /*=== Stage 4: Driver Framework ===*/
    pr_info("[Stage 4] Driver Framework\n");
    
    /* Initialize Driver Framework */
    pr_info("  Initializing driver framework...\n");
    driver_framework_init();
    
    /* Initialize PCI/PCIe */
    pr_info("  Initializing PCI subsystem...\n");
    pci_init();
    
    /* Initialize USB */
    pr_info("  Initializing USB subsystem...\n");
    usb_init();
    
    /* Probe and Load Drivers */
    pr_info("  Probing hardware...\n");
    driver_probe_all();
    
    /*=== Stage 5: Virtualization ===*/
    if (kernel_info.config.virtualization_enabled) {
        pr_info("[Stage 5] Virtualization\n");
        
        pr_info("  Initializing hypervisor...\n");
        hypervisor_init();
        
        pr_info("  Initializing VM manager...\n");
        vm_manager_init();
        
        pr_info("  Initializing container support...\n");
        container_init();
    }
    
    /*=== Stage 6: File Systems ===*/
    pr_info("[Stage 6] File Systems\n");
    
    /* Initialize VFS */
    pr_info("  Initializing VFS...\n");
    vfs_init();
    
    /* Register File Systems */
    pr_info("  Registering file systems...\n");
    nexfs_init();
    fat32_init();
    ext4_init();
    
    /* Mount Root File System */
    pr_info("  Mounting root filesystem...\n");
    mount_root();
    
    /*=== Stage 7: Networking ===*/
    pr_info("[Stage 7] Networking\n");
    
    /* Initialize Network Stack */
    pr_info("  Initializing network stack...\n");
    network_init();
    
    /* Initialize Protocols */
    pr_info("  Initializing network protocols...\n");
    tcp_init();
    udp_init();
    
    /* Initialize Firewall */
    pr_info("  Initializing firewall...\n");
    firewall_init();
    
    /*=== Stage 8: Security ===*/
    pr_info("[Stage 8] Security\n");
    
    /* Initialize Security Manager */
    pr_info("  Initializing security manager...\n");
    security_init();
    
    /* Initialize Crypto */
    pr_info("  Initializing cryptography...\n");
    crypto_init();
    
    /* Initialize Sandbox */
    pr_info("  Initializing sandbox...\n");
    sandbox_init();
    
    /*=== Stage 9: AI/ML (Optional) ===*/
    if (kernel_info.config.ai_acceleration_enabled) {
        pr_info("[Stage 9] AI/ML Engine\n");
        
        pr_info("  Initializing AI engine...\n");
        ai_engine_init();
        
        pr_info("  Initializing NPU...\n");
        npu_init();
    }
    
    /*=== Stage 10: Final Setup ===*/
    pr_info("[Stage 10] Final Setup\n");
    
    /* Initialize System Call Interface */
    pr_info("  Initializing syscalls...\n");
    syscall_init();
    
    /* Start Init Process */
    pr_info("  Starting init process...\n");
    start_init();
    
    kernel_info.state = KERNEL_STATE_RUNNING;
    kernel_info.boot_time = get_time_ms();
    
    pr_info("\n");
    pr_info("===============================================\n");
    pr_info("  NEXUS OS Initialization Complete!\n");
    pr_info("  Boot time: %llu ms\n", kernel_info.boot_time);
    pr_info("===============================================\n");
    pr_info("\n");
}

/* Start Scheduler (Never Returns) */
void __noreturn kernel_start_scheduler(void)
{
    pr_info("Starting scheduler on CPU %d...\n", get_cpu_id());
    
    /* Enable Interrupts */
    local_irq_enable();
    
    /* Enter Scheduler */
    scheduler_start();
    
    /* Should Never Reach Here */
    kernel_panic("Scheduler returned!");
}

/* Main Entry Point */
void kernel_main(void)
{
    /* Early Initialization */
    kernel_early_init();
    
    /* Full Initialization */
    kernel_init();
    
    /* Start Scheduler */
    kernel_start_scheduler();
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                          PANIC HANDLING                                   */
/*===========================================================================*/

static spinlock_t panic_lock = {0};
static volatile bool panic_in_progress = false;

void __noreturn kernel_panic(const char *fmt, ...)
{
    unsigned long flags;
    __builtin_va_list args;
    
    /* Prevent Recursive Panics */
    local_irq_save(flags);
    
    if (panic_in_progress) {
        /* Recursive panic - halt immediately */
        for (;;) {
            arch_halt();
        }
    }
    
    panic_in_progress = true;
    
    /* Stop Other CPUs */
    smp_send_stop();
    
    /* Print Panic Message */
    printk("\n");
    printk("!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!\n");
    printk("!!           KERNEL PANIC                    !!\n");
    printk("!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!\n");
    printk("\n");
    
    __builtin_va_start(args, fmt);
    vprintk(fmt, args);
    __builtin_va_end(args);
    
    printk("\n\n");
    
    /* Print CPU Info */
    printk("CPU: %d\n", get_cpu_id());
    
    /* Print Stack Trace */
    printk("\nStack Trace:\n");
    dump_stack();
    
    /* Print Register State */
    printk("\nRegister State:\n");
    dump_registers();
    
    /* Print Memory Info */
    printk("\nMemory State:\n");
    dump_memory_info();
    
    /* Halt */
    printk("\nSystem Halted.\n");
    
    for (;;) {
        arch_halt();
    }
}

void kernel_oops(const char *msg)
{
    printk("\n");
    printk("!!! OOPS: %s !!!\n", msg);
    printk("\n");
    
    dump_stack();
    
    /* Kill Current Process */
    if (current_process()) {
        process_kill(current_process(), -1);
    }
    
    schedule();
}

void kernel_assert_failed(const char *expr, const char *file, int line)
{
    kernel_panic("ASSERTION FAILED: %s\nFile: %s, Line: %d", expr, file, line);
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                         UTILITY FUNCTIONS                                 */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Per-CPU Data Access */
percpu_data_t *get_percpu(void)
{
    return &percpu_data[get_cpu_id()];
}

u32 get_cpu_id(void)
{
    return arch_get_cpu_id();
}

u32 get_num_cpus(void)
{
    return num_cpus;
}

/* Get Kernel Info */
const struct kernel_info *get_kernel_info(void)
{
    return &kernel_info;
}
```

## 3.3 Print/Logging (kernel/core/printk.c)

```c
/*
 * NEXUS OS - Kernel Print Functions
 * kernel/core/printk.c
 */

#include <kernel.h>
#include <stdarg.h>

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                           PRINT BUFFER                                    */
/*===========================================================================*/

#define PRINTK_BUFFER_SIZE  4096
#define LOG_BUFFER_SIZE     (1024 * 1024)   /* 1MB Log Buffer */

static char printk_buffer[PRINTK_BUFFER_SIZE];
static char log_buffer[LOG_BUFFER_SIZE];
static u64 log_buffer_head = 0;
static u64 log_buffer_tail = 0;
static spinlock_t printk_lock = {0};

/* Output Drivers */
static void (*console_output)(const char *str, size_t len) = NULL;
static void (*serial_output)(const char *str, size_t len) = NULL;
static void (*framebuffer_output)(const char *str, size_t len) = NULL;

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                      NUMBER TO STRING CONVERSION                          */
/*===========================================================================*/

static const char hex_digits[] = "0123456789abcdef";
static const char HEX_DIGITS[] = "0123456789ABCDEF";

static int format_uint(char *buf, u64 value, int base, bool upper, 
                       int width, char pad, bool is_signed)
{
    char tmp[65];
    const char *digits = upper ? HEX_DIGITS : hex_digits;
    int i = 0;
    int len;
    bool negative = false;
    
    if (is_signed && (s64)value < 0) {
        negative = true;
        value = -(s64)value;
    }
    
    if (value == 0) {
        tmp[i++] = '0';
    } else {
        while (value > 0) {
            tmp[i++] = digits[value % base];
            value /= base;
        }
    }
    
    if (negative) {
        tmp[i++] = '-';
    }
    
    /* Reverse */
    len = i;
    
    /* Padding */
    int pad_count = width - len;
    int pos = 0;
    
    if (pad_count > 0 && pad == '0' && negative) {
        buf[pos++] = '-';
        len--;
        i--;
    }
    
    while (pad_count-- > 0) {
        buf[pos++] = pad;
    }
    
    while (i > 0) {
        if (!(negative && i == len && pad == '0')) {
            buf[pos++] = tmp[--i];
        } else {
            i--;
        }
    }
    
    return pos;
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                          PRINTF IMPLEMENTATION                            */
/*===========================================================================*/

int vsnprintf(char *buf, size_t size, const char *fmt, va_list args)
{
    char *str = buf;
    char *end = buf + size - 1;
    
    for (; *fmt && str < end; fmt++) {
        if (*fmt != '%') {
            *str++ = *fmt;
            continue;
        }
        
        fmt++;
        
        /* Flags */
        char pad = ' ';
        bool left_justify = false;
        bool prefix = false;
        bool upper = false;
        
        while (*fmt == '-' || *fmt == '0' || *fmt == '#' || *fmt == '+') {
            if (*fmt == '-') left_justify = true;
            else if (*fmt == '0') pad = '0';
            else if (*fmt == '#') prefix = true;
            fmt++;
        }
        
        /* Width */
        int width = 0;
        if (*fmt == '*') {
            width = va_arg(args, int);
            fmt++;
        } else {
            while (*fmt >= '0' && *fmt <= '9') {
                width = width * 10 + (*fmt - '0');
                fmt++;
            }
        }
        
        /* Precision */
        int precision = -1;
        if (*fmt == '.') {
            fmt++;
            if (*fmt == '*') {
                precision = va_arg(args, int);
                fmt++;
            } else {
                precision = 0;
                while (*fmt >= '0' && *fmt <= '9') {
                    precision = precision * 10 + (*fmt - '0');
                    fmt++;
                }
            }
        }
        
        /* Length Modifier */
        int length = 0;  /* 0=int, 1=long, 2=long long */
        if (*fmt == 'l') {
            length = 1;
            fmt++;
            if (*fmt == 'l') {
                length = 2;
                fmt++;
            }
        } else if (*fmt == 'h') {
            length = -1;
            fmt++;
            if (*fmt == 'h') {
                length = -2;
                fmt++;
            }
        } else if (*fmt == 'z') {
            length = 2;
            fmt++;
        }
        
        /* Conversion Specifier */
        char tmp[128];
        int len = 0;
        
        switch (*fmt) {
        case 'd':
        case 'i': {
            s64 val;
            if (length == 2) val = va_arg(args, s64);
            else if (length == 1) val = va_arg(args, long);
            else val = va_arg(args, int);
            len = format_uint(tmp, val, 10, false, width, pad, true);
            break;
        }
        
        case 'u': {
            u64 val;
            if (length == 2) val = va_arg(args, u64);
            else if (length == 1) val = va_arg(args, unsigned long);
            else val = va_arg(args, unsigned int);
            len = format_uint(tmp, val, 10, false, width, pad, false);
            break;
        }
        
        case 'x':
        case 'X': {
            u64 val;
            if (length == 2) val = va_arg(args, u64);
            else if (length == 1) val = va_arg(args, unsigned long);
            else val = va_arg(args, unsigned int);
            
            if (prefix && val != 0) {
                *str++ = '0';
                if (str < end) *str++ = (*fmt == 'X') ? 'X' : 'x';
            }
            
            len = format_uint(tmp, val, 16, *fmt == 'X', width, pad, false);
            break;
        }
        
        case 'p': {
            u64 val = (u64)va_arg(args, void*);
            *str++ = '0';
            if (str < end) *str++ = 'x';
            len = format_uint(tmp, val, 16, false, 16, '0', false);
            break;
        }
        
        case 's': {
            const char *s = va_arg(args, const char*);
            if (!s) s = "(null)";
            while (*s && str < end) {
                *str++ = *s++;
            }
            continue;
        }
        
        case 'c':
            *str++ = (char)va_arg(args, int);
            continue;
        
        case '%':
            *str++ = '%';
            continue;
        
        default:
            *str++ = '%';
            if (str < end) *str++ = *fmt;
            continue;
        }
        
        /* Copy Formatted Number */
        for (int i = 0; i < len && str < end; i++) {
            *str++ = tmp[i];
        }
    }
    
    *str = '\0';
    return str - buf;
}

int snprintf(char *buf, size_t size, const char *fmt, ...)
{
    va_list args;
    va_start(args, fmt);
    int ret = vsnprintf(buf, size, fmt, args);
    va_end(args);
    return ret;
}

int sprintf(char *buf, const char *fmt, ...)
{
    va_list args;
    va_start(args, fmt);
    int ret = vsnprintf(buf, 4096, fmt, args);
    va_end(args);
    return ret;
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                           PRINTK                                          */
/*===========================================================================*/

int vprintk(const char *fmt, va_list args)
{
    unsigned long flags;
    int len;
    
    spin_lock_irqsave(&printk_lock, flags);
    
    len = vsnprintf(printk_buffer, PRINTK_BUFFER_SIZE, fmt, args);
    
    /* Store in Log Buffer */
    for (int i = 0; i < len && i < PRINTK_BUFFER_SIZE; i++) {
        log_buffer[log_buffer_head % LOG_BUFFER_SIZE] = printk_buffer[i];
        log_buffer_head++;
        
        if (log_buffer_head - log_buffer_tail > LOG_BUFFER_SIZE) {
            log_buffer_tail = log_buffer_head - LOG_BUFFER_SIZE;
        }
    }
    
    /* Output to Consoles */
    if (serial_output) {
        serial_output(printk_buffer, len);
    }
    
    if (console_output) {
        console_output(printk_buffer, len);
    }
    
    if (framebuffer_output) {
        framebuffer_output(printk_buffer, len);
    }
    
    spin_unlock_irqrestore(&printk_lock, flags);
    
    return len;
}

int printk(const char *fmt, ...)
{
    va_list args;
    va_start(args, fmt);
    int ret = vprintk(fmt, args);
    va_end(args);
    return ret;
}

/* Register Output Drivers */
void register_console_output(void (*output)(const char*, size_t))
{
    console_output = output;
}

void register_serial_output(void (*output)(const char*, size_t))
{
    serial_output = output;
}

void register_framebuffer_output(void (*output)(const char*, size_t))
{
    framebuffer_output = output;
}

/* Read Log Buffer */
size_t read_log_buffer(char *buf, size_t size, u64 *offset)
{
    size_t copied = 0;
    
    spin_lock(&printk_lock);
    
    if (*offset < log_buffer_tail) {
        *offset = log_buffer_tail;
    }
    
    while (*offset < log_buffer_head && copied < size) {
        buf[copied++] = log_buffer[(*offset)++ % LOG_BUFFER_SIZE];
    }
    
    spin_unlock(&printk_lock);
    
    return copied;
}
```

---

# 4. HARDWARE ABSTRACTION LAYER (HAL)

## 4.1 HAL Interface (hal/hal_interface.h)

```c
/*
 * NEXUS OS - Hardware Abstraction Layer Interface
 * hal/hal_interface.h
 */

#ifndef _NEXUS_HAL_H
#define _NEXUS_HAL_H

#include <kernel.h>

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                          HAL CONFIGURATION                                */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Supported Architectures */
typedef enum {
    ARCH_X86_64,
    ARCH_ARM64,
    ARCH_RISCV64,
    ARCH_UNKNOWN,
} arch_type_t;

/* Supported Platforms */
typedef enum {
    PLATFORM_PC,
    PLATFORM_SERVER,
    PLATFORM_MOBILE,
    PLATFORM_EMBEDDED,
    PLATFORM_IOT,
    PLATFORM_VM,
} platform_type_t;

/* HAL Capabilities */
typedef struct {
    /* CPU Features */
    bool has_smp;
    bool has_numa;
    bool has_simd;
    bool has_crypto_accel;
    
    /* Memory */
    bool has_iommu;
    bool has_huge_pages;
    bool has_memory_encryption;
    
    /* Power */
    bool has_acpi;
    bool has_device_tree;
    bool has_power_management;
    
    /* Virtualization */
    bool has_hardware_virt;
    bool has_nested_virt;
    
    /* I/O */
    bool has_pci;
    bool has_usb;
    bool has_nvme;
    
} hal_capabilities_t;

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                          CPU ABSTRACTION                                  */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* CPU Operations */
typedef struct {
    /* Initialization */
    int (*init)(void);
    int (*init_secondary)(u32 cpu_id);
    
    /* CPU Control */
    void (*halt)(void);
    void (*enable_interrupts)(void);
    void (*disable_interrupts)(void);
    unsigned long (*save_flags)(void);
    void (*restore_flags)(unsigned long flags);
    
    /* CPU ID */
    u32 (*get_cpu_id)(void);
    u32 (*get_apic_id)(void);
    
    /* Cache Operations */
    void (*flush_cache)(void);
    void (*flush_cache_range)(void *start, size_t size);
    void (*invalidate_cache)(void);
    void (*invalidate_cache_range)(void *start, size_t size);
    
    /* TLB Operations */
    void (*flush_tlb)(void);
    void (*flush_tlb_page)(virt_addr_t addr);
    void (*flush_tlb_range)(virt_addr_t start, virt_addr_t end);
    
    /* Context */
    void (*switch_context)(void *from, void *to);
    void (*save_fpu_state)(void *state);
    void (*restore_fpu_state)(void *state);
    
    /* Power */
    void (*enter_idle)(void);
    void (*enter_sleep)(int level);
    void (*wakeup_cpu)(u32 cpu_id);
    
    /* Features */
    void (*detect_features)(cpu_features_t *features);
    
} cpu_ops_t;

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                       INTERRUPT ABSTRACTION                               */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Interrupt Handler Type */
typedef enum {
    IRQ_TYPE_LEVEL_HIGH,
    IRQ_TYPE_LEVEL_LOW,
    IRQ_TYPE_EDGE_RISING,
    IRQ_TYPE_EDGE_FALLING,
    IRQ_TYPE_EDGE_BOTH,
} irq_type_t;

/* Interrupt Handler */
typedef int (*irq_handler_t)(u32 irq, void *data);

/* IRQ Descriptor */
typedef struct {
    u32 irq_num;
    irq_type_t type;
    irq_handler_t handler;
    void *data;
    const char *name;
    u32 target_cpu;
    bool shared;
    atomic_t count;
} irq_desc_t;

/* Interrupt Controller Operations */
typedef struct {
    /* Initialization */
    int (*init)(void);
    
    /* IRQ Management */
    int (*request_irq)(u32 irq, irq_handler_t handler, 
                       irq_type_t type, const char *name, void *data);
    void (*free_irq)(u32 irq, void *data);
    
    /* IRQ Control */
    void (*enable_irq)(u32 irq);
    void (*disable_irq)(u32 irq);
    void (*mask_irq)(u32 irq);
    void (*unmask_irq)(u32 irq);
    void (*ack_irq)(u32 irq);
    void (*eoi_irq)(u32 irq);
    
    /* IRQ Routing */
    int (*set_irq_affinity)(u32 irq, u64 cpu_mask);
    int (*set_irq_type)(u32 irq, irq_type_t type);
    
    /* IPI */
    void (*send_ipi)(u32 target_cpu, u32 vector);
    void (*send_ipi_all)(u32 vector);
    void (*send_ipi_others)(u32 vector);
    
} irq_controller_ops_t;

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                        TIMER ABSTRACTION                                  */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Timer Callback */
typedef void (*timer_callback_t)(void *data);

/* Timer Types */
typedef enum {
    TIMER_TYPE_ONESHOT,
    TIMER_TYPE_PERIODIC,
} timer_type_t;

/* Timer Structure */
typedef struct timer {
    struct list_head list;
    u64 expires;
    timer_type_t type;
    u64 interval;
    timer_callback_t callback;
    void *data;
    bool active;
} timer_t;

/* Timer Operations */
typedef struct {
    /* Initialization */
    int (*init)(void);
    
    /* Clock Source */
    u64 (*read_cycles)(void);
    u64 (*read_ns)(void);
    u64 (*get_frequency)(void);
    
    /* Timer Management */
    int (*setup_timer)(timer_t *timer, timer_callback_t callback, void *data);
    int (*start_timer)(timer_t *timer, u64 expires_ns, timer_type_t type);
    int (*stop_timer)(timer_t *timer);
    int (*modify_timer)(timer_t *timer, u64 expires_ns);
    
    /* Delay */
    void (*delay_ns)(u64 ns);
    void (*delay_us)(u64 us);
    void (*delay_ms)(u64 ms);
    
    /* Tick */
    void (*set_tick_rate)(u32 hz);
    
} timer_ops_t;

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                         MEMORY ABSTRACTION                                */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Memory Region Type */
typedef enum {
    MEM_TYPE_USABLE,
    MEM_TYPE_RESERVED,
    MEM_TYPE_ACPI_RECLAIMABLE,
    MEM_TYPE_ACPI_NVS,
    MEM_TYPE_BAD,
    MEM_TYPE_MMIO,
    MEM_TYPE_KERNEL,
} mem_type_t;

/* Memory Region */
typedef struct {
    phys_addr_t base;
    size_t size;
    mem_type_t type;
    u32 numa_node;
    u32 flags;
} mem_region_t;

/* Page Table Entry Flags */
typedef enum {
    PTE_PRESENT     = BIT(0),
    PTE_WRITABLE    = BIT(1),
    PTE_USER        = BIT(2),
    PTE_PWT         = BIT(3),
    PTE_PCD         = BIT(4),
    PTE_ACCESSED    = BIT(5),
    PTE_DIRTY       = BIT(6),
    PTE_HUGE        = BIT(7),
    PTE_GLOBAL      = BIT(8),
    PTE_NX          = BIT(63),
} pte_flags_t;

/* Memory Operations */
typedef struct {
    /* Initialization */
    int (*init)(void);
    
    /* Memory Map */
    int (*get_memory_map)(mem_region_t *regions, u32 *count);
    u64 (*get_total_memory)(void);
    u64 (*get_usable_memory)(void);
    
    /* Page Table */
    phys_addr_t (*create_page_table)(void);
    void (*destroy_page_table)(phys_addr_t pt);
    int (*map_page)(phys_addr_t pt, virt_addr_t vaddr, 
                    phys_addr_t paddr, u64 flags);
    int (*unmap_page)(phys_addr_t pt, virt_addr_t vaddr);
    phys_addr_t (*translate)(phys_addr_t pt, virt_addr_t vaddr);
    
    /* Page Table Switching */
    void (*load_page_table)(phys_addr_t pt);
    phys_addr_t (*get_current_page_table)(void);
    
    /* Cache Control */
    void (*set_memory_type)(virt_addr_t vaddr, size_t size, int type);
    
    /* IOMMU */
    int (*iommu_map)(void *domain, u64 iova, phys_addr_t paddr, 
                     size_t size, int flags);
    int (*iommu_unmap)(void *domain, u64 iova, size_t size);
    
} memory_ops_t;

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                         POWER MANAGEMENT                                  */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Power States */
typedef enum {
    POWER_STATE_ON,
    POWER_STATE_STANDBY,
    POWER_STATE_SUSPEND,
    POWER_STATE_HIBERNATE,
    POWER_STATE_OFF,
} power_state_t;

/* CPU Power States */
typedef enum {
    CPU_C0,     /* Active */
    CPU_C1,     /* Halt */
    CPU_C2,     /* Stop-Clock */
    CPU_C3,     /* Sleep */
    CPU_C6,     /* Deep Sleep */
} cpu_cstate_t;

/* Power Operations */
typedef struct {
    /* Initialization */
    int (*init)(void);
    
    /* System Power */
    int (*set_power_state)(power_state_t state);
    power_state_t (*get_power_state)(void);
    void (*reboot)(void);
    void (*shutdown)(void);
    
    /* CPU Power */
    int (*set_cpu_cstate)(u32 cpu_id, cpu_cstate_t state);
    int (*set_cpu_frequency)(u32 cpu_id, u32 freq_mhz);
    u32 (*get_cpu_frequency)(u32 cpu_id);
    
    /* Device Power */
    int (*set_device_power)(void *device, int state);
    int (*get_device_power)(void *device);
    
} power_ops_t;

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                           HAL INTERFACE                                   */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Main HAL Structure */
typedef struct {
    /* Architecture Info */
    arch_type_t arch;
    platform_type_t platform;
    hal_capabilities_t caps;
    
    /* Operation Tables */
    cpu_ops_t *cpu;
    irq_controller_ops_t *irq;
    timer_ops_t *timer;
    memory_ops_t *memory;
    power_ops_t *power;
    
} hal_t;

/* HAL Global Instance */
extern hal_t hal;

/* HAL Functions */
int hal_init(void);
int hal_late_init(void);
arch_type_t hal_get_arch(void);
platform_type_t hal_get_platform(void);
const hal_capabilities_t *hal_get_capabilities(void);

/* Architecture Detection */
static inline bool is_x86_64(void) { return hal.arch == ARCH_X86_64; }
static inline bool is_arm64(void) { return hal.arch == ARCH_ARM64; }
static inline bool is_riscv64(void) { return hal.arch == ARCH_RISCV64; }

/* Convenience Functions */
static inline void arch_halt(void) { hal.cpu->halt(); }
static inline u32 arch_get_cpu_id(void) { return hal.cpu->get_cpu_id(); }
static inline void arch_flush_tlb(void) { hal.cpu->flush_tlb(); }

#endif /* _NEXUS_HAL_H */
```

## 4.2 x86_64 CPU Implementation (kernel/arch/x86_64/cpu/cpu.c)

```c
/*
 * NEXUS OS - x86_64 CPU Implementation
 * kernel/arch/x86_64/cpu/cpu.c
 */

#include <kernel.h>
#include <hal/hal_interface.h>
#include <arch/x86_64/cpu.h>
#include <arch/x86_64/msr.h>
#include <arch/x86_64/cpuid.h>

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                          CPU ID & REGISTERS                               */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* CPUID Functions */
static inline void cpuid(u32 leaf, u32 subleaf, 
                         u32 *eax, u32 *ebx, u32 *ecx, u32 *edx)
{
    __asm__ __volatile__(
        "cpuid"
        : "=a"(*eax), "=b"(*ebx), "=c"(*ecx), "=d"(*edx)
        : "a"(leaf), "c"(subleaf)
    );
}

/* MSR Functions */
static inline u64 rdmsr(u32 msr)
{
    u32 low, high;
    __asm__ __volatile__(
        "rdmsr"
        : "=a"(low), "=d"(high)
        : "c"(msr)
    );
    return ((u64)high << 32) | low;
}

static inline void wrmsr(u32 msr, u64 value)
{
    __asm__ __volatile__(
        "wrmsr"
        :
        : "c"(msr), "a"((u32)value), "d"((u32)(value >> 32))
    );
}

/* Control Registers */
static inline u64 read_cr0(void)
{
    u64 val;
    __asm__ __volatile__("mov %%cr0, %0" : "=r"(val));
    return val;
}

static inline void write_cr0(u64 val)
{
    __asm__ __volatile__("mov %0, %%cr0" : : "r"(val));
}

static inline u64 read_cr2(void)
{
    u64 val;
    __asm__ __volatile__("mov %%cr2, %0" : "=r"(val));
    return val;
}

static inline u64 read_cr3(void)
{
    u64 val;
    __asm__ __volatile__("mov %%cr3, %0" : "=r"(val));
    return val;
}

static inline void write_cr3(u64 val)
{
    __asm__ __volatile__("mov %0, %%cr3" : : "r"(val) : "memory");
}

static inline u64 read_cr4(void)
{
    u64 val;
    __asm__ __volatile__("mov %%cr4, %0" : "=r"(val));
    return val;
}

static inline void write_cr4(u64 val)
{
    __asm__ __volatile__("mov %0, %%cr4" : : "r"(val));
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                           CPU OPERATIONS                                  */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Initialize BSP */
static int x86_cpu_init(void)
{
    pr_info("Initializing x86_64 CPU...\n");
    
    /* Enable SSE/SSE2/SSE3 */
    u64 cr0 = read_cr0();
    cr0 &= ~(1UL << 2);     /* Clear EM */
    cr0 |= (1UL << 1);      /* Set MP */
    write_cr0(cr0);
    
    u64 cr4 = read_cr4();
    cr4 |= (1UL << 9);      /* OSFXSR */
    cr4 |= (1UL << 10);     /* OSXMMEXCPT */
    write_cr4(cr4);
    
    /* Enable XSAVE if available */
    u32 eax, ebx, ecx, edx;
    cpuid(1, 0, &eax, &ebx, &ecx, &edx);
    
    if (ecx & (1 << 26)) {
        cr4 = read_cr4();
        cr4 |= (1UL << 18);  /* OSXSAVE */
        write_cr4(cr4);
        
        /* Enable AVX */
        u64 xcr0 = 0;
        xcr0 |= (1 << 0);    /* X87 */
        xcr0 |= (1 << 1);    /* SSE */
        xcr0 |= (1 << 2);    /* AVX */
        __asm__ __volatile__("xsetbv" : : "a"((u32)xcr0), "d"((u32)(xcr0 >> 32)), "c"(0));
    }
    
    /* Enable SMEP/SMAP if available */
    cpuid(7, 0, &eax, &ebx, &ecx, &edx);
    
    if (ebx & (1 << 7)) {   /* SMEP */
        cr4 = read_cr4();
        cr4 |= (1UL << 20);
        write_cr4(cr4);
        pr_info("  SMEP enabled\n");
    }
    
    if (ebx & (1 << 20)) {  /* SMAP */
        cr4 = read_cr4();
        cr4 |= (1UL << 21);
        write_cr4(cr4);
        pr_info("  SMAP enabled\n");
    }
    
    /* Enable NX bit */
    u64 efer = rdmsr(MSR_EFER);
    efer |= (1UL << 11);    /* NXE */
    wrmsr(MSR_EFER, efer);
    
    /* Set up SYSCALL/SYSRET */
    wrmsr(MSR_STAR, ((u64)KERNEL_CS << 32) | ((u64)(USER_CS - 16) << 48));
    wrmsr(MSR_LSTAR, (u64)syscall_entry);
    wrmsr(MSR_SFMASK, 0x200);  /* Mask IF */
    
    /* Enable SYSCALL */
    efer = rdmsr(MSR_EFER);
    efer |= (1UL << 0);     /* SCE */
    wrmsr(MSR_EFER, efer);
    
    return NEXUS_OK;
}

/* Initialize Secondary CPU */
static int x86_cpu_init_secondary(u32 cpu_id)
{
    pr_info("Initializing secondary CPU %d...\n", cpu_id);
    
    /* Same initialization as BSP */
    x86_cpu_init();
    
    /* Set up per-CPU structures */
    wrmsr(MSR_GS_BASE, (u64)&percpu_data[cpu_id]);
    
    return NEXUS_OK;
}

/* Halt CPU */
static void x86_cpu_halt(void)
{
    __asm__ __volatile__("hlt");
}

/* Enable Interrupts */
static void x86_enable_interrupts(void)
{
    __asm__ __volatile__("sti");
}

/* Disable Interrupts */
static void x86_disable_interrupts(void)
{
    __asm__ __volatile__("cli");
}

/* Save Flags */
static unsigned long x86_save_flags(void)
{
    unsigned long flags;
    __asm__ __volatile__(
        "pushfq\n\t"
        "pop %0\n\t"
        "cli"
        : "=r"(flags)
        :
        : "memory"
    );
    return flags;
}

/* Restore Flags */
static void x86_restore_flags(unsigned long flags)
{
    __asm__ __volatile__(
        "push %0\n\t"
        "popfq"
        :
        : "r"(flags)
        : "memory"
    );
}

/* Get CPU ID */
static u32 x86_get_cpu_id(void)
{
    /* Use GSBASE per-CPU data */
    percpu_data_t *percpu;
    __asm__ __volatile__(
        "movq %%gs:0, %0"
        : "=r"(percpu)
    );
    return percpu ? percpu->cpu_id : 0;
}

/* Get APIC ID */
static u32 x86_get_apic_id(void)
{
    u32 eax, ebx, ecx, edx;
    cpuid(1, 0, &eax, &ebx, &ecx, &edx);
    return (ebx >> 24) & 0xFF;
}

/* Flush All Caches */
static void x86_flush_cache(void)
{
    __asm__ __volatile__("wbinvd" ::: "memory");
}

/* Flush Cache Range */
static void x86_flush_cache_range(void *start, size_t size)
{
    u8 *ptr = (u8 *)start;
    u8 *end = ptr + size;
    
    for (; ptr < end; ptr += 64) {
        __asm__ __volatile__("clflush (%0)" : : "r"(ptr) : "memory");
    }
    
    __asm__ __volatile__("mfence" ::: "memory");
}

/* Invalidate Cache */
static void x86_invalidate_cache(void)
{
    __asm__ __volatile__("invd" ::: "memory");
}

/* Invalidate Cache Range */
static void x86_invalidate_cache_range(void *start, size_t size)
{
    u8 *ptr = (u8 *)start;
    u8 *end = ptr + size;
    
    for (; ptr < end; ptr += 64) {
        __asm__ __volatile__("clflushopt (%0)" : : "r"(ptr) : "memory");
    }
}

/* Flush TLB */
static void x86_flush_tlb(void)
{
    write_cr3(read_cr3());
}

/* Flush Single TLB Entry */
static void x86_flush_tlb_page(virt_addr_t addr)
{
    __asm__ __volatile__("invlpg (%0)" : : "r"(addr) : "memory");
}

/* Flush TLB Range */
static void x86_flush_tlb_range(virt_addr_t start, virt_addr_t end)
{
    for (virt_addr_t addr = start; addr < end; addr += PAGE_SIZE) {
        x86_flush_tlb_page(addr);
    }
}

/* Context Switch */
static void x86_switch_context(void *from_ctx, void *to_ctx)
{
    struct cpu_context *from = (struct cpu_context *)from_ctx;
    struct cpu_context *to = (struct cpu_context *)to_ctx;
    
    __asm__ __volatile__(
        /* Save Current Context */
        "pushfq\n\t"
        "pushq %%rbp\n\t"
        "pushq %%rbx\n\t"
        "pushq %%r12\n\t"
        "pushq %%r13\n\t"
        "pushq %%r14\n\t"
        "pushq %%r15\n\t"
        
        /* Save Stack Pointer */
        "movq %%rsp, %0\n\t"
        
        /* Load New Stack Pointer */
        "movq %1, %%rsp\n\t"
        
        /* Restore New Context */
        "popq %%r15\n\t"
        "popq %%r14\n\t"
        "popq %%r13\n\t"
        "popq %%r12\n\t"
        "popq %%rbx\n\t"
        "popq %%rbp\n\t"
        "popfq"
        
        : "=m"(from->rsp)
        : "m"(to->rsp)
        : "memory"
    );
}

/* Save FPU/SSE/AVX State */
static void x86_save_fpu_state(void *state)
{
    __asm__ __volatile__(
        "fxsave64 (%0)"
        :
        : "r"(state)
        : "memory"
    );
}

/* Restore FPU/SSE/AVX State */
static void x86_restore_fpu_state(void *state)
{
    __asm__ __volatile__(
        "fxrstor64 (%0)"
        :
        : "r"(state)
    );
}

/* Enter Idle State */
static void x86_enter_idle(void)
{
    __asm__ __volatile__(
        "sti\n\t"
        "hlt"
    );
}

/* Enter Sleep State */
static void x86_enter_sleep(int level)
{
    /* Use MWAIT for C-States if available */
    u32 eax, ebx, ecx, edx;
    cpuid(5, 0, &eax, &ebx, &ecx, &edx);
    
    if (ecx & 1) {
        /* MWAIT supported */
        u32 cstate_hint = level;  /* C-State number */
        __asm__ __volatile__(
            "monitor\n\t"
            "mwait"
            :
            : "a"(0), "c"(0), "d"(0)
        );
    } else {
        /* Fall back to HLT */
        x86_enter_idle();
    }
}

/* Wake Up CPU via IPI */
static void x86_wakeup_cpu(u32 cpu_id)
{
    /* Send IPI to wake up target CPU */
    lapic_send_ipi(cpu_id, IPI_VECTOR_WAKEUP);
}

/* Detect CPU Features */
static void x86_detect_features(cpu_features_t *features)
{
    u32 eax, ebx, ecx, edx;
    
    /* Get Vendor String */
    cpuid(0, 0, &eax, &ebx, &ecx, &edx);
    *((u32 *)&features->vendor_string[0]) = ebx;
    *((u32 *)&features->vendor_string[4]) = edx;
    *((u32 *)&features->vendor_string[8]) = ecx;
    features->vendor_string[12] = '\0';
    
    /* Get Brand String */
    cpuid(0x80000002, 0, &eax, &ebx, &ecx, &edx);
    *((u32 *)&features->brand_string[0]) = eax;
    *((u32 *)&features->brand_string[4]) = ebx;
    *((u32 *)&features->brand_string[8]) = ecx;
    *((u32 *)&features->brand_string[12]) = edx;
    
    cpuid(0x80000003, 0, &eax, &ebx, &ecx, &edx);
    *((u32 *)&features->brand_string[16]) = eax;
    *((u32 *)&features->brand_string[20]) = ebx;
    *((u32 *)&features->brand_string[24]) = ecx;
    *((u32 *)&features->brand_string[28]) = edx;
    
    cpuid(0x80000004, 0, &eax, &ebx, &ecx, &edx);
    *((u32 *)&features->brand_string[32]) = eax;
    *((u32 *)&features->brand_string[36]) = ebx;
    *((u32 *)&features->brand_string[40]) = ecx;
    *((u32 *)&features->brand_string[44]) = edx;
    features->brand_string[48] = '\0';
    
    /* Get Family/Model/Stepping */
    cpuid(1, 0, &eax, &ebx, &ecx, &edx);
    features->stepping = eax & 0xF;
    features->model = ((eax >> 4) & 0xF) | ((eax >> 12) & 0xF0);
    features->family = ((eax >> 8) & 0xF) + ((eax >> 20) & 0xFF);
    
    /* Store Feature Flags */
    features->features = ((u64)ecx << 32) | edx;
    
    /* Check Virtualization */
    features->has_vmx = !!(ecx & (1 << 5));
    features->has_svm = false;  /* AMD-V checked separately */
    
    /* AMD-V Check */
    if (features->vendor_string[0] == 'A') {
        cpuid(0x80000001, 0, &eax, &ebx, &ecx, &edx);
        features->has_svm = !!(ecx & (1 << 2));
    }
    
    /* Extended Features */
    cpuid(7, 0, &eax, &ebx, &ecx, &edx);
    features->has_smep = !!(ebx & (1 << 7));
    features->has_smap = !!(ebx & (1 << 20));
    
    /* Topology Information */
    cpuid(0xB, 0, &eax, &ebx, &ecx, &edx);
    features->logical_cores = ebx & 0xFFFF;
    
    cpuid(0xB, 1, &eax, &ebx, &ecx, &edx);
    features->physical_cores = (ebx & 0xFFFF) / 2;  /* Assuming HT */
    
    /* Cache Information */
    cpuid(0x80000006, 0, &eax, &ebx, &ecx, &edx);
    features->cache_line_size = ecx & 0xFF;
    features->l2_cache_size = ((ecx >> 16) & 0xFFFF) * 1024;
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                         CPU OPERATIONS TABLE                              */
/*===========================================================================*/

cpu_ops_t x86_cpu_ops = {
    .init = x86_cpu_init,
    .init_secondary = x86_cpu_init_secondary,
    .halt = x86_cpu_halt,
    .enable_interrupts = x86_enable_interrupts,
    .disable_interrupts = x86_disable_interrupts,
    .save_flags = x86_save_flags,
    .restore_flags = x86_restore_flags,
    .get_cpu_id = x86_get_cpu_id,
    .get_apic_id = x86_get_apic_id,
    .flush_cache = x86_flush_cache,
    .flush_cache_range = x86_flush_cache_range,
    .invalidate_cache = x86_invalidate_cache,
    .invalidate_cache_range = x86_invalidate_cache_range,
    .flush_tlb = x86_flush_tlb,
    .flush_tlb_page = x86_flush_tlb_page,
    .flush_tlb_range = x86_flush_tlb_range,
    .switch_context = x86_switch_context,
    .save_fpu_state = x86_save_fpu_state,
    .restore_fpu_state = x86_restore_fpu_state,
    .enter_idle = x86_enter_idle,
    .enter_sleep = x86_enter_sleep,
    .wakeup_cpu = x86_wakeup_cpu,
    .detect_features = x86_detect_features,
};
```

---

# 5. MEMORY MANAGEMENT

## 5.1 Physical Memory Manager (kernel/mm/pmm.c)

```c
/*
 * NEXUS OS - Physical Memory Manager
 * kernel/mm/pmm.c
 */

#include <kernel.h>
#include <mm/mm.h>
#include <mm/pmm.h>

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                     PHYSICAL MEMORY STRUCTURES                            */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Page Frame Structure */
typedef struct page_frame {
    struct list_head list;
    atomic_t refcount;
    u32 flags;
    u32 order;          /* For buddy allocator */
    void *private;
} page_frame_t;

/* Page Flags */
#define PG_RESERVED     BIT(0)
#define PG_ALLOCATED    BIT(1)
#define PG_KERNEL       BIT(2)
#define PG_USER         BIT(3)
#define PG_DMA          BIT(4)
#define PG_SLAB         BIT(5)
#define PG_LOCKED       BIT(6)
#define PG_DIRTY        BIT(7)

/* Memory Zone */
typedef enum {
    ZONE_DMA,           /* 0 - 16 MB */
    ZONE_DMA32,         /* 16 MB - 4 GB */
    ZONE_NORMAL,        /* 4 GB+ */
    ZONE_HIGHMEM,       /* High Memory (32-bit only) */
    NUM_ZONES,
} zone_type_t;

/* Free Area for Buddy Allocator */
typedef struct {
    struct list_head free_list;
    u64 free_count;
} free_area_t;

#define MAX_ORDER       11      /* Max 2^11 = 2048 pages = 8MB */

/* Memory Zone Structure */
typedef struct memory_zone {
    const char *name;
    zone_type_t type;
    
    /* Physical Range */
    phys_addr_t start;
    phys_addr_t end;
    
    /* Free Areas (Buddy System) */
    free_area_t free_area[MAX_ORDER];
    
    /* Statistics */
    u64 total_pages;
    u64 free_pages;
    u64 reserved_pages;
    
    /* Lock */
    spinlock_t lock;
} memory_zone_t;

/* Page Frame Database */
static page_frame_t *page_frames = NULL;
static u64 total_page_frames = 0;
static phys_addr_t max_physical_address = 0;

/* Memory Zones */
static memory_zone_t zones[NUM_ZONES] = {
    [ZONE_DMA] = { .name = "DMA", .start = 0, .end = MB(16) },
    [ZONE_DMA32] = { .name = "DMA32", .start = MB(16), .end = GB(4) },
    [ZONE_NORMAL] = { .name = "Normal", .start = GB(4), .end = 0 },
};

/* Total Memory */
static u64 total_memory = 0;
static u64 free_memory = 0;

/* PMM Lock */
static spinlock_t pmm_lock = {0};

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                          HELPER FUNCTIONS                                 */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Physical Address to Page Frame Number */
static inline u64 phys_to_pfn(phys_addr_t addr)
{
    return addr >> PAGE_SHIFT;
}

/* Page Frame Number to Physical Address */
static inline phys_addr_t pfn_to_phys(u64 pfn)
{
    return pfn << PAGE_SHIFT;
}

/* Get Page Frame from Physical Address */
static inline page_frame_t *phys_to_page(phys_addr_t addr)
{
    u64 pfn = phys_to_pfn(addr);
    if (pfn >= total_page_frames) {
        return NULL;
    }
    return &page_frames[pfn];
}

/* Get Physical Address from Page Frame */
static inline phys_addr_t page_to_phys(page_frame_t *page)
{
    return pfn_to_phys(page - page_frames);
}

/* Get Zone for Physical Address */
static memory_zone_t *get_zone_for_addr(phys_addr_t addr)
{
    for (int i = 0; i < NUM_ZONES; i++) {
        if (addr >= zones[i].start && addr < zones[i].end) {
            return &zones[i];
        }
    }
    return &zones[ZONE_NORMAL];
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                        BUDDY ALLOCATOR                                    */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Get Buddy Address */
static inline phys_addr_t get_buddy_addr(phys_addr_t addr, u32 order)
{
    return addr ^ (PAGE_SIZE << order);
}

/* Check if Pages Can Be Merged */
static bool can_merge(page_frame_t *page, u32 order)
{
    phys_addr_t addr = page_to_phys(page);
    phys_addr_t buddy_addr = get_buddy_addr(addr, order);
    
    /* Check if buddy is within bounds */
    if (buddy_addr >= max_physical_address) {
        return false;
    }
    
    page_frame_t *buddy = phys_to_page(buddy_addr);
    
    /* Buddy must be free and same order */
    if (buddy->flags & PG_ALLOCATED) {
        return false;
    }
    
    if (buddy->order != order) {
        return false;
    }
    
    /* Must be in same zone */
    memory_zone_t *zone1 = get_zone_for_addr(addr);
    memory_zone_t *zone2 = get_zone_for_addr(buddy_addr);
    
    return zone1 == zone2;
}

/* Add Pages to Free List */
static void buddy_add_to_free_list(memory_zone_t *zone, page_frame_t *page, u32 order)
{
    ASSERT(order < MAX_ORDER);
    
    page->order = order;
    page->flags &= ~PG_ALLOCATED;
    
    list_add(&page->list, &zone->free_area[order].free_list);
    zone->free_area[order].free_count++;
    zone->free_pages += (1UL << order);
}

/* Remove Pages from Free List */
static void buddy_remove_from_free_list(memory_zone_t *zone, page_frame_t *page, u32 order)
{
    ASSERT(order < MAX_ORDER);
    
    list_del(&page->list);
    zone->free_area[order].free_count--;
}

/* Allocate Pages (Buddy System) */
static phys_addr_t buddy_alloc_pages(memory_zone_t *zone, u32 order)
{
    ASSERT(order < MAX_ORDER);
    
    /* Find Free Block */
    u32 current_order = order;
    
    while (current_order < MAX_ORDER) {
        if (!list_empty(&zone->free_area[current_order].free_list)) {
            /* Found free block */
            page_frame_t *page = list_entry(
                zone->free_area[current_order].free_list.next,
                page_frame_t, list
            );
            
            buddy_remove_from_free_list(zone, page, current_order);
            
            /* Split if necessary */
            while (current_order > order) {
                current_order--;
                
                /* Get buddy half */
                phys_addr_t buddy_addr = page_to_phys(page) + (PAGE_SIZE << current_order);
                page_frame_t *buddy = phys_to_page(buddy_addr);
                
                /* Add buddy to free list */
                buddy_add_to_free_list(zone, buddy, current_order);
            }
            
            /* Mark as allocated */
            page->flags |= PG_ALLOCATED;
            page->order = order;
            atomic_set(&page->refcount, 1);
            
            zone->free_pages -= (1UL << order);
            
            return page_to_phys(page);
        }
        
        current_order++;
    }
    
    return 0;  /* No memory */
}

/* Free Pages (Buddy System) */
static void buddy_free_pages(memory_zone_t *zone, phys_addr_t addr, u32 order)
{
    ASSERT(order < MAX_ORDER);
    
    page_frame_t *page = phys_to_page(addr);
    
    ASSERT(page->flags & PG_ALLOCATED);
    
    /* Try to merge with buddies */
    while (order < MAX_ORDER - 1) {
        if (!can_merge(page, order)) {
            break;
        }
        
        /* Get buddy */
        phys_addr_t buddy_addr = get_buddy_addr(addr, order);
        page_frame_t *buddy = phys_to_page(buddy_addr);
        
        /* Remove buddy from free list */
        buddy_remove_from_free_list(zone, buddy, order);
        
        /* Use lower address as base */
        if (buddy_addr < addr) {
            page = buddy;
            addr = buddy_addr;
        }
        
        order++;
    }
    
    /* Add to free list */
    buddy_add_to_free_list(zone, page, order);
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                         PMM INITIALIZATION                                */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Early Initialization (Before Heap) */
void pmm_early_init(struct boot_params *params)
{
    pr_info("PMM Early Init: Analyzing memory map...\n");
    
    /* Calculate Total Memory */
    for (u32 i = 0; i < params->memory_map_entries; i++) {
        struct memory_map_entry *entry = &params->memory_map[i];
        
        if (entry->type == 1) {  /* Usable */
            total_memory += entry->length;
        }
        
        phys_addr_t end = entry->base + entry->length;
        if (end > max_physical_address) {
            max_physical_address = end;
        }
    }
    
    total_page_frames = phys_to_pfn(max_physical_address);
    
    pr_info("  Total Memory: %llu MB\n", total_memory / MB(1));
    pr_info("  Max Physical Address: 0x%llx\n", max_physical_address);
    pr_info("  Total Page Frames: %llu\n", total_page_frames);
    
    /* Update Zone Boundaries */
    zones[ZONE_NORMAL].end = max_physical_address;
}

/* Full Initialization */
void pmm_init(void)
{
    pr_info("PMM Init: Setting up physical memory manager...\n");
    
    /* Allocate Page Frame Database */
    size_t pfdb_size = total_page_frames * sizeof(page_frame_t);
    pfdb_size = ALIGN(pfdb_size, PAGE_SIZE);
    
    /* Find suitable location for PFDB */
    /* For now, place it after kernel */
    extern char _kernel_end[];
    phys_addr_t pfdb_phys = ALIGN((phys_addr_t)_kernel_end - KERNEL_VIRTUAL_BASE + 
                                   KERNEL_PHYSICAL_BASE, PAGE_SIZE);
    
    page_frames = (page_frame_t *)(pfdb_phys + KERNEL_VIRTUAL_BASE - KERNEL_PHYSICAL_BASE);
    
    pr_info("  Page Frame Database: 0x%llx (%llu KB)\n", pfdb_phys, pfdb_size / 1024);
    
    /* Initialize Page Frames */
    memset(page_frames, 0, pfdb_size);
    
    for (u64 i = 0; i < total_page_frames; i++) {
        INIT_LIST_HEAD(&page_frames[i].list);
        page_frames[i].flags = PG_RESERVED;
        atomic_set(&page_frames[i].refcount, 0);
    }
    
    /* Initialize Zones */
    for (int z = 0; z < NUM_ZONES; z++) {
        spin_lock_init(&zones[z].lock);
        zones[z].total_pages = 0;
        zones[z].free_pages = 0;
        zones[z].reserved_pages = 0;
        
        for (int o = 0; o < MAX_ORDER; o++) {
            INIT_LIST_HEAD(&zones[z].free_area[o].free_list);
            zones[z].free_area[o].free_count = 0;
        }
    }
    
    /* Mark Usable Memory */
    extern struct boot_params boot_params;
    
    for (u32 i = 0; i < boot_params.memory_map_entries; i++) {
        struct memory_map_entry *entry = &boot_params.memory_map[i];
        
        if (entry->type != 1) continue;  /* Not usable */
        
        phys_addr_t start = ALIGN(entry->base, PAGE_SIZE);
        phys_addr_t end = ALIGN_DOWN(entry->base + entry->length, PAGE_SIZE);
        
        /* Skip low memory and kernel area */
        if (start < MB(2)) start = MB(2);
        if (start < pfdb_phys + pfdb_size) start = pfdb_phys + pfdb_size;
        
        /* Add pages to buddy allocator */
        for (phys_addr_t addr = start; addr < end; addr += PAGE_SIZE) {
            page_frame_t *page = phys_to_page(addr);
            memory_zone_t *zone = get_zone_for_addr(addr);
            
            page->flags = 0;
            zone->total_pages++;
            
            /* Add as single pages initially */
            buddy_add_to_free_list(zone, page, 0);
            free_memory += PAGE_SIZE;
        }
    }
    
    pr_info("  Free Memory: %llu MB\n", free_memory / MB(1));
    
    /* Coalesce Free Pages */
    for (int z = 0; z < NUM_ZONES; z++) {
        pr_info("  Zone %s: %llu pages free\n", 
                zones[z].name, zones[z].free_pages);
    }
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                          PUBLIC API                                       */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Allocate Physical Pages */
phys_addr_t pmm_alloc_pages(u32 order, u32 flags)
{
    phys_addr_t addr = 0;
    zone_type_t preferred_zone = ZONE_NORMAL;
    
    /* Select Zone Based on Flags */
    if (flags & PMM_FLAG_DMA) {
        preferred_zone = ZONE_DMA;
    } else if (flags & PMM_FLAG_DMA32) {
        preferred_zone = ZONE_DMA32;
    }
    
    spin_lock(&pmm_lock);
    
    /* Try Preferred Zone First */
    for (zone_type_t z = preferred_zone; z < NUM_ZONES; z++) {
        addr = buddy_alloc_pages(&zones[z], order);
        if (addr) break;
    }
    
    /* Fallback to Lower Zones */
    if (!addr && preferred_zone > 0) {
        for (int z = preferred_zone - 1; z >= 0; z--) {
            addr = buddy_alloc_pages(&zones[z], order);
            if (addr) break;
        }
    }
    
    spin_unlock(&pmm_lock);
    
    /* Zero Memory if Requested */
    if (addr && (flags & PMM_FLAG_ZERO)) {
        void *vaddr = (void *)(addr + KERNEL_VIRTUAL_BASE - KERNEL_PHYSICAL_BASE);
        memset(vaddr, 0, PAGE_SIZE << order);
    }
    
    return addr;
}

/* Allocate Single Page */
phys_addr_t pmm_alloc_page(u32 flags)
{
    return pmm_alloc_pages(0, flags);
}

/* Free Physical Pages */
void pmm_free_pages(phys_addr_t addr, u32 order)
{
    if (!addr || addr >= max_physical_address) {
        return;
    }
    
    page_frame_t *page = phys_to_page(addr);
    
    if (!atomic_dec_and_test(&page->refcount)) {
        return;  /* Still referenced */
    }
    
    memory_zone_t *zone = get_zone_for_addr(addr);
    
    spin_lock(&pmm_lock);
    buddy_free_pages(zone, addr, order);
    free_memory += PAGE_SIZE << order;
    spin_unlock(&pmm_lock);
}

/* Free Single Page */
void pmm_free_page(phys_addr_t addr)
{
    pmm_free_pages(addr, 0);
}

/* Get Page Reference */
void pmm_get_page(phys_addr_t addr)
{
    page_frame_t *page = phys_to_page(addr);
    if (page) {
        atomic_inc(&page->refcount);
    }
}

/* Get Memory Statistics */
void pmm_get_stats(pmm_stats_t *stats)
{
    spin_lock(&pmm_lock);
    
    stats->total_memory = total_memory;
    stats->free_memory = free_memory;
    stats->used_memory = total_memory - free_memory;
    
    for (int z = 0; z < NUM_ZONES; z++) {
        stats->zone_free[z] = zones[z].free_pages * PAGE_SIZE;
        stats->zone_total[z] = zones[z].total_pages * PAGE_SIZE;
    }
    
    spin_unlock(&pmm_lock);
}
```

## 5.2 Virtual Memory Manager (kernel/mm/vmm.c)

```c
/*
 * NEXUS OS - Virtual Memory Manager
 * kernel/mm/vmm.c
 */

#include <kernel.h>
#include <mm/mm.h>
#include <mm/vmm.h>
#include <mm/pmm.h>

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                     VIRTUAL MEMORY STRUCTURES                             */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Virtual Memory Area (VMA) */
typedef struct vma {
    struct list_head list;
    struct rb_node rb_node;
    
    virt_addr_t start;
    virt_addr_t end;
    
    u64 flags;
    u64 prot;
    
    /* Backing */
    struct {
        struct file *file;
        off_t offset;
    } backing;
    
    /* Reference */
    struct mm_struct *mm;
} vma_t;

/* Memory Map Structure */
typedef struct mm_struct {
    /* Page Table */
    phys_addr_t pgd;
    
    /* VMA Management */
    struct list_head vma_list;
    struct rb_root vma_tree;
    u32 vma_count;
    
    /* Memory Regions */
    virt_addr_t start_code, end_code;
    virt_addr_t start_data, end_data;
    virt_addr_t start_brk, brk;
    virt_addr_t start_stack;
    virt_addr_t arg_start, arg_end;
    virt_addr_t env_start, env_end;
    
    /* Limits */
    virt_addr_t mmap_base;
    size_t total_vm;
    size_t locked_vm;
    size_t pinned_vm;
    
    /* Statistics */
    atomic_t page_faults;
    atomic_t minor_faults;
    atomic_t major_faults;
    
    /* Lock */
    rwlock_t lock;
    
    /* Reference Count */
    atomic_t refcount;
    
} mm_struct_t;

/* VMA Flags */
#define VMA_READ        BIT(0)
#define VMA_WRITE       BIT(1)
#define VMA_EXEC        BIT(2)
#define VMA_SHARED      BIT(3)
#define VMA_PRIVATE     BIT(4)
#define VMA_GROWSDOWN   BIT(5)
#define VMA_GROWSUP     BIT(6)
#define VMA_LOCKED      BIT(7)
#define VMA_DONTCOPY    BIT(8)
#define VMA_DONTEXPAND  BIT(9)
#define VMA_STACK       BIT(10)
#define VMA_HEAP        BIT(11)

/* Page Table Levels (x86_64) */
#define PML4_SHIFT      39
#define PDPT_SHIFT      30
#define PD_SHIFT        21
#define PT_SHIFT        12

#define PML4_INDEX(addr)    (((addr) >> PML4_SHIFT) & 0x1FF)
#define PDPT_INDEX(addr)    (((addr) >> PDPT_SHIFT) & 0x1FF)
#define PD_INDEX(addr)      (((addr) >> PD_SHIFT) & 0x1FF)
#define PT_INDEX(addr)      (((addr) >> PT_SHIFT) & 0x1FF)

/* Page Table Entry */
typedef u64 pte_t;

/* Kernel Page Table */
static phys_addr_t kernel_pgd = 0;

/* VMM Lock */
static spinlock_t vmm_lock = {0};

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                       PAGE TABLE OPERATIONS                               */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Get Page Table Entry Pointer */
static pte_t *get_pte(phys_addr_t pgd, virt_addr_t vaddr, bool create)
{
    /* PML4 */
    pte_t *pml4 = (pte_t *)phys_to_virt(pgd);
    u32 pml4_idx = PML4_INDEX(vaddr);
    
    if (!(pml4[pml4_idx] & PTE_PRESENT)) {
        if (!create) return NULL;
        
        phys_addr_t new_page = pmm_alloc_page(PMM_FLAG_ZERO);
        if (!new_page) return NULL;
        
        pml4[pml4_idx] = new_page | PTE_PRESENT | PTE_WRITABLE | PTE_USER;
    }
    
    /* PDPT */
    pte_t *pdpt = (pte_t *)phys_to_virt(pml4[pml4_idx] & ~0xFFF);
    u32 pdpt_idx = PDPT_INDEX(vaddr);
    
    if (!(pdpt[pdpt_idx] & PTE_PRESENT)) {
        if (!create) return NULL;
        
        phys_addr_t new_page = pmm_alloc_page(PMM_FLAG_ZERO);
        if (!new_page) return NULL;
        
        pdpt[pdpt_idx] = new_page | PTE_PRESENT | PTE_WRITABLE | PTE_USER;
    }
    
    /* Check for 1GB Page */
    if (pdpt[pdpt_idx] & PTE_HUGE) {
        return &pdpt[pdpt_idx];
    }
    
    /* PD */
    pte_t *pd = (pte_t *)phys_to_virt(pdpt[pdpt_idx] & ~0xFFF);
    u32 pd_idx = PD_INDEX(vaddr);
    
    if (!(pd[pd_idx] & PTE_PRESENT)) {
        if (!create) return NULL;
        
        phys_addr_t new_page = pmm_alloc_page(PMM_FLAG_ZERO);
        if (!new_page) return NULL;
