        pd[pd_idx] = new_page | PTE_PRESENT | PTE_WRITABLE | PTE_USER;
    }
    
    /* Check for 2MB Page */
    if (pd[pd_idx] & PTE_HUGE) {
        return &pd[pd_idx];
    }
    
    /* PT */
    pte_t *pt = (pte_t *)phys_to_virt(pd[pd_idx] & ~0xFFF);
    u32 pt_idx = PT_INDEX(vaddr);
    
    return &pt[pt_idx];
}

/* Map Page */
int vmm_map_page(phys_addr_t pgd, virt_addr_t vaddr, phys_addr_t paddr, u64 flags)
{
    pte_t *pte = get_pte(pgd, vaddr, true);
    if (!pte) {
        return NEXUS_ENOMEM;
    }
    
    /* Build PTE */
    u64 entry = paddr & ~0xFFF;
    entry |= PTE_PRESENT;
    
    if (flags & VMA_WRITE) entry |= PTE_WRITABLE;
    if (flags & VMA_USER) entry |= PTE_USER;
    if (!(flags & VMA_EXEC)) entry |= PTE_NX;
    
    *pte = entry;
    
    /* Flush TLB */
    hal.cpu->flush_tlb_page(vaddr);
    
    return NEXUS_OK;
}

/* Unmap Page */
int vmm_unmap_page(phys_addr_t pgd, virt_addr_t vaddr)
{
    pte_t *pte = get_pte(pgd, vaddr, false);
    if (!pte) {
        return NEXUS_ENOENT;
    }
    
    /* Get Physical Address */
    phys_addr_t paddr = *pte & ~0xFFF;
    
    /* Clear Entry */
    *pte = 0;
    
    /* Flush TLB */
    hal.cpu->flush_tlb_page(vaddr);
    
    /* Free Physical Page if not shared */
    pmm_free_page(paddr);
    
    return NEXUS_OK;
}

/* Translate Virtual to Physical */
phys_addr_t vmm_translate(phys_addr_t pgd, virt_addr_t vaddr)
{
    pte_t *pte = get_pte(pgd, vaddr, false);
    if (!pte || !(*pte & PTE_PRESENT)) {
        return 0;
    }
    
    return (*pte & ~0xFFF) | (vaddr & 0xFFF);
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                         VMA OPERATIONS                                    */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Create VMA */
static vma_t *vma_create(virt_addr_t start, virt_addr_t end, u64 flags)
{
    vma_t *vma = kmalloc(sizeof(vma_t));
    if (!vma) return NULL;
    
    memset(vma, 0, sizeof(vma_t));
    INIT_LIST_HEAD(&vma->list);
    
    vma->start = start;
    vma->end = end;
    vma->flags = flags;
    
    return vma;
}

/* Find VMA for Address */
vma_t *vmm_find_vma(mm_struct_t *mm, virt_addr_t addr)
{
    struct rb_node *node = mm->vma_tree.rb_node;
    
    while (node) {
        vma_t *vma = container_of(node, vma_t, rb_node);
        
        if (addr < vma->start) {
            node = node->rb_left;
        } else if (addr >= vma->end) {
            node = node->rb_right;
        } else {
            return vma;
        }
    }
    
    return NULL;
}

/* Insert VMA */
static int vma_insert(mm_struct_t *mm, vma_t *vma)
{
    struct rb_node **link = &mm->vma_tree.rb_node;
    struct rb_node *parent = NULL;
    
    while (*link) {
        parent = *link;
        vma_t *entry = container_of(parent, vma_t, rb_node);
        
        if (vma->end <= entry->start) {
            link = &parent->rb_left;
        } else if (vma->start >= entry->end) {
            link = &parent->rb_right;
        } else {
            /* Overlap */
            return NEXUS_EEXIST;
        }
    }
    
    /* Add to RB-Tree */
    rb_link_node(&vma->rb_node, parent, link);
    rb_insert_color(&vma->rb_node, &mm->vma_tree);
    
    /* Add to List */
    list_add_tail(&vma->list, &mm->vma_list);
    mm->vma_count++;
    
    vma->mm = mm;
    
    return NEXUS_OK;
}

/* Memory Map (mmap) */
virt_addr_t vmm_mmap(mm_struct_t *mm, virt_addr_t addr, size_t length,
                     u64 prot, u64 flags, struct file *file, off_t offset)
{
    length = ALIGN(length, PAGE_SIZE);
    
    /* Find Free Region if No Address Specified */
    if (addr == 0) {
        addr = mm->mmap_base;
        
        /* Simple linear search for gap */
        vma_t *vma;
        list_for_each_entry(vma, &mm->vma_list, list) {
            if (addr + length <= vma->start) {
                break;
            }
            addr = ALIGN(vma->end, PAGE_SIZE);
        }
    } else {
        addr = ALIGN_DOWN(addr, PAGE_SIZE);
    }
    
    /* Check for Overlap */
    vma_t *existing = vmm_find_vma(mm, addr);
    if (existing && existing->start < addr + length) {
        return (virt_addr_t)-1;
    }
    
    /* Create VMA */
    vma_t *new_vma = vma_create(addr, addr + length, flags);
    if (!new_vma) {
        return (virt_addr_t)-1;
    }
    
    new_vma->prot = prot;
    
    if (file) {
        new_vma->backing.file = file;
        new_vma->backing.offset = offset;
    }
    
    /* Insert VMA */
    if (vma_insert(mm, new_vma) != NEXUS_OK) {
        kfree(new_vma);
        return (virt_addr_t)-1;
    }
    
    /* Pre-map if Anonymous Private */
    if ((flags & VMA_PRIVATE) && !file) {
        for (virt_addr_t va = addr; va < addr + length; va += PAGE_SIZE) {
            phys_addr_t pa = pmm_alloc_page(PMM_FLAG_ZERO);
            if (pa) {
                vmm_map_page(mm->pgd, va, pa, flags | VMA_USER);
            }
        }
    }
    
    mm->total_vm += length;
    
    return addr;
}

/* Memory Unmap (munmap) */
int vmm_munmap(mm_struct_t *mm, virt_addr_t addr, size_t length)
{
    length = ALIGN(length, PAGE_SIZE);
    
    vma_t *vma = vmm_find_vma(mm, addr);
    if (!vma) {
        return NEXUS_ENOENT;
    }
    
    /* Unmap Pages */
    for (virt_addr_t va = addr; va < addr + length; va += PAGE_SIZE) {
        vmm_unmap_page(mm->pgd, va);
    }
    
    /* Remove VMA */
    list_del(&vma->list);
    rb_erase(&vma->rb_node, &mm->vma_tree);
    mm->vma_count--;
    mm->total_vm -= length;
    
    kfree(vma);
    
    return NEXUS_OK;
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                        PAGE FAULT HANDLER                                 */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Page Fault Handler */
int vmm_handle_page_fault(virt_addr_t fault_addr, u64 error_code)
{
    mm_struct_t *mm = current_process()->mm;
    
    atomic_inc(&mm->page_faults);
    
    /* Find VMA */
    vma_t *vma = vmm_find_vma(mm, fault_addr);
    
    if (!vma) {
        /* No VMA - Segmentation Fault */
        pr_debug("Page fault: No VMA for 0x%llx\n", fault_addr);
        return NEXUS_EACCES;
    }
    
    /* Check Permissions */
    if ((error_code & 2) && !(vma->flags & VMA_WRITE)) {
        /* Write to read-only */
        pr_debug("Page fault: Write to read-only 0x%llx\n", fault_addr);
        return NEXUS_EACCES;
    }
    
    if ((error_code & 16) && !(vma->flags & VMA_EXEC)) {
        /* Execute non-executable */
        pr_debug("Page fault: Execute non-exec 0x%llx\n", fault_addr);
        return NEXUS_EACCES;
    }
    
    /* Handle Fault */
    phys_addr_t paddr;
    
    if (vma->backing.file) {
        /* File-Backed - Load from File */
        /* TODO: Implement file mapping */
        paddr = pmm_alloc_page(PMM_FLAG_ZERO);
        atomic_inc(&mm->major_faults);
    } else {
        /* Anonymous - Allocate New Page */
        paddr = pmm_alloc_page(PMM_FLAG_ZERO);
        atomic_inc(&mm->minor_faults);
    }
    
    if (!paddr) {
        pr_err("Page fault: Out of memory\n");
        return NEXUS_ENOMEM;
    }
    
    /* Map Page */
    virt_addr_t page_addr = ALIGN_DOWN(fault_addr, PAGE_SIZE);
    vmm_map_page(mm->pgd, page_addr, paddr, vma->flags | VMA_USER);
    
    return NEXUS_OK;
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                     MM STRUCT OPERATIONS                                  */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Create Memory Map */
mm_struct_t *vmm_create_mm(void)
{
    mm_struct_t *mm = kzalloc(sizeof(mm_struct_t));
    if (!mm) return NULL;
    
    /* Create Page Table */
    mm->pgd = pmm_alloc_page(PMM_FLAG_ZERO);
    if (!mm->pgd) {
        kfree(mm);
        return NULL;
    }
    
    /* Copy Kernel Mappings */
    pte_t *new_pml4 = (pte_t *)phys_to_virt(mm->pgd);
    pte_t *kern_pml4 = (pte_t *)phys_to_virt(kernel_pgd);
    
    for (int i = 256; i < 512; i++) {
        new_pml4[i] = kern_pml4[i];
    }
    
    /* Initialize VMA List */
    INIT_LIST_HEAD(&mm->vma_list);
    mm->vma_tree.rb_node = NULL;
    
    /* Set Defaults */
    mm->mmap_base = 0x00007F0000000000ULL;
    
    rwlock_init(&mm->lock);
    atomic_set(&mm->refcount, 1);
    
    return mm;
}

/* Destroy Memory Map */
void vmm_destroy_mm(mm_struct_t *mm)
{
    if (!atomic_dec_and_test(&mm->refcount)) {
        return;
    }
    
    /* Free All VMAs */
    vma_t *vma, *tmp;
    list_for_each_entry_safe(vma, tmp, &mm->vma_list, list) {
        for (virt_addr_t va = vma->start; va < vma->end; va += PAGE_SIZE) {
            vmm_unmap_page(mm->pgd, va);
        }
        list_del(&vma->list);
        kfree(vma);
    }
    
    /* Free Page Tables */
    /* TODO: Recursively free page table pages */
    
    pmm_free_page(mm->pgd);
    kfree(mm);
}

/* Clone Memory Map (for fork) */
mm_struct_t *vmm_clone_mm(mm_struct_t *src)
{
    mm_struct_t *dst = vmm_create_mm();
    if (!dst) return NULL;
    
    read_lock(&src->lock);
    
    /* Clone VMAs */
    vma_t *src_vma;
    list_for_each_entry(src_vma, &src->vma_list, list) {
        vma_t *dst_vma = vma_create(src_vma->start, src_vma->end, src_vma->flags);
        if (!dst_vma) {
            read_unlock(&src->lock);
            vmm_destroy_mm(dst);
            return NULL;
        }
        
        dst_vma->prot = src_vma->prot;
        dst_vma->backing = src_vma->backing;
        
        vma_insert(dst, dst_vma);
        
        /* Copy Pages (COW optimization possible) */
        for (virt_addr_t va = src_vma->start; va < src_vma->end; va += PAGE_SIZE) {
            phys_addr_t src_pa = vmm_translate(src->pgd, va);
            if (src_pa) {
                phys_addr_t dst_pa = pmm_alloc_page(0);
                if (dst_pa) {
                    memcpy(phys_to_virt(dst_pa), phys_to_virt(src_pa), PAGE_SIZE);
                    vmm_map_page(dst->pgd, va, dst_pa, src_vma->flags | VMA_USER);
                }
            }
        }
    }
    
    /* Copy Other Fields */
    dst->start_code = src->start_code;
    dst->end_code = src->end_code;
    dst->start_data = src->start_data;
    dst->end_data = src->end_data;
    dst->start_brk = src->start_brk;
    dst->brk = src->brk;
    dst->start_stack = src->start_stack;
    dst->total_vm = src->total_vm;
    
    read_unlock(&src->lock);
    
    return dst;
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                       VMM INITIALIZATION                                  */
/*===========================================================================*/

void vmm_init(void)
{
    pr_info("VMM Init: Setting up virtual memory manager...\n");
    
    /* Get Current Page Table (Set up by bootloader) */
    kernel_pgd = hal.memory->get_current_page_table();
    
    pr_info("  Kernel PGD: 0x%llx\n", kernel_pgd);
    
    /* Map Kernel Region */
    pr_info("  Kernel mapped at: 0x%llx\n", KERNEL_VIRTUAL_BASE);
    
    pr_info("VMM initialization complete.\n");
}

/* Switch Address Space */
void vmm_switch(mm_struct_t *mm)
{
    if (mm) {
        hal.memory->load_page_table(mm->pgd);
    } else {
        hal.memory->load_page_table(kernel_pgd);
    }}

# NEXUS OS - Continued Implementation

## 6.1 Process Structures (kernel/sched/process.h) - Continued

```c
/*
 * NEXUS OS - Process and Thread Definitions
 * kernel/sched/process.h
 */

#ifndef _NEXUS_PROCESS_H
#define _NEXUS_PROCESS_H

#include <kernel.h>
#include <mm/vmm.h>

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                          PROCESS STATES                                   */
/*===========================================================================*/

typedef enum {
    PROCESS_STATE_NEW,
    PROCESS_STATE_READY,
    PROCESS_STATE_RUNNING,
    PROCESS_STATE_BLOCKED,
    PROCESS_STATE_SUSPENDED,
    PROCESS_STATE_ZOMBIE,
    PROCESS_STATE_DEAD,
} process_state_t;

typedef enum {
    THREAD_STATE_NEW,
    THREAD_STATE_READY,
    THREAD_STATE_RUNNING,
    THREAD_STATE_BLOCKED,
    THREAD_STATE_SLEEPING,
    THREAD_STATE_DEAD,
} thread_state_t;

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                         CPU CONTEXT                                       */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Architecture-Specific CPU Context (x86_64) */
typedef struct cpu_context {
    /* General Purpose Registers */
    u64 rax, rbx, rcx, rdx;
    u64 rsi, rdi, rbp, rsp;
    u64 r8, r9, r10, r11;
    u64 r12, r13, r14, r15;
    
    /* Instruction Pointer */
    u64 rip;
    
    /* Flags */
    u64 rflags;
    
    /* Segment Selectors */
    u64 cs, ss, ds, es, fs, gs;
    
    /* Control Registers */
    u64 cr3;
    
    /* FPU/SSE/AVX State (512+ bytes, 64-byte aligned) */
    u8 fpu_state[1024] __aligned(64);
    
} cpu_context_t;

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                        THREAD STRUCTURE                                   */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Thread Flags */
#define THREAD_FLAG_KERNEL      BIT(0)
#define THREAD_FLAG_IDLE        BIT(1)
#define THREAD_FLAG_NEED_RESCHED BIT(2)
#define THREAD_FLAG_SIGNALED    BIT(3)
#define THREAD_FLAG_INTERRUPTED BIT(4)

/* Thread Structure */
typedef struct thread {
    /* Thread ID */
    tid_t tid;
    char name[64];
    
    /* State */
    thread_state_t state;
    u32 flags;
    
    /* CPU Context */
    cpu_context_t context;
    
    /* Stack */
    void *kernel_stack;
    void *user_stack;
    size_t kernel_stack_size;
    size_t user_stack_size;
    
    /* Scheduling */
    s32 priority;
    s32 static_priority;
    s32 dynamic_priority;
    u64 time_slice;
    u64 remaining_time;
    u64 total_runtime;
    u64 last_scheduled;
    u32 cpu_affinity;
    u32 current_cpu;
    
    /* CFS Scheduling */
    u64 vruntime;
    struct rb_node sched_node;
    
    /* Wait Queue */
    wait_queue_entry_t wait_entry;
    void *wait_channel;
    int wait_result;
    
    /* Signals */
    u64 pending_signals;
    u64 blocked_signals;
    struct sigaction signal_handlers[64];
    
    /* Linked Lists */
    struct list_head thread_list;   /* All threads in process */
    struct list_head ready_list;    /* Ready queue */
    struct list_head global_list;   /* Global thread list */
    
    /* Parent Process */
    struct process *process;
    
    /* Thread Local Storage */
    void *tls_base;
    size_t tls_size;
    
    /* Exit */
    int exit_code;
    
    /* Statistics */
    u64 context_switches;
    u64 voluntary_switches;
    u64 involuntary_switches;
    u64 page_faults;
    
    /* Lock */
    spinlock_t lock;
    
} thread_t;

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                       PROCESS STRUCTURE                                   */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Process Flags */
#define PROC_FLAG_KERNEL        BIT(0)
#define PROC_FLAG_INIT          BIT(1)
#define PROC_FLAG_DAEMON        BIT(2)
#define PROC_FLAG_TRACED        BIT(3)
#define PROC_FLAG_EXECVE        BIT(4)
#define PROC_FLAG_EXITING       BIT(5)

/* File Descriptor Entry */
typedef struct fd_entry {
    struct file *file;
    u32 flags;
    u32 close_on_exec;
} fd_entry_t;

/* File Descriptor Table */
typedef struct fd_table {
    fd_entry_t *entries;
    u32 max_fds;
    u32 next_fd;
    spinlock_t lock;
    atomic_t refcount;
} fd_table_t;

/* Process Credentials */
typedef struct credentials {
    uid_t uid, euid, suid;
    gid_t gid, egid, sgid;
    u32 num_groups;
    gid_t groups[32];
    u64 capabilities;
    atomic_t refcount;
} credentials_t;

/* Resource Limits */
typedef struct rlimits {
    struct {
        u64 soft;
        u64 hard;
    } limits[16];
} rlimits_t;

/* Resource Limit Types */
#define RLIMIT_CPU          0
#define RLIMIT_FSIZE        1
#define RLIMIT_DATA         2
#define RLIMIT_STACK        3
#define RLIMIT_CORE         4
#define RLIMIT_RSS          5
#define RLIMIT_NPROC        6
#define RLIMIT_NOFILE       7
#define RLIMIT_MEMLOCK      8
#define RLIMIT_AS           9
#define RLIMIT_LOCKS        10

/* Process Structure */
typedef struct process {
    /* Process ID */
    pid_t pid;
    char name[256];
    char cmdline[1024];
    
    /* State */
    process_state_t state;
    u32 flags;
    
    /* Memory */
    mm_struct_t *mm;
    
    /* Threads */
    struct list_head thread_list;
    u32 thread_count;
    thread_t *main_thread;
    
    /* Process Tree */
    struct process *parent;
    struct list_head children;
    struct list_head sibling;
    
    /* Credentials */
    credentials_t *cred;
    
    /* File System */
    fd_table_t *fd_table;
    struct vfs_node *root;
    struct vfs_node *cwd;
    mode_t umask;
    
    /* Signals */
    spinlock_t sighand_lock;
    u64 pending_signals;
    struct list_head signal_queue;
    
    /* Resource Limits */
    rlimits_t *rlimits;
    
    /* Namespaces (for containers) */
    struct {
        struct pid_namespace *pid_ns;
        struct mount_namespace *mnt_ns;
        struct net_namespace *net_ns;
        struct user_namespace *user_ns;
        struct ipc_namespace *ipc_ns;
    } namespaces;
    
    /* CGroups */
    struct cgroup *cgroup;
    
    /* Exit */
    int exit_code;
    int exit_signal;
    
    /* Timing */
    u64 start_time;
    u64 user_time;
    u64 system_time;
    u64 children_user_time;
    u64 children_system_time;
    
    /* Statistics */
    u64 total_forks;
    u64 total_execs;
    
    /* Wait Queue */
    wait_queue_t wait_queue;
    
    /* Global List */
    struct list_head global_list;
    struct rb_node pid_node;
    
    /* Lock */
    spinlock_t lock;
    rwlock_t mm_lock;
    
    /* Reference Count */
    atomic_t refcount;
    
} process_t;

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                        FUNCTION DECLARATIONS                              */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Process Management */
int process_init(void);
process_t *process_create(const char *name, u32 flags);
process_t *process_fork(process_t *parent);
int process_exec(process_t *proc, const char *path, char *const argv[], char *const envp[]);
void process_exit(process_t *proc, int exit_code);
void process_kill(process_t *proc, int signal);
process_t *process_get_by_pid(pid_t pid);
void process_put(process_t *proc);

/* Thread Management */
thread_t *thread_create(process_t *proc, const char *name, 
                        void (*entry)(void*), void *arg, u32 flags);
thread_t *thread_create_kernel(const char *name, void (*entry)(void*), void *arg);
void thread_exit(thread_t *thread, int exit_code);
void thread_sleep(u64 milliseconds);
void thread_yield(void);
void thread_block(wait_queue_t *wq);
void thread_unblock(thread_t *thread);
thread_t *thread_get_by_tid(tid_t tid);

/* Wait Functions */
pid_t wait_pid(pid_t pid, int *status, int options);
int wait_for_thread(thread_t *thread);

/* Context Switching */
void switch_to(thread_t *prev, thread_t *next);
void context_switch(thread_t *prev, thread_t *next);

/* Current Thread/Process Access */
#define current         (this_cpu()->current_thread)
#define current_proc    (current->process)

#endif /* _NEXUS_PROCESS_H */
```

## 6.2 Process Implementation (kernel/sched/process.c)

```c
/*
 * NEXUS OS - Process Management
 * kernel/sched/process.c
 */

#include <kernel.h>
#include <sched/process.h>
#include <sched/scheduler.h>
#include <mm/mm.h>
#include <fs/vfs.h>

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                          GLOBAL DATA                                      */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Process Table */
static struct {
    struct rb_root pid_tree;
    struct list_head process_list;
    spinlock_t lock;
    pid_t next_pid;
    u64 total_processes;
} process_table = {
    .pid_tree = { NULL },
    .process_list = LIST_HEAD_INIT(process_table.process_list),
    .next_pid = 1,
    .total_processes = 0,
};

/* Thread Table */
static struct {
    struct list_head thread_list;
    spinlock_t lock;
    tid_t next_tid;
    u64 total_threads;
} thread_table = {
    .thread_list = LIST_HEAD_INIT(thread_table.thread_list),
    .next_tid = 1,
    .total_threads = 0,
};

/* Init Process */
static process_t *init_process = NULL;

/* Kernel Process */
static process_t *kernel_process = NULL;

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                       PID ALLOCATION                                      */
/*===========================================================================*/

static pid_t allocate_pid(void)
{
    spin_lock(&process_table.lock);
    pid_t pid = process_table.next_pid++;
    if (process_table.next_pid >= MAX_PROCESSES) {
        process_table.next_pid = 1;  /* Wrap around */
    }
    spin_unlock(&process_table.lock);
    return pid;
}

static tid_t allocate_tid(void)
{
    spin_lock(&thread_table.lock);
    tid_t tid = thread_table.next_tid++;
    spin_unlock(&thread_table.lock);
    return tid;
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                    FILE DESCRIPTOR TABLE                                  */
/*===========================================================================*/

static fd_table_t *fd_table_create(void)
{
    fd_table_t *fdt = kzalloc(sizeof(fd_table_t));
    if (!fdt) return NULL;
    
    fdt->max_fds = 256;  /* Initial size */
    fdt->entries = kzalloc(sizeof(fd_entry_t) * fdt->max_fds);
    if (!fdt->entries) {
        kfree(fdt);
        return NULL;
    }
    
    spin_lock_init(&fdt->lock);
    atomic_set(&fdt->refcount, 1);
    fdt->next_fd = 0;
    
    return fdt;
}

static fd_table_t *fd_table_clone(fd_table_t *src)
{
    fd_table_t *dst = fd_table_create();
    if (!dst) return NULL;
    
    spin_lock(&src->lock);
    
    for (u32 i = 0; i < src->max_fds && i < dst->max_fds; i++) {
        if (src->entries[i].file) {
            dst->entries[i] = src->entries[i];
            vfs_file_get(src->entries[i].file);
        }
    }
    dst->next_fd = src->next_fd;
    
    spin_unlock(&src->lock);
    
    return dst;
}

static void fd_table_destroy(fd_table_t *fdt)
{
    if (!atomic_dec_and_test(&fdt->refcount)) {
        return;
    }
    
    for (u32 i = 0; i < fdt->max_fds; i++) {
        if (fdt->entries[i].file) {
            vfs_close(fdt->entries[i].file);
        }
    }
    
    kfree(fdt->entries);
    kfree(fdt);
}

int fd_alloc(process_t *proc, struct file *file)
{
    fd_table_t *fdt = proc->fd_table;
    
    spin_lock(&fdt->lock);
    
    /* Find free slot */
    for (u32 i = fdt->next_fd; i < fdt->max_fds; i++) {
        if (fdt->entries[i].file == NULL) {
            fdt->entries[i].file = file;
            fdt->entries[i].flags = 0;
            fdt->next_fd = i + 1;
            spin_unlock(&fdt->lock);
            return i;
        }
    }
    
    /* Try from beginning */
    for (u32 i = 0; i < fdt->next_fd; i++) {
        if (fdt->entries[i].file == NULL) {
            fdt->entries[i].file = file;
            fdt->entries[i].flags = 0;
            fdt->next_fd = i + 1;
            spin_unlock(&fdt->lock);
            return i;
        }
    }
    
    spin_unlock(&fdt->lock);
    return -1;  /* No free slot */
}

struct file *fd_get(process_t *proc, int fd)
{
    fd_table_t *fdt = proc->fd_table;
    
    if (fd < 0 || fd >= (int)fdt->max_fds) {
        return NULL;
    }
    
    return fdt->entries[fd].file;
}

int fd_close(process_t *proc, int fd)
{
    fd_table_t *fdt = proc->fd_table;
    
    if (fd < 0 || fd >= (int)fdt->max_fds) {
        return NEXUS_EINVAL;
    }
    
    spin_lock(&fdt->lock);
    
    if (fdt->entries[fd].file == NULL) {
        spin_unlock(&fdt->lock);
        return NEXUS_ENOENT;
    }
    
    vfs_close(fdt->entries[fd].file);
    fdt->entries[fd].file = NULL;
    fdt->entries[fd].flags = 0;
    
    if ((u32)fd < fdt->next_fd) {
        fdt->next_fd = fd;
    }
    
    spin_unlock(&fdt->lock);
    return NEXUS_OK;
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                       CREDENTIALS                                         */
/*===========================================================================*/

static credentials_t *credentials_create(uid_t uid, gid_t gid)
{
    credentials_t *cred = kzalloc(sizeof(credentials_t));
    if (!cred) return NULL;
    
    cred->uid = cred->euid = cred->suid = uid;
    cred->gid = cred->egid = cred->sgid = gid;
    cred->num_groups = 0;
    cred->capabilities = 0;
    atomic_set(&cred->refcount, 1);
    
    return cred;
}

static credentials_t *credentials_clone(credentials_t *src)
{
    credentials_t *dst = kzalloc(sizeof(credentials_t));
    if (!dst) return NULL;
    
    memcpy(dst, src, sizeof(credentials_t));
    atomic_set(&dst->refcount, 1);
    
    return dst;
}

static void credentials_put(credentials_t *cred)
{
    if (atomic_dec_and_test(&cred->refcount)) {
        kfree(cred);
    }
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                       THREAD CREATION                                     */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Allocate Kernel Stack */
static void *alloc_kernel_stack(void)
{
    void *stack = vmalloc(KERNEL_STACK_SIZE);
    if (!stack) return NULL;
    
    /* Guard page at bottom */
    vmm_unmap_page(kernel_pgd, (virt_addr_t)stack);
    
    return stack;
}

/* Free Kernel Stack */
static void free_kernel_stack(void *stack)
{
    /* Remap guard page */
    vfree(stack);
}

/* Thread Entry Wrapper */
static void thread_entry_wrapper(void)
{
    thread_t *thread = current;
    
    /* Enable Interrupts */
    local_irq_enable();
    
    /* Call Actual Entry Point */
    void (*entry)(void*) = (void (*)(void*))thread->context.rdi;
    void *arg = (void*)thread->context.rsi;
    
    entry(arg);
    
    /* Thread Exit */
    thread_exit(thread, 0);
}

/* Create Thread */
thread_t *thread_create(process_t *proc, const char *name,
                        void (*entry)(void*), void *arg, u32 flags)
{
    thread_t *thread = kzalloc(sizeof(thread_t));
    if (!thread) return NULL;
    
    /* Basic Setup */
    thread->tid = allocate_tid();
    strncpy(thread->name, name, sizeof(thread->name) - 1);
    thread->state = THREAD_STATE_NEW;
    thread->flags = flags;
    thread->process = proc;
    
    /* Initialize Lists */
    INIT_LIST_HEAD(&thread->thread_list);
    INIT_LIST_HEAD(&thread->ready_list);
    INIT_LIST_HEAD(&thread->global_list);
    
    /* Allocate Kernel Stack */
    thread->kernel_stack_size = KERNEL_STACK_SIZE;
    thread->kernel_stack = alloc_kernel_stack();
    if (!thread->kernel_stack) {
        kfree(thread);
        return NULL;
    }
    
    /* Initialize Context */
    memset(&thread->context, 0, sizeof(cpu_context_t));
    
    /* Set Stack Pointer (grows down) */
    thread->context.rsp = (u64)thread->kernel_stack + thread->kernel_stack_size - 8;
    
    /* Set Entry Point */
    thread->context.rip = (u64)thread_entry_wrapper;
    thread->context.rdi = (u64)entry;
    thread->context.rsi = (u64)arg;
    
    /* Set Segment Selectors */
    if (flags & THREAD_FLAG_KERNEL) {
        thread->context.cs = KERNEL_CS;
        thread->context.ss = KERNEL_DS;
    } else {
        thread->context.cs = USER_CS;
        thread->context.ss = USER_DS;
    }
    thread->context.rflags = 0x200;  /* IF enabled */
    
    /* Set Page Table */
    thread->context.cr3 = proc->mm ? proc->mm->pgd : kernel_pgd;
    
    /* Scheduling Parameters */
    thread->priority = SCHED_PRIORITY_DEFAULT;
    thread->static_priority = SCHED_PRIORITY_DEFAULT;
    thread->dynamic_priority = SCHED_PRIORITY_DEFAULT;
    thread->time_slice = SCHED_TIME_SLICE_MS;
    thread->remaining_time = SCHED_TIME_SLICE_MS;
    thread->cpu_affinity = 0xFFFFFFFF;  /* All CPUs */
    thread->vruntime = 0;
    
    /* Initialize Lock */
    spin_lock_init(&thread->lock);
    
    /* Add to Process Thread List */
    spin_lock(&proc->lock);
    list_add_tail(&thread->thread_list, &proc->thread_list);
    proc->thread_count++;
    spin_unlock(&proc->lock);
    
    /* Add to Global Thread List */
    spin_lock(&thread_table.lock);
    list_add_tail(&thread->global_list, &thread_table.thread_list);
    thread_table.total_threads++;
    spin_unlock(&thread_table.lock);
    
    pr_debug("Created thread %d '%s' for process %d\n", 
             thread->tid, thread->name, proc->pid);
    
    return thread;
}

/* Create Kernel Thread */
thread_t *thread_create_kernel(const char *name, void (*entry)(void*), void *arg)
{
    return thread_create(kernel_process, name, entry, arg, THREAD_FLAG_KERNEL);
}

/* Thread Exit */
void thread_exit(thread_t *thread, int exit_code)
{
    thread->exit_code = exit_code;
    thread->state = THREAD_STATE_DEAD;
    
    /* If Main Thread, Process Exits */
    if (thread == thread->process->main_thread) {
        process_exit(thread->process, exit_code);
    }
    
    /* Wake Up Waiters */
    wake_up(&thread->process->wait_queue);
    
    /* Schedule Another Thread */
    schedule();
    
    /* Never Reach Here */
    kernel_panic("thread_exit returned!");
}

/* Thread Sleep */
void thread_sleep(u64 milliseconds)
{
    thread_t *thread = current;
    
    thread->state = THREAD_STATE_SLEEPING;
    
    /* Create Timer */
    timer_t timer;
    setup_timer(&timer, (timer_callback_t)thread_unblock, thread);
    start_timer(&timer, milliseconds * 1000000, TIMER_TYPE_ONESHOT);
    
    /* Sleep */
    schedule();
    
    /* Cancel Timer if Still Active */
    stop_timer(&timer);
    
    thread->state = THREAD_STATE_RUNNING;
}

/* Thread Yield */
void thread_yield(void)
{
    current->remaining_time = 0;
    schedule();
}

/* Thread Block */
void thread_block(wait_queue_t *wq)
{
    thread_t *thread = current;
    unsigned long flags;
    
    spin_lock_irqsave(&wq->lock, flags);
    
    thread->state = THREAD_STATE_BLOCKED;
    thread->wait_channel = wq;
    
    /* Add to Wait Queue */
    thread->wait_entry.thread = thread;
    list_add_tail(&thread->wait_entry.list, &wq->head);
    
    spin_unlock_irqrestore(&wq->lock, flags);
    
    schedule();
}

/* Thread Unblock */
void thread_unblock(thread_t *thread)
{
    wait_queue_t *wq = thread->wait_channel;
    unsigned long flags;
    
    if (wq) {
        spin_lock_irqsave(&wq->lock, flags);
        list_del(&thread->wait_entry.list);
        thread->wait_channel = NULL;
        spin_unlock_irqrestore(&wq->lock, flags);
    }
    
    thread->state = THREAD_STATE_READY;
    scheduler_enqueue(thread);
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                       PROCESS CREATION                                    */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Create Process */
process_t *process_create(const char *name, u32 flags)
{
    process_t *proc = kzalloc(sizeof(process_t));
    if (!proc) return NULL;
    
    /* Basic Setup */
    proc->pid = allocate_pid();
    strncpy(proc->name, name, sizeof(proc->name) - 1);
    proc->state = PROCESS_STATE_NEW;
    proc->flags = flags;
    proc->start_time = get_time_ms();
    
    /* Initialize Lists */
    INIT_LIST_HEAD(&proc->thread_list);
    INIT_LIST_HEAD(&proc->children);
    INIT_LIST_HEAD(&proc->sibling);
    INIT_LIST_HEAD(&proc->global_list);
    INIT_LIST_HEAD(&proc->signal_queue);
    
    /* Initialize Wait Queue */
    init_waitqueue_head(&proc->wait_queue);
    
    /* Create Memory Map */
    if (!(flags & PROC_FLAG_KERNEL)) {
        proc->mm = vmm_create_mm();
        if (!proc->mm) {
            kfree(proc);
            return NULL;
        }
    }
    
    /* Create File Descriptor Table */
    proc->fd_table = fd_table_create();
    if (!proc->fd_table) {
        if (proc->mm) vmm_destroy_mm(proc->mm);
        kfree(proc);
        return NULL;
    }
    
    /* Create Credentials */
    proc->cred = credentials_create(0, 0);  /* Root by default */
    if (!proc->cred) {
        fd_table_destroy(proc->fd_table);
        if (proc->mm) vmm_destroy_mm(proc->mm);
        kfree(proc);
        return NULL;
    }
    
    /* Create Resource Limits */
    proc->rlimits = kzalloc(sizeof(rlimits_t));
    if (!proc->rlimits) {
        credentials_put(proc->cred);
        fd_table_destroy(proc->fd_table);
        if (proc->mm) vmm_destroy_mm(proc->mm);
        kfree(proc);
        return NULL;
    }
    
    /* Set Default Resource Limits */
    proc->rlimits->limits[RLIMIT_NOFILE].soft = 1024;
    proc->rlimits->limits[RLIMIT_NOFILE].hard = 65536;
    proc->rlimits->limits[RLIMIT_STACK].soft = 8 * 1024 * 1024;
    proc->rlimits->limits[RLIMIT_STACK].hard = 64 * 1024 * 1024;
    
    /* Initialize Locks */
    spin_lock_init(&proc->lock);
    spin_lock_init(&proc->sighand_lock);
    rwlock_init(&proc->mm_lock);
    
    /* Reference Count */
    atomic_set(&proc->refcount, 1);
    
    /* Set umask */
    proc->umask = 0022;
    
    /* Add to Global Process List */
    spin_lock(&process_table.lock);
    list_add_tail(&proc->global_list, &process_table.process_list);
    /* Add to PID Tree */
    rb_insert_pid(&process_table.pid_tree, proc);
    process_table.total_processes++;
    spin_unlock(&process_table.lock);
    
    pr_debug("Created process %d '%s'\n", proc->pid, proc->name);
    
    return proc;
}

/* Fork Process */
process_t *process_fork(process_t *parent)
{
    process_t *child = kzalloc(sizeof(process_t));
    if (!child) return NULL;
    
    /* Copy from Parent */
    child->pid = allocate_pid();
    strncpy(child->name, parent->name, sizeof(child->name));
    child->state = PROCESS_STATE_NEW;
    child->flags = parent->flags & ~PROC_FLAG_INIT;
    child->parent = parent;
    child->start_time = get_time_ms();
    child->umask = parent->umask;
    
    /* Initialize Lists */
    INIT_LIST_HEAD(&child->thread_list);
    INIT_LIST_HEAD(&child->children);
    INIT_LIST_HEAD(&child->sibling);
    INIT_LIST_HEAD(&child->global_list);
    INIT_LIST_HEAD(&child->signal_queue);
    init_waitqueue_head(&child->wait_queue);
    
    /* Clone Memory Map */
    child->mm = vmm_clone_mm(parent->mm);
    if (!child->mm) {
        kfree(child);
        return NULL;
    }
    
    /* Clone File Descriptor Table */
    child->fd_table = fd_table_clone(parent->fd_table);
    if (!child->fd_table) {
        vmm_destroy_mm(child->mm);
        kfree(child);
        return NULL;
    }
    
    /* Clone Credentials */
    child->cred = credentials_clone(parent->cred);
    if (!child->cred) {
        fd_table_destroy(child->fd_table);
        vmm_destroy_mm(child->mm);
        kfree(child);
        return NULL;
    }
    
    /* Clone Resource Limits */
    child->rlimits = kzalloc(sizeof(rlimits_t));
    memcpy(child->rlimits, parent->rlimits, sizeof(rlimits_t));
    
    /* Copy FS info */
    child->root = parent->root;
    child->cwd = parent->cwd;
    if (child->root) vfs_node_get(child->root);
    if (child->cwd) vfs_node_get(child->cwd);
    
    /* Initialize Locks */
    spin_lock_init(&child->lock);
    spin_lock_init(&child->sighand_lock);
    rwlock_init(&child->mm_lock);
    atomic_set(&child->refcount, 1);
    
    /* Add to Parent's Children List */
    spin_lock(&parent->lock);
    list_add_tail(&child->sibling, &parent->children);
    spin_unlock(&parent->lock);
    
    /* Add to Global Process List */
    spin_lock(&process_table.lock);
    list_add_tail(&child->global_list, &process_table.process_list);
    rb_insert_pid(&process_table.pid_tree, child);
    process_table.total_processes++;
    spin_unlock(&process_table.lock);
    
    /* Clone Main Thread */
    thread_t *parent_thread = parent->main_thread;
    thread_t *child_thread = thread_create(child, parent_thread->name,
                                           NULL, NULL, parent_thread->flags);
    if (!child_thread) {
        process_exit(child, -1);
        return NULL;
    }
    
    /* Copy Thread Context */
    memcpy(&child_thread->context, &parent_thread->context, sizeof(cpu_context_t));
    child_thread->context.rax = 0;  /* Return 0 in child */
    child_thread->context.cr3 = child->mm->pgd;
    
    child->main_thread = child_thread;
    child_thread->state = THREAD_STATE_READY;
    
    /* Make Child Ready */
    child->state = PROCESS_STATE_READY;
    scheduler_enqueue(child_thread);
    
    parent->total_forks++;
    
    pr_debug("Forked process %d -> %d\n", parent->pid, child->pid);
    
    return child;
}

/* Process Exit */
void process_exit(process_t *proc, int exit_code)
{
    proc->exit_code = exit_code;
    proc->state = PROCESS_STATE_ZOMBIE;
    proc->flags |= PROC_FLAG_EXITING;
    
    pr_debug("Process %d '%s' exiting with code %d\n", 
             proc->pid, proc->name, exit_code);
    
    /* Close All Files */
    fd_table_destroy(proc->fd_table);
    proc->fd_table = NULL;
    
    /* Release Memory */
    if (proc->mm) {
        vmm_destroy_mm(proc->mm);
        proc->mm = NULL;
    }
    
    /* Reparent Children to Init */
    process_t *child, *tmp;
    list_for_each_entry_safe(child, tmp, &proc->children, sibling) {
        spin_lock(&child->lock);
        child->parent = init_process;
        list_del(&child->sibling);
        list_add_tail(&child->sibling, &init_process->children);
        spin_unlock(&child->lock);
    }
    
    /* Notify Parent */
    if (proc->parent) {
        proc->parent->pending_signals |= (1UL << SIGCHLD);
        wake_up(&proc->parent->wait_queue);
    }
    
    /* Kill All Threads */
    thread_t *thread;
    list_for_each_entry(thread, &proc->thread_list, thread_list) {
        if (thread != current) {
            thread->state = THREAD_STATE_DEAD;
        }
    }
    
    /* Schedule Away */
    if (current->process == proc) {
        current->state = THREAD_STATE_DEAD;
        schedule();
    }
}

/* Process Kill */
void process_kill(process_t *proc, int signal)
{
    spin_lock(&proc->sighand_lock);
    proc->pending_signals |= (1UL << signal);
    spin_unlock(&proc->sighand_lock);
    
    /* Wake Up If Blocked */
    thread_t *thread;
    list_for_each_entry(thread, &proc->thread_list, thread_list) {
        if (thread->state == THREAD_STATE_BLOCKED ||
            thread->state == THREAD_STATE_SLEEPING) {
            thread_unblock(thread);
        }
    }
}

/* Get Process by PID */
process_t *process_get_by_pid(pid_t pid)
{
    spin_lock(&process_table.lock);
    
    struct rb_node *node = process_table.pid_tree.rb_node;
    process_t *proc = NULL;
    
    while (node) {
        process_t *entry = container_of(node, process_t, pid_node);
        
        if (pid < entry->pid) {
            node = node->rb_left;
        } else if (pid > entry->pid) {
            node = node->rb_right;
        } else {
            proc = entry;
            atomic_inc(&proc->refcount);
            break;
        }
    }
    
    spin_unlock(&process_table.lock);
    return proc;
}

/* Put Process */
void process_put(process_t *proc)
{
    if (atomic_dec_and_test(&proc->refcount)) {
        /* Final Cleanup */
        spin_lock(&process_table.lock);
        list_del(&proc->global_list);
        rb_erase(&proc->pid_node, &process_table.pid_tree);
        process_table.total_processes--;
        spin_unlock(&process_table.lock);
        
        /* Free Resources */
        if (proc->cred) credentials_put(proc->cred);
        if (proc->rlimits) kfree(proc->rlimits);
        
        /* Free Threads */
        thread_t *thread, *tmp;
        list_for_each_entry_safe(thread, tmp, &proc->thread_list, thread_list) {
            list_del(&thread->thread_list);
            free_kernel_stack(thread->kernel_stack);
            kfree(thread);
        }
        
        kfree(proc);
    }
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                     WAIT FUNCTIONS                                        */
/*===========================================================================*/

pid_t wait_pid(pid_t pid, int *status, int options)
{
    process_t *current_proc = current->process;
    
    while (1) {
        spin_lock(&current_proc->lock);
        
        process_t *child;
        list_for_each_entry(child, &current_proc->children, sibling) {
            if (pid > 0 && child->pid != pid) continue;
            if (pid == 0 && child->cred->gid != current_proc->cred->gid) continue;
            
            if (child->state == PROCESS_STATE_ZOMBIE) {
                pid_t child_pid = child->pid;
                if (status) *status = child->exit_code;
                
                /* Collect Zombie */
                list_del(&child->sibling);
                spin_unlock(&current_proc->lock);
                
                /* Account Time */
                current_proc->children_user_time += child->user_time;
                current_proc->children_system_time += child->system_time;
                
                process_put(child);
                return child_pid;
            }
        }
        
        spin_unlock(&current_proc->lock);
        
        /* No Children */
        if (list_empty(&current_proc->children)) {
            return -1;
        }
        
        /* WNOHANG */
        if (options & WNOHANG) {
            return 0;
        }
        
        /* Wait */
        thread_block(&current_proc->wait_queue);
        
        /* Check Signals */
        if (current->pending_signals) {
            return -1;  /* EINTR */
        }
    }
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                     INITIALIZATION                                        */
/*===========================================================================*/

int process_init(void)
{
    pr_info("Initializing process management...\n");
    
    /* Initialize Locks */
    spin_lock_init(&process_table.lock);
    spin_lock_init(&thread_table.lock);
    
    /* Create Kernel Process (PID 0) */
    kernel_process = kzalloc(sizeof(process_t));
    kernel_process->pid = 0;
    strcpy(kernel_process->name, "kernel");
    kernel_process->flags = PROC_FLAG_KERNEL;
    kernel_process->state = PROCESS_STATE_RUNNING;
    INIT_LIST_HEAD(&kernel_process->thread_list);
    INIT_LIST_HEAD(&kernel_process->children);
    INIT_LIST_HEAD(&kernel_process->sibling);
    INIT_LIST_HEAD(&kernel_process->global_list);
    spin_lock_init(&kernel_process->lock);
    atomic_set(&kernel_process->refcount, 1);
    
    /* Create Boot Thread */
    thread_t *boot_thread = kzalloc(sizeof(thread_t));
    boot_thread->tid = 0;
    strcpy(boot_thread->name, "swapper");
    boot_thread->flags = THREAD_FLAG_KERNEL | THREAD_FLAG_IDLE;
    boot_thread->state = THREAD_STATE_RUNNING;
    boot_thread->process = kernel_process;
    boot_thread->priority = SCHED_PRIORITY_MIN;
    INIT_LIST_HEAD(&boot_thread->thread_list);
    spin_lock_init(&boot_thread->lock);
    
    list_add(&boot_thread->thread_list, &kernel_process->thread_list);
    kernel_process->main_thread = boot_thread;
    kernel_process->thread_count = 1;
    
    /* Set Current Thread */
    this_cpu()->current_thread = boot_thread;
    this_cpu()->current_process = kernel_process;
    this_cpu()->idle_thread = boot_thread;
    
    pr_info("Process management initialized.\n");
    return NEXUS_OK;
}

/* Start Init Process */
void start_init(void)
{
    pr_info("Starting init process...\n");
    
    /* Create Init Process */
    init_process = process_create("init", PROC_FLAG_INIT);
    if (!init_process) {
        kernel_panic("Failed to create init process!");
    }
    
    /* Create Main Thread */
    thread_t *init_thread = thread_create(init_process, "init",
                                          init_entry, NULL, 0);
    if (!init_thread) {
        kernel_panic("Failed to create init thread!");
    }
    
    init_process->main_thread = init_thread;
    
    /* Open Standard FDs */
    struct file *console = vfs_open("/dev/console", O_RDWR);
    if (console) {
        fd_alloc(init_process, console);  /* stdin */
        fd_alloc(init_process, console);  /* stdout */
        fd_alloc(init_process, console);  /* stderr */
    }
    
    /* Make Ready */
    init_thread->state = THREAD_STATE_READY;
    init_process->state = PROCESS_STATE_READY;
    scheduler_enqueue(init_thread);
    
    pr_info("Init process (PID 1) started.\n");
}
```

---

# 7. VIRTUALIZATION ENGINE

## 7.1 Hypervisor Core (virt/hypervisor/hypervisor_core.c)

```c
/*
 * NEXUS OS - Hypervisor Core
 * virt/hypervisor/hypervisor_core.c
 */

#include <kernel.h>
#include <virt/hypervisor.h>
#include <virt/vm.h>
#include <mm/mm.h>

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                        HYPERVISOR TYPES                                   */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Virtualization Type */
typedef enum {
    VIRT_TYPE_NONE,
    VIRT_TYPE_VMX,      /* Intel VT-x */
    VIRT_TYPE_SVM,      /* AMD-V */
    VIRT_TYPE_ARM_VHE,  /* ARM VHE */
} virt_type_t;

/* VMCS/VMCB Field IDs */
typedef enum {
    /* Control Fields */
    VMCS_CTRL_PIN_BASED         = 0x4000,
    VMCS_CTRL_PROC_BASED        = 0x4002,
    VMCS_CTRL_PROC_BASED2       = 0x401E,
    VMCS_CTRL_EXIT              = 0x400C,
    VMCS_CTRL_ENTRY             = 0x4012,
    
    /* Guest State */
    VMCS_GUEST_ES_SELECTOR      = 0x0800,
    VMCS_GUEST_CS_SELECTOR      = 0x0802,
    VMCS_GUEST_SS_SELECTOR      = 0x0804,
    VMCS_GUEST_DS_SELECTOR      = 0x0806,
    VMCS_GUEST_FS_SELECTOR      = 0x0808,
    VMCS_GUEST_GS_SELECTOR      = 0x080A,
    VMCS_GUEST_TR_SELECTOR      = 0x080E,
    VMCS_GUEST_LDTR_SELECTOR    = 0x080C,
    
    VMCS_GUEST_CR0              = 0x6800,
    VMCS_GUEST_CR3              = 0x6802,
    VMCS_GUEST_CR4              = 0x6804,
    VMCS_GUEST_RSP              = 0x681C,
    VMCS_GUEST_RIP              = 0x681E,
    VMCS_GUEST_RFLAGS           = 0x6820,
    
    /* Host State */
    VMCS_HOST_CR0               = 0x6C00,
    VMCS_HOST_CR3               = 0x6C02,
    VMCS_HOST_CR4               = 0x6C04,
    VMCS_HOST_RSP               = 0x6C14,
    VMCS_HOST_RIP               = 0x6C16,
    
    /* Exit Information */
    VMCS_EXIT_REASON            = 0x4402,
    VMCS_EXIT_QUALIFICATION     = 0x6400,
    VMCS_EXIT_INT_INFO          = 0x4404,
    VMCS_EXIT_INT_ERROR         = 0x4406,
    VMCS_GUEST_LINEAR_ADDR      = 0x640A,
} vmcs_field_t;

/* VM Exit Reasons */
typedef enum {
    EXIT_REASON_EXCEPTION       = 0,
    EXIT_REASON_EXT_INTERRUPT   = 1,
    EXIT_REASON_TRIPLE_FAULT    = 2,
    EXIT_REASON_INIT            = 3,
    EXIT_REASON_SIPI            = 4,
    EXIT_REASON_IO_SMI          = 5,
    EXIT_REASON_SMI             = 6,
    EXIT_REASON_INT_WINDOW      = 7,
    EXIT_REASON_NMI_WINDOW      = 8,
    EXIT_REASON_TASK_SWITCH     = 9,
    EXIT_REASON_CPUID           = 10,
    EXIT_REASON_GETSEC          = 11,
    EXIT_REASON_HLT             = 12,
    EXIT_REASON_INVD            = 13,
    EXIT_REASON_INVLPG          = 14,
    EXIT_REASON_RDPMC           = 15,
    EXIT_REASON_RDTSC           = 16,
    EXIT_REASON_RSM             = 17,
    EXIT_REASON_VMCALL          = 18,
    EXIT_REASON_VMCLEAR         = 19,
    EXIT_REASON_VMLAUNCH        = 20,
    EXIT_REASON_VMPTRLD         = 21,
    EXIT_REASON_VMPTRST         = 22,
    EXIT_REASON_VMREAD          = 23,
    EXIT_REASON_VMRESUME        = 24,
    EXIT_REASON_VMWRITE         = 25,
    EXIT_REASON_VMXOFF          = 26,
    EXIT_REASON_VMXON           = 27,
    EXIT_REASON_CR_ACCESS       = 28,
    EXIT_REASON_DR_ACCESS       = 29,
    EXIT_REASON_IO              = 30,
    EXIT_REASON_MSR_READ        = 31,
    EXIT_REASON_MSR_WRITE       = 32,
    EXIT_REASON_INVALID_STATE   = 33,
    EXIT_REASON_MSR_LOAD_FAIL   = 34,
    EXIT_REASON_MWAIT           = 36,
    EXIT_REASON_MONITOR         = 39,
    EXIT_REASON_PAUSE           = 40,
    EXIT_REASON_MCE             = 41,
    EXIT_REASON_TPR_THRESHOLD   = 43,
    EXIT_REASON_APIC_ACCESS     = 44,
    EXIT_REASON_GDTR_IDTR       = 46,
    EXIT_REASON_LDTR_TR         = 47,
    EXIT_REASON_EPT_VIOLATION   = 48,
    EXIT_REASON_EPT_MISCONFIG   = 49,
    EXIT_REASON_INVEPT          = 50,
    EXIT_REASON_RDTSCP          = 51,
    EXIT_REASON_PREEMPT_TIMER   = 52,
    EXIT_REASON_INVVPID         = 53,
    EXIT_REASON_WBINVD          = 54,
    EXIT_REASON_XSETBV          = 55,
    EXIT_REASON_APIC_WRITE      = 56,
    EXIT_REASON_RDRAND          = 57,
    EXIT_REASON_INVPCID         = 58,
    EXIT_REASON_VMFUNC          = 59,
    EXIT_REASON_RDSEED          = 61,
    EXIT_REASON_XSAVES          = 63,
    EXIT_REASON_XRSTORS         = 64,
} vm_exit_reason_t;

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                      HYPERVISOR STRUCTURES                                */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Virtual CPU */
typedef struct vcpu {
    u32 vcpu_id;
    struct vm *vm;
    
    /* State */
    enum {
        VCPU_STATE_STOPPED,
        VCPU_STATE_RUNNING,
        VCPU_STATE_BLOCKED,
        VCPU_STATE_PAUSED,
    } state;
    
    /* Hardware State */
    union {
        struct {
            void *vmcs;
            phys_addr_t vmcs_phys;
        } vmx;
        struct {
            void *vmcb;
            phys_addr_t vmcb_phys;
        } svm;
    } hw;
    
    /* Guest Registers */
    struct {
        u64 rax, rbx, rcx, rdx;
        u64 rsi, rdi, rbp, rsp;
        u64 r8, r9, r10, r11;
        u64 r12, r13, r14, r15;
        u64 rip, rflags;
        u64 cr0, cr2, cr3, cr4;
        u64 dr0, dr1, dr2, dr3, dr6, dr7;
        u64 efer;
    } regs;
    
    /* FPU State */
    u8 fpu_state[4096] __aligned(64);
    
    /* Virtual APIC */
    struct {
        u32 id;
        u32 version;
        u32 tpr;
        u32 apr;
        u32 ppr;
        u32 eoi;
        u32 ldr;
        u32 dfr;
        u32 svr;
        u32 isr[8];
        u32 tmr[8];
        u32 irr[8];
        u32 esr;
        u32 icr_low;
        u32 icr_high;
        u32 lvt_timer;
        u32 lvt_thermal;
        u32 lvt_perf;
        u32 lvt_lint0;
        u32 lvt_lint1;
        u32 lvt_error;
        u32 timer_initial;
        u32 timer_current;
        u32 timer_divide;
    } lapic;
    
    /* Interrupt Injection */
    struct {
        bool pending;
        u32 vector;
        u32 type;
        u32 error_code;
        bool has_error;
    } injection;
    
    /* Exit Info */
    struct {
        u32 reason;
        u64 qualification;
        u64 guest_linear;
        u64 guest_physical;
    } exit;
    
    /* Statistics */
    u64 exits;
    u64 host_switches;
    
    /* Thread Running This VCPU */
    thread_t *thread;
    
    /* Lock */
    spinlock_t lock;
    
} vcpu_t;

/* Virtual Machine */
typedef struct vm {
    u32 vm_id;
    char name[64];
    
    /* State */
    enum {
        VM_STATE_CREATED,
        VM_STATE_RUNNING,
        VM_STATE_PAUSED,
        VM_STATE_STOPPED,
    } state;
    
    /* VCPUs */
    vcpu_t *vcpus[MAX_VCPUS];
    u32 vcpu_count;
    
    /* Memory */
    struct {
        phys_addr_t ept_root;       /* EPT/NPT root */
        u64 ram_size;
        void *ram_base;
        struct list_head memory_regions;
    } memory;
    
    /* Virtual Devices */
    struct list_head devices;
    
    /* I/O */
    struct {
        struct io_handler *handlers[65536];
    } pio;
    
    struct {
        struct rb_root mmio_tree;
    } mmio;
    
    /* Event Injection */
    wait_queue_t event_queue;
    
    /* Owner Process */
    process_t *owner;
    
    /* Statistics */
    u64 total_exits;
    u64 ept_violations;
    u64 io_exits;
    
    /* Lock */
    rwlock_t lock;
    
    /* Reference Count */
    atomic_t refcount;
    
} vm_t;

/* Memory Region */
typedef struct vm_memory_region {
    struct list_head list;
    u64 guest_phys_addr;
    u64 size;
    void *host_virt_addr;
    phys_addr_t host_phys_addr;
    u32 flags;
} vm_memory_region_t;

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                        GLOBAL STATE                                       */
/*===========================================================================*/

static struct {
    virt_type_t type;
    bool enabled;
    bool ept_supported;
    bool unrestricted_guest;
    
    /* Per-CPU VMXON region */
    void *vmxon_region[MAX_CPUS];
    phys_addr_t vmxon_phys[MAX_CPUS];
    
    /* VM List */
    struct list_head vm_list;
    spinlock_t lock;
    u32 next_vm_id;
    
} hypervisor = {
    .type = VIRT_TYPE_NONE,
    .enabled = false,
    .vm_list = LIST_HEAD_INIT(hypervisor.vm_list),
    .next_vm_id = 1,
};

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                      VMX OPERATIONS                                       */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* VMX Instructions */
static inline int vmxon(phys_addr_t phys)
{
    u8 error;
    __asm__ __volatile__(
        "vmxon %1; setna %0"
        : "=qm"(error)
        : "m"(phys)
        : "cc", "memory"
    );
    return error ? -1 : 0;
}

static inline void vmxoff(void)
{
    __asm__ __volatile__("vmxoff" ::: "cc");
}

static inline int vmclear(phys_addr_t phys)
{
    u8 error;
    __asm__ __volatile__(
        "vmclear %1; setna %0"
        : "=qm"(error)
        : "m"(phys)
        : "cc", "memory"
    );
    return error ? -1 : 0;
}

static inline int vmptrld(phys_addr_t phys)
{
    u8 error;
    __asm__ __volatile__(
        "vmptrld %1; setna %0"
        : "=qm"(error)
        : "m"(phys)
        : "cc", "memory"
    );
    return error ? -1 : 0;
}

static inline u64 vmread(u64 field)
{
    u64 value;
    __asm__ __volatile__(
        "vmread %1, %0"
        : "=r"(value)
        : "r"(field)
        : "cc"
    );
    return value;
}

static inline void vmwrite(u64 field, u64 value)
{
    __asm__ __volatile__(
        "vmwrite %1, %0"
        :
        : "r"(field), "r"(value)
        : "cc"
    );
}

static inline int vmlaunch(void)
{
    u8 error;
    __asm__ __volatile__(
        "vmlaunch; setna %0"
        : "=qm"(error)
        :
        : "cc", "memory"
    );
    return error ? -1 : 0;
}

static inline int vmresume(void)
{
    u8 error;
    __asm__ __volatile__(
        "vmresume; setna %0"
        : "=qm"(error)
        :
        : "cc", "memory"
    );
    return error ? -1 : 0;
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                     VMX INITIALIZATION                                    */
/*===========================================================================*/

static int vmx_enable(void)
{
    u32 cpu_id = get_cpu_id();
    
    /* Check VMX Support */
    u32 eax, ebx, ecx, edx;
    cpuid(1, 0, &eax, &ebx, &ecx, &edx);
    
    if (!(ecx & (1 << 5))) {
        pr_err("VMX not supported on CPU %d\n", cpu_id);
        return NEXUS_ENOTSUPP;
    }
    
    /* Check IA32_FEATURE_CONTROL */
    u64 feature_control = rdmsr(MSR_IA32_FEATURE_CONTROL);
    
    if (!(feature_control & 1)) {
        /* Lock bit not set - can configure */
        feature_control |= 1;  /* Lock */
        feature_control |= 4;  /* Enable VMX outside SMX */
        wrmsr(MSR_IA32_FEATURE_CONTROL, feature_control);
    } else if (!(feature_control & 4)) {
        pr_err("VMX disabled by BIOS on CPU %d\n", cpu_id);
        return NEXUS_ENOTSUPP;
    }
    
    /* Enable VMX in CR4 */
    u64 cr4 = read_cr4();
    cr4 |= (1 << 13);  /* VMXE */
    write_cr4(cr4);
    
    /* Allocate VMXON Region */
    void *vmxon_region = (void *)pmm_alloc_page(PMM_FLAG_ZERO);
    if (!vmxon_region) {
        return NEXUS_ENOMEM;
    }
    
    hypervisor.vmxon_region[cpu_id] = phys_to_virt((phys_addr_t)vmxon_region);
    hypervisor.vmxon_phys[cpu_id] = (phys_addr_t)vmxon_region;
    
    /* Set VMCS Revision ID */
    u64 vmx_basic = rdmsr(MSR_IA32_VMX_BASIC);
    u32 revision_id = vmx_basic & 0x7FFFFFFF;
    *(u32 *)hypervisor.vmxon_region[cpu_id] = revision_id;
    
    /* Execute VMXON */
    if (vmxon(hypervisor.vmxon_phys[cpu_id]) != 0) {
        pr_err("VMXON failed on CPU %d\n", cpu_id);
        pmm_free_page((phys_addr_t)vmxon_region);
        return NEXUS_ERROR;
    }
    
    pr_info("VMX enabled on CPU %d\n", cpu_id);
    return NEXUS_OK;
}

static void vmx_disable(void)
{
    u32 cpu_id = get_cpu_id();
    
    vmxoff();
    
    if (hypervisor.vmxon_phys[cpu_id]) {
        pmm_free_page(hypervisor.vmxon_phys[cpu_id]);
        hypervisor.vmxon_region[cpu_id] = NULL;
        hypervisor.vmxon_phys[cpu_id] = 0;
    }
    
    /* Disable VMX in CR4 */
    u64 cr4 = read_cr4();
    cr4 &= ~(1 << 13);
    write_cr4(cr4);
    
    pr_info("VMX disabled on CPU %d\n", cpu_id);
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                       EPT MANAGEMENT                                      */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* EPT Entry Flags */
#define EPT_READ        BIT(0)
#define EPT_WRITE       BIT(1)
#define EPT_EXEC        BIT(2)
#define EPT_MEMTYPE_WB  (6UL << 3)
#define EPT_IGNORE_PAT  BIT(6)
#define EPT_LARGE_PAGE  BIT(7)

/* EPT Levels */
#define EPT_PML4_SHIFT  39
#define EPT_PDPT_SHIFT  30
#define EPT_PD_SHIFT    21
#define EPT_PT_SHIFT    12

typedef u64 ept_entry_t;

/* Create EPT Root */
static phys_addr_t ept_create(void)
{
    phys_addr_t root = pmm_alloc_page(PMM_FLAG_ZERO);
    return root;
}

/* Destroy EPT */
static void ept_destroy(phys_addr_t root)
{
    /* TODO: Walk and free all pages */
    pmm_free_page(root);
}

/* Map Guest Physical to Host Physical */
static int ept_map(phys_addr_t ept_root, u64 gpa, phys_addr_t hpa, u64 size, u64 flags)
{
    /* For simplicity, map 4KB pages */
    for (u64 offset = 0; offset < size; offset += PAGE_SIZE) {
        u64 gpa_curr = gpa + offset;
        phys_addr_t hpa_curr = hpa + offset;
        
        /* Get PML4 Entry */
        ept_entry_t *pml4 = phys_to_virt(ept_root);
        u32 pml4_idx = (gpa_curr >> EPT_PML4_SHIFT) & 0x1FF;
        
        if (!(pml4[pml4_idx] & EPT_READ)) {
            phys_addr_t pdpt = pmm_alloc_page(PMM_FLAG_ZERO);
            pml4[pml4_idx] = pdpt | EPT_READ | EPT_WRITE | EPT_EXEC;
        }
        
        /* Get PDPT Entry */
        ept_entry_t *pdpt = phys_to_virt(pml4[pml4_idx] & ~0xFFF);
        u32 pdpt_idx = (gpa_curr >> EPT_PDPT_SHIFT) & 0x1FF;
        
        if (!(pdpt[pdpt_idx] & EPT_READ)) {
            phys_addr_t pd = pmm_alloc_page(PMM_FLAG_ZERO);
            pdpt[pdpt_idx] = pd | EPT_READ | EPT_WRITE | EPT_EXEC;
        }
        
        /* Get PD Entry */
        ept_entry_t *pd = phys_to_virt(pdpt[pdpt_idx] & ~0xFFF);
        u32 pd_idx = (gpa_curr >> EPT_PD_SHIFT) & 0x1FF;
        
        if (!(pd[pd_idx] & EPT_READ)) {
            phys_addr_t pt = pmm_alloc_page(PMM_FLAG_ZERO);
            pd[pd_idx] = pt | EPT_READ | EPT_WRITE | EPT_EXEC;
        }
        
        /* Get PT Entry */
        ept_entry_t *pt = phys_to_virt(pd[pd_idx] & ~0xFFF);
        u32 pt_idx = (gpa_curr >> EPT_PT_SHIFT) & 0x1FF;
        
        pt[pt_idx] = hpa_curr | flags | EPT_MEMTYPE_WB | EPT_IGNORE_PAT;
    }
    
    return NEXUS_OK;
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                        VCPU OPERATIONS                                    */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Create VCPU */
vcpu_t *vcpu_create(vm_t *vm, u32 vcpu_id)
{
    vcpu_t *vcpu = kzalloc(sizeof(vcpu_t));
    if (!vcpu) return NULL;
    
    vcpu->vcpu_id = vcpu_id;
    vcpu->vm = vm;
    vcpu->state = VCPU_STATE_STOPPED;
    spin_lock_init(&vcpu->lock);
    
    /* Allocate VMCS */
    vcpu->hw.vmx.vmcs_phys = pmm_alloc_page(PMM_FLAG_ZERO);
    if (!vcpu->hw.vmx.vmcs_phys) {
        kfree(vcpu);
        return NULL;
    }
    vcpu->hw.vmx.vmcs = phys_to_virt(vcpu->hw.vmx.vmcs_phys);
    
    /* Set VMCS Revision ID */
    u64 vmx_basic = rdmsr(MSR_IA32_VMX_BASIC);
    *(u32 *)vcpu->hw.vmx.vmcs = vmx_basic & 0x7FFFFFFF;
    
    /* Clear VMCS */
    vmclear(vcpu->hw.vmx.vmcs_phys);
    
    /* Load VMCS */
    vmptrld(vcpu->hw.vmx.vmcs_phys);
    
    /* Setup VMCS */
    vcpu_setup_vmcs(vcpu);
    
    pr_debug("Created VCPU %d for VM %d\n", vcpu_id, vm->vm_id);
    
    return vcpu;
}

/* Setup VMCS */
static void vcpu_setup_vmcs(vcpu_t *vcpu)
{
    /* Pin-Based Controls */
    u64 pin_based = rdmsr(MSR_IA32_VMX_PINBASED_CTLS);
    u32 pin_based_min = pin_based & 0xFFFFFFFF;
    u32 pin_based_max = pin_based >> 32;
    u32 pin_ctrl = pin_based_min;
    pin_ctrl |= (1 << 0);  /* External Interrupt Exiting */
    vmwrite(VMCS_CTRL_PIN_BASED, pin_ctrl);
    
    /* Primary Proc-Based Controls */
    u64 proc_based = rdmsr(MSR_IA32_VMX_PROCBASED_CTLS);
    u32 proc_based_min = proc_based & 0xFFFFFFFF;
    u32 proc_ctrl = proc_based_min;
    proc_ctrl |= (1 << 7);   /* HLT Exiting */
    proc_ctrl |= (1 << 24);  /* I/O Exiting */
    proc_ctrl |= (1 << 25);  /* I/O Bitmaps */
    proc_ctrl |= (1 << 28);  /* MSR Bitmaps */
    proc_ctrl |= (1 << 31);  /* Secondary Controls */
    vmwrite(VMCS_CTRL_PROC_BASED, proc_ctrl);
    
    /* Secondary Proc-Based Controls */
    u64 proc_based2 = rdmsr(MSR_IA32_VMX_PROCBASED_CTLS2);
    u32 proc_ctrl2 = 0;
    proc_ctrl2 |= (1 << 1);  /* EPT */
    proc_ctrl2 |= (1 << 5);  /* VPID */
    if (hypervisor.unrestricted_guest) {
        proc_ctrl2 |= (1 << 7);  /* Unrestricted Guest */
    }
    vmwrite(VMCS_CTRL_PROC_BASED2, proc_ctrl2);
    
    /* VM Exit Controls */
    u64 exit_ctls = rdmsr(MSR_IA32_VMX_EXIT_CTLS);
    u32 exit_ctrl = exit_ctls & 0xFFFFFFFF;
    exit_ctrl |= (1 << 9);   /* Host Address Space Size (64-bit) */
    exit_ctrl |= (1 << 15);  /* Acknowledge Interrupt on Exit */
    vmwrite(VMCS_CTRL_EXIT, exit_ctrl);
    
    /* VM Entry Controls */
    u64 entry_ctls = rdmsr(MSR_IA32_VMX_ENTRY_CTLS);
    u32 entry_ctrl = entry_ctls & 0xFFFFFFFF;
    entry_ctrl |= (1 << 9);  /* IA-32e Mode Guest */
    vmwrite(VMCS_CTRL_ENTRY, entry_ctrl);
    
    /* EPT Pointer */
    u64 eptp = vcpu->vm->memory.ept_root;
    eptp |= (3 << 3);  /* Page-walk length 4 */
    eptp |= 6;         /* Write-back memory type */
    vmwrite(0x201A, eptp);
    
    /* VPID */
    vmwrite(0x0000, vcpu->vm->vm_id);
    
    /* Setup Host State */
    vmwrite(VMCS_HOST_CR0, read_cr0());
    vmwrite(VMCS_HOST_CR3, read_cr3());
    vmwrite(VMCS_HOST_CR4, read_cr4());
    vmwrite(VMCS_HOST_RSP, (u64)vcpu + sizeof(vcpu_t));
    vmwrite(VMCS_HOST_RIP, (u64)vm_exit_handler);
    
    /* Host Segment Selectors */
    vmwrite(0x0C00, KERNEL_CS);  /* CS */
    vmwrite(0x0C02, KERNEL_DS);  /* SS */
    vmwrite(0x0C04, KERNEL_DS);  /* DS */
    vmwrite(0x0C06, KERNEL_DS);  /* ES */
    vmwrite(0x0C08, KERNEL_DS);  /* FS */
    vmwrite(0x0C0A, KERNEL_DS);  /* GS */
    vmwrite(0x0C0C, TSS_SELECTOR);  /* TR */
    
    /* Initialize Guest State */
    vcpu_init_guest_state(vcpu);
}

/* Initialize Guest State */
static void vcpu_init_guest_state(vcpu_t *vcpu)
{
    /* Segment Selectors */
    vmwrite(VMCS_GUEST_CS_SELECTOR, 0);
    vmwrite(VMCS_GUEST_SS_SELECTOR, 0);
    vmwrite(VMCS_GUEST_DS_SELECTOR, 0);
    vmwrite(VMCS_GUEST_ES_SELECTOR, 0);
    vmwrite(VMCS_GUEST_FS_SELECTOR, 0);
    vmwrite(VMCS_GUEST_GS_SELECTOR, 0);
    vmwrite(VMCS_GUEST_TR_SELECTOR, 0);
    vmwrite(VMCS_GUEST_LDTR_SELECTOR, 0);
    
    /* Control Registers */
    vmwrite(VMCS_GUEST_CR0, 0x60000010);  /* PE, PG bits */
    vmwrite(VMCS_GUEST_CR3, 0);
    vmwrite(VMCS_GUEST_CR4, 0x2000);      /* VMXE */
    
    /* RIP, RSP, RFLAGS */
    vmwrite(VMCS_GUEST_RIP, 0xFFF0);      /* Reset vector */
    vmwrite(VMCS_GUEST_RSP, 0);
    vmwrite(VMCS_GUEST_RFLAGS, 0x2);
    
    /* Initialize LAPIC */
    vcpu->lapic.id = vcpu->vcpu_id << 24;
    vcpu->lapic.version = 0x14;
    vcpu->lapic.svr = 0xFF;
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                         VM OPERATIONS                                     */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Create VM */
vm_t *vm_create(const char *name)
{
    vm_t *vm = kzalloc(sizeof(vm_t));
    if (!vm) return NULL;
    
    spin_lock(&hypervisor.lock);
    vm->vm_id = hypervisor.next_vm_id++;
    spin_unlock(&hypervisor.lock);
    
    strncpy(vm->name, name, sizeof(vm->name) - 1);
    vm->state = VM_STATE_CREATED;
    vm->owner = current_proc;
    
    INIT_LIST_HEAD(&vm->memory.memory_regions);
    INIT_LIST_HEAD(&vm->devices);
    init_waitqueue_head(&vm->event_queue);
    rwlock_init(&vm->lock);
    atomic_set(&vm->refcount, 1);
    
    /* Create EPT */
    vm->memory.ept_root = ept_create();
    if (!vm->memory.ept_root) {
        kfree(vm);
        return NULL;
    }
    
    /* Add to VM List */
    spin_lock(&hypervisor.lock);
    list_add_tail(&vm->list, &hypervisor.vm_list);
    spin_unlock(&hypervisor.lock);
    
    pr_info("Created VM %d '%s'\n", vm->vm_id, vm->name);
    
    return vm;
}

/* Add Memory to VM */
int vm_add_memory(vm_t *vm, u64 guest_phys, u64 size)
{
    /* Allocate Host Memory */
    void *host_mem = vmalloc(size);
    if (!host_mem) {
        return NEXUS_ENOMEM;
    }
    
    memset(host_mem, 0, size);
    
    /* Create Memory Region */
    vm_memory_region_t *region = kzalloc(sizeof(vm_memory_region_t));
    if (!region) {
        vfree(host_mem);
        return NEXUS_ENOMEM;
    }
    
    region->guest_phys_addr = guest_phys;
    region->size = size;
    region->host_virt_addr = host_mem;
    region->host_phys_addr = vmm_translate(kernel_pgd, (virt_addr_t)host_mem);
    region->flags = EPT_READ | EPT_WRITE | EPT_EXEC;
    
    /* Map in EPT */
    /* Note: This simplified version doesn't handle fragmented physical memory */
    for (u64 offset = 0; offset < size; offset += PAGE_SIZE) {
        phys_addr_t hpa = vmm_translate(kernel_pgd, 
                                        (virt_addr_t)host_mem + offset);
        ept_map(vm->memory.ept_root, guest_phys + offset, hpa, 
                PAGE_SIZE, region->flags);
    }
    
    write_lock(&vm->lock);
    list_add_tail(&region->list, &vm->memory.memory_regions);
    vm->memory.ram_size += size;
    write_unlock(&vm->lock);
    
    pr_debug("VM %d: Added %llu MB at GPA 0x%llx\n", 
             vm->vm_id, size / MB(1), guest_phys);
    
    return NEXUS_OK;
}

/* Run VCPU */
int vcpu_run(vcpu_t *vcpu)
{
    int result;
    
    spin_lock(&vcpu->lock);
    
    if (vcpu->state != VCPU_STATE_STOPPED && vcpu->state != VCPU_STATE_BLOCKED) {
        spin_unlock(&vcpu->lock);
        return NEXUS_EBUSY;
    }
    
    vcpu->state = VCPU_STATE_RUNNING;
    vcpu->thread = current;
    
    spin_unlock(&vcpu->lock);
    
    /* Load VMCS */
    vmptrld(vcpu->hw.vmx.vmcs_phys);
    
    /* Inject Pending Interrupt */
    if (vcpu->injection.pending) {
        u32 int_info = vcpu->injection.vector;
        int_info |= (vcpu->injection.type << 8);
        int_info |= (1 << 31);  /* Valid */
        if (vcpu->injection.has_error) {
            int_info |= (1 << 11);
            vmwrite(0x4018, vcpu->injection.error_code);
        }
        vmwrite(0x4016, int_info);
        vcpu->injection.pending = false;
    }
    
    /* Save Host FPU State, Load Guest FPU State */
    hal.cpu->save_fpu_state(current->context.fpu_state);
    hal.cpu->restore_fpu_state(vcpu->fpu_state);
    
    /* VM Entry */
    result = vm_enter(vcpu);
    
    /* Save Guest FPU State, Restore Host FPU State */
    hal.cpu->save_fpu_state(vcpu->fpu_state);
    hal.cpu->restore_fpu_state(current->context.fpu_state);
    
    /* Read Exit Info */
    vcpu->exit.reason = vmread(VMCS_EXIT_REASON) & 0xFFFF;
    vcpu->exit.qualification = vmread(VMCS_EXIT_QUALIFICATION);
    
    vcpu->exits++;
    vcpu->vm->total_exits++;
    
    /* Handle Exit */
    result = vm_exit_handle(vcpu);
    
    return result;
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                         VM EXIT HANDLING                                  */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* VM Exit Handler (Assembly Entry Point) */
__attribute__((naked)) void vm_exit_handler(void)
{
    __asm__ __volatile__(
        /* Save Guest Registers */
        "push %%rax\n\t"
        "push %%rbx\n\t"
        "push %%rcx\n\t"
        "push %%rdx\n\t"
        "push %%rsi\n\t"
        "push %%rdi\n\t"
        "push %%rbp\n\t"
        "push %%r8\n\t"
        "push %%r9\n\t"
        "push %%r10\n\t"
        "push %%r11\n\t"
        "push %%r12\n\t"
        "push %%r13\n\t"
        "push %%r14\n\t"
        "push %%r15\n\t"
        
        /* Call C Handler */
        "mov %%rsp, %%rdi\n\t"
        "call vm_exit_handle_asm\n\t"
        
        /* Restore Guest Registers */
        "pop %%r15\n\t"
        "pop %%r14\n\t"
        "pop %%r13\n\t"
        "pop %%r12\n\t"
        "pop %%r11\n\t"
        "pop %%r10\n\t"
        "pop %%r9\n\t"
        "pop %%r8\n\t"
        "pop %%rbp\n\t"
        "pop %%rdi\n\t"
        "pop %%rsi\n\t"
        "pop %%rdx\n\t"
        "pop %%rcx\n\t"
        "pop %%rbx\n\t"
        "pop %%rax\n\t"
        
        /* Resume */
        "vmresume\n\t"
        
        ::: "memory"
    );
}

/* Handle VM Exit */
int vm_exit_handle(vcpu_t *vcpu)
{
    switch (vcpu->exit.reason) {
    case EXIT_REASON_CPUID:
        return handle_cpuid(vcpu);
        
    case EXIT_REASON_HLT:
        return handle_hlt(vcpu);
        
    case EXIT_REASON_IO:
        return handle_io(vcpu);
        
    case EXIT_REASON_MSR_READ:
        return handle_rdmsr(vcpu);
        
    case EXIT_REASON_MSR_WRITE:
        return handle_wrmsr(vcpu);
        
    case EXIT_REASON_EPT_VIOLATION:
        return handle_ept_violation(vcpu);
        
    case EXIT_REASON_VMCALL:
        return handle_vmcall(vcpu);
        
    case EXIT_REASON_CR_ACCESS:
        return handle_cr_access(vcpu);
        
    case EXIT_REASON_EXT_INTERRUPT:
        /* Host Interrupt - Return to Handle */
        return 1;
        
    default:
        pr_warn("Unhandled VM exit: reason=%d\n", vcpu->exit.reason);
        return -1;
    }
}

/* Handle CPUID */
static int handle_cpuid(vcpu_t *vcpu)
{
    u32 leaf = vcpu->regs.rax;
    u32 subleaf = vcpu->regs.rcx;
    u32 eax, ebx, ecx, edx;
    
    /* Execute Real CPUID */
    cpuid(leaf, subleaf, &eax, &ebx, &ecx, &edx);
    
    /* Mask Features */
    if (leaf == 1) {
        ecx &= ~(1 << 5);  /* Hide VMX */
    }
    
    vcpu->regs.rax = eax;
    vcpu->regs.rbx = ebx;
    vcpu->regs.rcx = ecx;
    vcpu->regs.rdx = edx;
    
    /* Advance RIP */
    vcpu->regs.rip += vmread(0x440C);  /* VM Exit Instruction Length */
    vmwrite(VMCS_GUEST_RIP, vcpu->regs.rip);
    
    return 0;
}

/* Handle I/O */
static int handle_io(vcpu_t *vcpu)
{
    u64 qual = vcpu->exit.qualification;
    
    u16 port = (qual >> 16) & 0xFFFF;
    u8 size = (qual & 7) + 1;
    bool is_in = (qual >> 3) & 1;
    bool is_string = (qual >> 4) & 1;
    
    if (is_string) {
        /* String I/O - More complex handling needed */
        pr_warn("String I/O not fully implemented\n");
        return -1;
    }
    
    if (is_in) {
        /* Port Input */
        u32 value = 0;
        
        /* Check for Virtual Device */
        if (vcpu->vm->pio.handlers[port]) {
            value = vcpu->vm->pio.handlers[port]->read(port, size);
        } else {
            /* Pass Through */
            switch (size) {
            case 1: value = inb(port); break;
            case 2: value = inw(port); break;
            case 4: value = inl(port); break;
            }
        }
        
        vcpu->regs.rax = value;
    } else {
        /* Port Output */
        u32 value = vcpu->regs.rax;
        
        if (vcpu->vm->pio.handlers[port]) {
            vcpu->vm->pio.handlers[port]->write(port, size, value);
        } else {
            switch (size) {
            case 1: outb(port, value); break;
            case 2: outw(port, value); break;
            case 4: outl(port, value); break;
            }
        }
    }
    
    vcpu->vm->io_exits++;
    
    /* Advance RIP */
    vcpu->regs.rip += vmread(0x440C);
    vmwrite(VMCS_GUEST_RIP, vcpu->regs.rip);
    
    return 0;
}

/* Handle EPT Violation */
static int handle_ept_violation(vcpu_t *vcpu)
{
    u64 guest_phys = vmread(0x2400);
    u64 guest_linear = vmread(VMCS_GUEST_LINEAR_ADDR);
    u64 qual = vcpu->exit.qualification;
    
    pr_debug("EPT violation: GPA=0x%llx GVA=0x%llx qual=0x%llx\n",
             guest_phys, guest_linear, qual);
    
    vcpu->vm->ept_violations++;
    
    /* Check MMIO */
    /* TODO: Handle MMIO */
    
    return -1;  /* Unhandled */
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                     HYPERVISOR INITIALIZATION                             */
/*===========================================================================*/

int hypervisor_init(void)
{
    pr_info("Initializing hypervisor...\n");
    
    /* Detect Virtualization Type */
    u32 eax, ebx, ecx, edx;
    cpuid(1, 0, &eax, &ebx, &ecx, &edx);
    
    if (ecx & (1 << 5)) {
        hypervisor.type = VIRT_TYPE_VMX;
        pr_info("  Intel VT-x detected\n");
    } else {
        cpuid(0x80000001, 0, &eax, &ebx, &ecx, &edx);
        if (ecx & (1 << 2)) {
            hypervisor.type = VIRT_TYPE_SVM;
            pr_info("  AMD-V detected\n");
        }
    }
    
    if (hypervisor.type == VIRT_TYPE_NONE) {
        pr_warn("  No hardware virtualization support\n");
        return NEXUS_ENOTSUPP;
    }
    
    /* Check EPT Support */
    if (hypervisor.type == VIRT_TYPE_VMX) {
        u64 ept_vpid_cap = rdmsr(MSR_IA32_VMX_EPT_VPID_CAP);
        hypervisor.ept_supported = (ept_vpid_cap & 0x4000004C) == 0x4000004C;
        
        u64 proc_based2 = rdmsr(MSR_IA32_VMX_PROCBASED_CTLS2);
        hypervisor.unrestricted_guest = (proc_based2 >> 32) & (1 << 7);
        
        pr_info("  EPT: %s\n", hypervisor.ept_supported ? "supported" : "not supported");
        pr_info("  Unrestricted Guest: %s\n", 
                hypervisor.unrestricted_guest ? "supported" : "not supported");
    }
    
    /* Initialize Lock */
    spin_lock_init(&hypervisor.lock);
    
    /* Enable VMX on Boot CPU */
    int ret = vmx_enable();
    if (ret != NEXUS_OK) {
        return ret;
    }
    
    hypervisor.enabled = true;
    
    pr_info("Hypervisor initialized.\n");
    return NEXUS_OK;
}

/* Enable Hypervisor on Secondary CPUs */
void hypervisor_enable_secondary(void)
{
    if (!hypervisor.enabled) return;
    
    if (hypervisor.type == VIRT_TYPE_VMX) {
        vmx_enable();
    }
}
```

---

# 8. FILE SYSTEM

## 8.1 VFS Core (fs/vfs/vfs_core.c)

```c
/*
 * NEXUS OS - Virtual File System
 * fs/vfs/vfs_core.c
 */

#include <kernel.h>
#include <fs/vfs.h>
#include <mm/mm.h>

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                         VFS STRUCTURES                                    */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* File Types */
typedef enum {
    VFS_TYPE_UNKNOWN,
    VFS_TYPE_FILE,
    VFS_TYPE_DIR,
    VFS_TYPE_SYMLINK,
    VFS_TYPE_CHARDEV,
    VFS_TYPE_BLOCKDEV,
    VFS_TYPE_FIFO,
    VFS_TYPE_SOCKET,
} vfs_type_t;

/* File Permissions */
#define VFS_PERM_READ   0x04
#define VFS_PERM_WRITE  0x02
#define VFS_PERM_EXEC   0x01

/* VFS Inode */
typedef struct vfs_inode {
    u64 ino;
    vfs_type_t type;
    mode_t mode;
    uid_t uid;
    gid_t gid;
    u64 size;
    u64 blocks;
    time_t atime;
    time_t mtime;
    time_t ctime;
    u32 nlink;
    
    /* Device Numbers (for device files) */
    u32 major;
    u32 minor;
    
    /* Operations */
    struct inode_ops *ops;
    struct file_ops *fops;
    
    /* File System */
    struct superblock *sb;
    void *fs_data;
    
    /* Cache */
    struct list_head dirty_list;
    bool dirty;
    
    /* Reference Count */
    atomic_t refcount;
    
    /* Lock */
    rwlock_t lock;
    
    /* List */
    struct list_head list;
    struct rb_node rb_node;
    
} vfs_inode_t;

/* Directory Entry */
typedef struct vfs_dentry {
    char name[256];
    vfs_inode_t *inode;
    struct vfs_dentry *parent;
    struct list_head children;
    struct list_head sibling;
    
    /* Hash */
    u32 hash;
    struct list_head hash_list;
    
    /* Flags */
    u32 flags;
    #define DENTRY_MOUNTED  BIT(0)
    #define DENTRY_NEGATIVE BIT(1)
    
    /* Mount Point */
    struct mount *mount;
    
    /* Reference Count */
    atomic_t refcount;
    
    /* Lock */
    spinlock_t lock;
    
} vfs_dentry_t;

/* File */
typedef struct file {
    vfs_dentry_t *dentry;
    vfs_inode_t *inode;
    struct file_ops *ops;
    
    off_t pos;
    u32 flags;
    mode_t mode;
    
    /* Private Data */
    void *private_data;
    
    /* Lock */
    spinlock_t lock;
    
    /* Reference Count */
    atomic_t refcount;
    
} file_t;

/* Inode Operations */
typedef struct inode_ops {
    int (*create)(vfs_inode_t *dir, vfs_dentry_t *dentry, mode_t mode);
    vfs_dentry_t *(*lookup)(vfs_inode_t *dir, const char *name);
    int (*link)(vfs_dentry_t *old, vfs_inode_t *dir, vfs_dentry_t *new);
    int (*unlink)(vfs_inode_t *dir, vfs_dentry_t *dentry);
    int (*symlink)(vfs_inode_t *dir, vfs_dentry_t *dentry, const char *target);
    int (*mkdir)(vfs_inode_t *dir, vfs_dentry_t *dentry, mode_t mode);
    int (*rmdir)(vfs_inode_t *dir, vfs_dentry_t *dentry);
    int (*rename)(vfs_inode_t *old_dir, vfs_dentry_t *old,
                  vfs_inode_t *new_dir, vfs_dentry_t *new);
    int (*truncate)(vfs_inode_t *inode, off_t size);
    int (*setattr)(vfs_inode_t *inode, struct stat *attr);
    int (*getattr)(vfs_inode_t *inode, struct stat *attr);
} inode_ops_t;

/* File Operations */
typedef struct file_ops {
    int (*open)(vfs_inode_t *inode, file_t *file);
    int (*close)(file_t *file);
    ssize_t (*read)(file_t *file, void *buf, size_t count, off_t *pos);
    ssize_t (*write)(file_t *file, const void *buf, size_t count, off_t *pos);
    off_t (*seek)(file_t *file, off_t offset, int whence);
    int (*readdir)(file_t *file, struct dirent *dirent);
    int (*ioctl)(file_t *file, u32 cmd, void *arg);
    int (*mmap)(file_t *file, struct vm_area_struct *vma);
    int (*fsync)(file_t *file);
    int (*poll)(file_t *file, struct poll_table *wait);
} file_ops_t;

/* Superblock */
typedef struct superblock {
    char type[32];
    struct fs_type *fs_type;
    struct block_device *bdev;
    
    u64 block_size;
    u64 total_blocks;
    u64 free_blocks;
    u64 total_inodes;
    u64 free_inodes;
    
    vfs_inode_t *root_inode;
    vfs_dentry_t *root_dentry;
    
    struct superblock_ops *ops;
    void *fs_data;
    
    /* Mount */
    struct list_head mounts;
    
    /* Dirty Inodes */
    struct list_head dirty_inodes;
    
    /* Lock */
    rwlock_t lock;
    
    /* List */
```
