    struct list_head list;
    
} superblock_t;

/* Superblock Operations */
typedef struct superblock_ops {
    void (*write_super)(superblock_t *sb);
    void (*put_super)(superblock_t *sb);
    int (*sync_fs)(superblock_t *sb, int wait);
    int (*statfs)(superblock_t *sb, struct statfs *buf);
    vfs_inode_t *(*alloc_inode)(superblock_t *sb);
    void (*free_inode)(vfs_inode_t *inode);
    void (*write_inode)(vfs_inode_t *inode, bool sync);
    void (*drop_inode)(vfs_inode_t *inode);
} superblock_ops_t;

/* File System Type */
typedef struct fs_type {
    const char *name;
    u32 flags;
    #define FS_REQUIRES_DEV     BIT(0)
    #define FS_NODEV            BIT(1)
    #define FS_NOUSER           BIT(2)
    
    superblock_t *(*mount)(struct fs_type *fs, const char *dev, 
                           const void *data);
    void (*unmount)(superblock_t *sb);
    
    struct list_head list;
} fs_type_t;

/* Mount */
typedef struct mount {
    superblock_t *sb;
    vfs_dentry_t *mountpoint;
    vfs_dentry_t *root;
    
    char *device;
    char *mount_path;
    u32 flags;
    
    struct list_head list;
    struct list_head sb_list;
    
    atomic_t refcount;
} mount_t;

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                          GLOBAL DATA                                      */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Root */
static vfs_dentry_t *vfs_root = NULL;
static superblock_t *root_sb = NULL;

/* File System Types */
static LIST_HEAD(fs_types);
static spinlock_t fs_types_lock = {0};

/* Mount List */
static LIST_HEAD(mount_list);
static rwlock_t mount_lock = {0};

/* Dentry Cache */
#define DENTRY_HASH_SIZE    4096
static struct list_head dentry_hashtable[DENTRY_HASH_SIZE];
static spinlock_t dentry_hash_lock = {0};

/* Inode Cache */
static struct kmem_cache *inode_cache = NULL;
static struct kmem_cache *dentry_cache = NULL;
static struct kmem_cache *file_cache = NULL;

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                        DENTRY OPERATIONS                                  */
/*===========================================================================*/

static u32 dentry_hash(const char *name, vfs_dentry_t *parent)
{
    u32 hash = 5381;
    while (*name) {
        hash = ((hash << 5) + hash) + *name++;
    }
    hash ^= (u64)parent;
    return hash % DENTRY_HASH_SIZE;
}

static vfs_dentry_t *dentry_alloc(const char *name, vfs_dentry_t *parent)
{
    vfs_dentry_t *dentry = kmem_cache_alloc(dentry_cache);
    if (!dentry) return NULL;
    
    memset(dentry, 0, sizeof(vfs_dentry_t));
    strncpy(dentry->name, name, sizeof(dentry->name) - 1);
    dentry->parent = parent;
    dentry->hash = dentry_hash(name, parent);
    
    INIT_LIST_HEAD(&dentry->children);
    INIT_LIST_HEAD(&dentry->sibling);
    INIT_LIST_HEAD(&dentry->hash_list);
    
    spin_lock_init(&dentry->lock);
    atomic_set(&dentry->refcount, 1);
    
    /* Add to Parent */
    if (parent) {
        spin_lock(&parent->lock);
        list_add_tail(&dentry->sibling, &parent->children);
        spin_unlock(&parent->lock);
    }
    
    /* Add to Hash Table */
    spin_lock(&dentry_hash_lock);
    list_add(&dentry->hash_list, &dentry_hashtable[dentry->hash]);
    spin_unlock(&dentry_hash_lock);
    
    return dentry;
}

static vfs_dentry_t *dentry_lookup_hash(const char *name, vfs_dentry_t *parent)
{
    u32 hash = dentry_hash(name, parent);
    
    spin_lock(&dentry_hash_lock);
    
    vfs_dentry_t *dentry;
    list_for_each_entry(dentry, &dentry_hashtable[hash], hash_list) {
        if (dentry->parent == parent && strcmp(dentry->name, name) == 0) {
            atomic_inc(&dentry->refcount);
            spin_unlock(&dentry_hash_lock);
            return dentry;
        }
    }
    
    spin_unlock(&dentry_hash_lock);
    return NULL;
}

void vfs_dentry_get(vfs_dentry_t *dentry)
{
    atomic_inc(&dentry->refcount);
}

void vfs_dentry_put(vfs_dentry_t *dentry)
{
    if (atomic_dec_and_test(&dentry->refcount)) {
        /* Remove from Hash */
        spin_lock(&dentry_hash_lock);
        list_del(&dentry->hash_list);
        spin_unlock(&dentry_hash_lock);
        
        /* Remove from Parent */
        if (dentry->parent) {
            spin_lock(&dentry->parent->lock);
            list_del(&dentry->sibling);
            spin_unlock(&dentry->parent->lock);
        }
        
        if (dentry->inode) {
            vfs_inode_put(dentry->inode);
        }
        
        kmem_cache_free(dentry_cache, dentry);
    }
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                        INODE OPERATIONS                                   */
/*===========================================================================*/

vfs_inode_t *vfs_inode_alloc(superblock_t *sb)
{
    vfs_inode_t *inode;
    
    if (sb->ops && sb->ops->alloc_inode) {
        inode = sb->ops->alloc_inode(sb);
    } else {
        inode = kmem_cache_alloc(inode_cache);
    }
    
    if (!inode) return NULL;
    
    memset(inode, 0, sizeof(vfs_inode_t));
    inode->sb = sb;
    
    INIT_LIST_HEAD(&inode->dirty_list);
    INIT_LIST_HEAD(&inode->list);
    
    rwlock_init(&inode->lock);
    atomic_set(&inode->refcount, 1);
    
    return inode;
}

void vfs_inode_get(vfs_inode_t *inode)
{
    atomic_inc(&inode->refcount);
}

void vfs_inode_put(vfs_inode_t *inode)
{
    if (atomic_dec_and_test(&inode->refcount)) {
        if (inode->sb->ops && inode->sb->ops->drop_inode) {
            inode->sb->ops->drop_inode(inode);
        }
        
        if (inode->sb->ops && inode->sb->ops->free_inode) {
            inode->sb->ops->free_inode(inode);
        } else {
            kmem_cache_free(inode_cache, inode);
        }
    }
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                        PATH RESOLUTION                                    */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Resolve Path to Dentry */
vfs_dentry_t *vfs_path_resolve(const char *path, vfs_dentry_t *base)
{
    if (!path || !*path) return NULL;
    
    vfs_dentry_t *current;
    
    /* Absolute or Relative */
    if (path[0] == '/') {
        current = vfs_root;
        path++;
    } else if (base) {
        current = base;
    } else {
        current = current_proc->cwd;
        if (!current) current = vfs_root;
    }
    
    vfs_dentry_get(current);
    
    char component[256];
    
    while (*path) {
        /* Skip Slashes */
        while (*path == '/') path++;
        if (!*path) break;
        
        /* Extract Component */
        int i = 0;
        while (*path && *path != '/' && i < 255) {
            component[i++] = *path++;
        }
        component[i] = '\0';
        
        /* Handle . and .. */
        if (strcmp(component, ".") == 0) {
            continue;
        } else if (strcmp(component, "..") == 0) {
            if (current->parent && current != vfs_root) {
                vfs_dentry_t *parent = current->parent;
                vfs_dentry_get(parent);
                vfs_dentry_put(current);
                current = parent;
            }
            continue;
        }
        
        /* Lookup in Cache */
        vfs_dentry_t *next = dentry_lookup_hash(component, current);
        
        if (!next) {
            /* Cache Miss - Call FS Lookup */
            if (current->inode && current->inode->ops && 
                current->inode->ops->lookup) {
                next = current->inode->ops->lookup(current->inode, component);
                if (next) {
                    /* Add to Cache */
                    vfs_dentry_t *cached = dentry_alloc(component, current);
                    cached->inode = next->inode;
                    if (cached->inode) vfs_inode_get(cached->inode);
                    next = cached;
                }
            }
        }
        
        if (!next) {
            vfs_dentry_put(current);
            return NULL;
        }
        
        /* Handle Mount Points */
        if (next->flags & DENTRY_MOUNTED) {
            vfs_dentry_t *mounted_root = next->mount->root;
            vfs_dentry_get(mounted_root);
            vfs_dentry_put(next);
            next = mounted_root;
        }
        
        vfs_dentry_put(current);
        current = next;
    }
    
    return current;
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                        FILE OPERATIONS                                    */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Open File */
file_t *vfs_open(const char *path, u32 flags)
{
    /* Resolve Path */
    vfs_dentry_t *dentry = vfs_path_resolve(path, NULL);
    
    /* Handle O_CREAT */
    if (!dentry && (flags & O_CREAT)) {
        /* Get Parent Directory */
        char *parent_path = strdup(path);
        char *name = strrchr(parent_path, '/');
        if (name) {
            *name = '\0';
            name++;
        } else {
            name = parent_path;
            parent_path = ".";
        }
        
        vfs_dentry_t *parent = vfs_path_resolve(parent_path, NULL);
        if (!parent || !parent->inode) {
            return NULL;
        }
        
        /* Create File */
        if (parent->inode->ops && parent->inode->ops->create) {
            vfs_dentry_t *new_dentry = dentry_alloc(name, parent);
            if (parent->inode->ops->create(parent->inode, new_dentry, 0644) == 0) {
                dentry = new_dentry;
            }
        }
        
        vfs_dentry_put(parent);
    }
    
    if (!dentry || !dentry->inode) {
        if (dentry) vfs_dentry_put(dentry);
        return NULL;
    }
    
    /* Allocate File */
    file_t *file = kmem_cache_alloc(file_cache);
    if (!file) {
        vfs_dentry_put(dentry);
        return NULL;
    }
    
    memset(file, 0, sizeof(file_t));
    file->dentry = dentry;
    file->inode = dentry->inode;
    file->ops = dentry->inode->fops;
    file->flags = flags;
    file->pos = 0;
    
    spin_lock_init(&file->lock);
    atomic_set(&file->refcount, 1);
    
    vfs_inode_get(file->inode);
    
    /* Call Open */
    if (file->ops && file->ops->open) {
        int ret = file->ops->open(file->inode, file);
        if (ret != 0) {
            vfs_inode_put(file->inode);
            vfs_dentry_put(dentry);
            kmem_cache_free(file_cache, file);
            return NULL;
        }
    }
    
    /* Handle O_TRUNC */
    if ((flags & O_TRUNC) && (flags & O_WRONLY || flags & O_RDWR)) {
        if (file->inode->ops && file->inode->ops->truncate) {
            file->inode->ops->truncate(file->inode, 0);
        }
    }
    
    /* Handle O_APPEND */
    if (flags & O_APPEND) {
        file->pos = file->inode->size;
    }
    
    return file;
}

/* Close File */
int vfs_close(file_t *file)
{
    if (!file) return NEXUS_EINVAL;
    
    if (!atomic_dec_and_test(&file->refcount)) {
        return NEXUS_OK;
    }
    
    /* Call Close */
    if (file->ops && file->ops->close) {
        file->ops->close(file);
    }
    
    vfs_inode_put(file->inode);
    vfs_dentry_put(file->dentry);
    kmem_cache_free(file_cache, file);
    
    return NEXUS_OK;
}

/* Read File */
ssize_t vfs_read(file_t *file, void *buf, size_t count)
{
    if (!file || !buf) return -NEXUS_EINVAL;
    if (!file->ops || !file->ops->read) return -NEXUS_ENOTSUPP;
    
    spin_lock(&file->lock);
    ssize_t ret = file->ops->read(file, buf, count, &file->pos);
    spin_unlock(&file->lock);
    
    return ret;
}

/* Write File */
ssize_t vfs_write(file_t *file, const void *buf, size_t count)
{
    if (!file || !buf) return -NEXUS_EINVAL;
    if (!file->ops || !file->ops->write) return -NEXUS_ENOTSUPP;
    
    spin_lock(&file->lock);
    ssize_t ret = file->ops->write(file, buf, count, &file->pos);
    spin_unlock(&file->lock);
    
    return ret;
}

/* Seek File */
off_t vfs_seek(file_t *file, off_t offset, int whence)
{
    if (!file) return -NEXUS_EINVAL;
    
    spin_lock(&file->lock);
    
    off_t new_pos;
    
    switch (whence) {
    case SEEK_SET:
        new_pos = offset;
        break;
    case SEEK_CUR:
        new_pos = file->pos + offset;
        break;
    case SEEK_END:
        new_pos = file->inode->size + offset;
        break;
    default:
        spin_unlock(&file->lock);
        return -NEXUS_EINVAL;
    }
    
    if (new_pos < 0) {
        spin_unlock(&file->lock);
        return -NEXUS_EINVAL;
    }
    
    file->pos = new_pos;
    
    spin_unlock(&file->lock);
    
    return new_pos;
}

/* Get File Reference */
void vfs_file_get(file_t *file)
{
    atomic_inc(&file->refcount);
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                      DIRECTORY OPERATIONS                                 */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Create Directory */
int vfs_mkdir(const char *path, mode_t mode)
{
    char *parent_path = strdup(path);
    char *name = strrchr(parent_path, '/');
    
    if (name) {
        *name = '\0';
        name++;
    } else {
        name = parent_path;
        parent_path = ".";
    }
    
    vfs_dentry_t *parent = vfs_path_resolve(parent_path, NULL);
    if (!parent || !parent->inode) {
        return NEXUS_ENOENT;
    }
    
    if (!parent->inode->ops || !parent->inode->ops->mkdir) {
        vfs_dentry_put(parent);
        return NEXUS_ENOTSUPP;
    }
    
    vfs_dentry_t *new_dentry = dentry_alloc(name, parent);
    int ret = parent->inode->ops->mkdir(parent->inode, new_dentry, mode);
    
    if (ret != 0) {
        vfs_dentry_put(new_dentry);
    }
    
    vfs_dentry_put(parent);
    return ret;
}

/* Remove Directory */
int vfs_rmdir(const char *path)
{
    vfs_dentry_t *dentry = vfs_path_resolve(path, NULL);
    if (!dentry) return NEXUS_ENOENT;
    
    if (dentry->inode->type != VFS_TYPE_DIR) {
        vfs_dentry_put(dentry);
        return NEXUS_ENOTDIR;
    }
    
    /* Check Empty */
    if (!list_empty(&dentry->children)) {
        vfs_dentry_put(dentry);
        return NEXUS_ENOTEMPTY;
    }
    
    vfs_dentry_t *parent = dentry->parent;
    if (!parent || !parent->inode->ops || !parent->inode->ops->rmdir) {
        vfs_dentry_put(dentry);
        return NEXUS_ENOTSUPP;
    }
    
    int ret = parent->inode->ops->rmdir(parent->inode, dentry);
    
    vfs_dentry_put(dentry);
    return ret;
}

/* Unlink File */
int vfs_unlink(const char *path)
{
    vfs_dentry_t *dentry = vfs_path_resolve(path, NULL);
    if (!dentry) return NEXUS_ENOENT;
    
    if (dentry->inode->type == VFS_TYPE_DIR) {
        vfs_dentry_put(dentry);
        return NEXUS_EISDIR;
    }
    
    vfs_dentry_t *parent = dentry->parent;
    if (!parent || !parent->inode->ops || !parent->inode->ops->unlink) {
        vfs_dentry_put(dentry);
        return NEXUS_ENOTSUPP;
    }
    
    int ret = parent->inode->ops->unlink(parent->inode, dentry);
    
    vfs_dentry_put(dentry);
    return ret;
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                       MOUNT OPERATIONS                                    */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Register File System */
int vfs_register_fs(fs_type_t *fs)
{
    spin_lock(&fs_types_lock);
    list_add_tail(&fs->list, &fs_types);
    spin_unlock(&fs_types_lock);
    
    pr_info("VFS: Registered filesystem '%s'\n", fs->name);
    return NEXUS_OK;
}

/* Find File System */
static fs_type_t *find_fs_type(const char *name)
{
    fs_type_t *fs;
    
    spin_lock(&fs_types_lock);
    list_for_each_entry(fs, &fs_types, list) {
        if (strcmp(fs->name, name) == 0) {
            spin_unlock(&fs_types_lock);
            return fs;
        }
    }
    spin_unlock(&fs_types_lock);
    
    return NULL;
}

/* Mount File System */
int vfs_mount(const char *source, const char *target, 
              const char *fstype, u32 flags, const void *data)
{
    /* Find FS Type */
    fs_type_t *fs = find_fs_type(fstype);
    if (!fs) {
        pr_err("VFS: Unknown filesystem type '%s'\n", fstype);
        return NEXUS_ENOENT;
    }
    
    /* Get Mount Point */
    vfs_dentry_t *mountpoint = vfs_path_resolve(target, NULL);
    if (!mountpoint) {
        pr_err("VFS: Mount point '%s' not found\n", target);
        return NEXUS_ENOENT;
    }
    
    /* Call FS Mount */
    superblock_t *sb = fs->mount(fs, source, data);
    if (!sb) {
        vfs_dentry_put(mountpoint);
        return NEXUS_ERROR;
    }
    
    /* Create Mount */
    mount_t *mnt = kzalloc(sizeof(mount_t));
    mnt->sb = sb;
    mnt->mountpoint = mountpoint;
    mnt->root = sb->root_dentry;
    mnt->device = source ? strdup(source) : NULL;
    mnt->mount_path = strdup(target);
    mnt->flags = flags;
    atomic_set(&mnt->refcount, 1);
    
    /* Mark Mount Point */
    mountpoint->flags |= DENTRY_MOUNTED;
    mountpoint->mount = mnt;
    
    /* Add to Lists */
    write_lock(&mount_lock);
    list_add_tail(&mnt->list, &mount_list);
    list_add_tail(&mnt->sb_list, &sb->mounts);
    write_unlock(&mount_lock);
    
    pr_info("VFS: Mounted '%s' on '%s' type '%s'\n", 
            source ? source : "none", target, fstype);
    
    return NEXUS_OK;
}

/* Unmount File System */
int vfs_umount(const char *target)
{
    vfs_dentry_t *mountpoint = vfs_path_resolve(target, NULL);
    if (!mountpoint) return NEXUS_ENOENT;
    
    if (!(mountpoint->flags & DENTRY_MOUNTED)) {
        vfs_dentry_put(mountpoint);
        return NEXUS_EINVAL;
    }
    
    mount_t *mnt = mountpoint->mount;
    
    /* Remove from Lists */
    write_lock(&mount_lock);
    list_del(&mnt->list);
    list_del(&mnt->sb_list);
    write_unlock(&mount_lock);
    
    /* Clear Mount Point */
    mountpoint->flags &= ~DENTRY_MOUNTED;
    mountpoint->mount = NULL;
    
    /* Unmount FS */
    if (mnt->sb->fs_type->unmount) {
        mnt->sb->fs_type->unmount(mnt->sb);
    }
    
    if (mnt->device) kfree(mnt->device);
    kfree(mnt->mount_path);
    kfree(mnt);
    
    vfs_dentry_put(mountpoint);
    
    pr_info("VFS: Unmounted '%s'\n", target);
    
    return NEXUS_OK;
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                         VFS INITIALIZATION                                */
/*===========================================================================*/

int vfs_init(void)
{
    pr_info("Initializing VFS...\n");
    
    /* Initialize Hash Tables */
    for (int i = 0; i < DENTRY_HASH_SIZE; i++) {
        INIT_LIST_HEAD(&dentry_hashtable[i]);
    }
    
    spin_lock_init(&dentry_hash_lock);
    spin_lock_init(&fs_types_lock);
    rwlock_init(&mount_lock);
    
    /* Create Caches */
    inode_cache = kmem_cache_create("inode_cache", sizeof(vfs_inode_t), 0);
    dentry_cache = kmem_cache_create("dentry_cache", sizeof(vfs_dentry_t), 0);
    file_cache = kmem_cache_create("file_cache", sizeof(file_t), 0);
    
    /* Create Root Dentry */
    vfs_root = dentry_alloc("/", NULL);
    vfs_root->parent = vfs_root;
    
    pr_info("VFS initialized.\n");
    return NEXUS_OK;
}

/* Mount Root Filesystem */
int mount_root(void)
{
    pr_info("Mounting root filesystem...\n");
    
    /* Try tmpfs first as root */
    int ret = vfs_mount(NULL, "/", "tmpfs", 0, NULL);
    if (ret != 0) {
        pr_err("Failed to mount root filesystem!\n");
        return ret;
    }
    
    /* Create Essential Directories */
    vfs_mkdir("/dev", 0755);
    vfs_mkdir("/proc", 0555);
    vfs_mkdir("/sys", 0555);
    vfs_mkdir("/tmp", 01777);
    vfs_mkdir("/var", 0755);
    vfs_mkdir("/etc", 0755);
    vfs_mkdir("/bin", 0755);
    vfs_mkdir("/lib", 0755);
    vfs_mkdir("/usr", 0755);
    vfs_mkdir("/home", 0755);
    
    /* Mount devfs */
    vfs_mount(NULL, "/dev", "devfs", 0, NULL);
    
    /* Mount procfs */
    vfs_mount(NULL, "/proc", "procfs", 0, NULL);
    
    /* Mount sysfs */
    vfs_mount(NULL, "/sys", "sysfs", 0, NULL);
    
    pr_info("Root filesystem mounted.\n");
    return NEXUS_OK;
}
```

---

# 9. NETWORK STACK

## 9.1 Network Core (net/core/network.c)

```c
/*
 * NEXUS OS - Network Stack Core
 * net/core/network.c
 */

#include <kernel.h>
#include <net/network.h>
#include <net/socket.h>
#include <net/skbuff.h>

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                       NETWORK STRUCTURES                                  */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Ethernet Header */
typedef struct eth_header {
    u8 dest[6];
    u8 src[6];
    u16 type;
} __packed eth_header_t;

#define ETH_TYPE_IP     0x0800
#define ETH_TYPE_ARP    0x0806
#define ETH_TYPE_IPV6   0x86DD

/* IP Header */
typedef struct ip_header {
    u8 version_ihl;
    u8 tos;
    u16 total_length;
    u16 id;
    u16 flags_fragment;
    u8 ttl;
    u8 protocol;
    u16 checksum;
    u32 src_addr;
    u32 dst_addr;
} __packed ip_header_t;

#define IP_PROTO_ICMP   1
#define IP_PROTO_TCP    6
#define IP_PROTO_UDP    17

/* TCP Header */
typedef struct tcp_header {
    u16 src_port;
    u16 dst_port;
    u32 seq_num;
    u32 ack_num;
    u8 data_offset;
    u8 flags;
    u16 window;
    u16 checksum;
    u16 urgent_ptr;
} __packed tcp_header_t;

#define TCP_FLAG_FIN    0x01
#define TCP_FLAG_SYN    0x02
#define TCP_FLAG_RST    0x04
#define TCP_FLAG_PSH    0x08
#define TCP_FLAG_ACK    0x10
#define TCP_FLAG_URG    0x20

/* UDP Header */
typedef struct udp_header {
    u16 src_port;
    u16 dst_port;
    u16 length;
    u16 checksum;
} __packed udp_header_t;

/* Socket Buffer */
typedef struct sk_buff {
    struct list_head list;
    
    /* Data Pointers */
    u8 *head;
    u8 *data;
    u8 *tail;
    u8 *end;
    
    u32 len;
    u32 data_len;
    
    /* Protocol Headers */
    union {
        eth_header_t *eth;
        void *raw;
    } mac;
    
    union {
        ip_header_t *ip;
        void *raw;
    } network;
    
    union {
        tcp_header_t *tcp;
        udp_header_t *udp;
        void *raw;
    } transport;
    
    /* Network Device */
    struct net_device *dev;
    
    /* Socket */
    struct socket *sk;
    
    /* Routing */
    u32 mark;
    u32 priority;
    
    /* Timestamps */
    u64 tstamp;
    
    /* Reference Count */
    atomic_t refcount;
    
} sk_buff_t;

/* Network Device */
typedef struct net_device {
    char name[16];
    u32 index;
    
    /* Addresses */
    u8 mac_addr[6];
    u32 ip_addr;
    u32 netmask;
    u32 gateway;
    
    /* State */
    u32 flags;
    #define NETDEV_UP       BIT(0)
    #define NETDEV_RUNNING  BIT(1)
    #define NETDEV_PROMISC  BIT(2)
    
    u32 mtu;
    
    /* Operations */
    struct net_device_ops *ops;
    
    /* TX/RX Queues */
    struct list_head tx_queue;
    struct list_head rx_queue;
    spinlock_t tx_lock;
    spinlock_t rx_lock;
    
    /* Statistics */
    u64 rx_packets;
    u64 tx_packets;
    u64 rx_bytes;
    u64 tx_bytes;
    u64 rx_errors;
    u64 tx_errors;
    u64 rx_dropped;
    u64 tx_dropped;
    
    /* Driver Data */
    void *priv;
    
    /* List */
    struct list_head list;
    
} net_device_t;

/* Network Device Operations */
typedef struct net_device_ops {
    int (*open)(net_device_t *dev);
    int (*stop)(net_device_t *dev);
    int (*start_xmit)(sk_buff_t *skb, net_device_t *dev);
    int (*set_mac_address)(net_device_t *dev, void *addr);
    int (*set_rx_mode)(net_device_t *dev);
    int (*ioctl)(net_device_t *dev, int cmd, void *arg);
} net_device_ops_t;

/* Socket Address */
typedef struct sockaddr {
    u16 family;
    char data[14];
} sockaddr_t;

typedef struct sockaddr_in {
    u16 family;
    u16 port;
    u32 addr;
    u8 zero[8];
} sockaddr_in_t;

/* Socket */
typedef struct socket {
    int type;
    int protocol;
    int state;
    
    #define SOCK_STATE_UNCONNECTED  0
    #define SOCK_STATE_CONNECTING   1
    #define SOCK_STATE_CONNECTED    2
    #define SOCK_STATE_LISTENING    3
    #define SOCK_STATE_CLOSING      4
    
    /* Addresses */
    sockaddr_in_t local_addr;
    sockaddr_in_t remote_addr;
    
    /* Buffers */
    struct list_head recv_queue;
    struct list_head send_queue;
    size_t recv_buf_size;
    size_t send_buf_size;
    
    /* TCP State */
    struct {
        u32 seq;
        u32 ack;
        u32 window;
        u32 mss;
        int state;
        
        #define TCP_STATE_CLOSED        0
        #define TCP_STATE_LISTEN        1
        #define TCP_STATE_SYN_SENT      2
        #define TCP_STATE_SYN_RECEIVED  3
        #define TCP_STATE_ESTABLISHED   4
        #define TCP_STATE_FIN_WAIT_1    5
        #define TCP_STATE_FIN_WAIT_2    6
        #define TCP_STATE_CLOSE_WAIT    7
        #define TCP_STATE_CLOSING       8
        #define TCP_STATE_LAST_ACK      9
        #define TCP_STATE_TIME_WAIT     10
        
        /* Retransmission */
        timer_t retransmit_timer;
        struct list_head retransmit_queue;
        
    } tcp;
    
    /* Wait Queues */
    wait_queue_t recv_wait;
    wait_queue_t send_wait;
    wait_queue_t accept_wait;
    
    /* Accept Queue */
    struct list_head accept_queue;
    int backlog;
    int pending_connections;
    
    /* Owner */
    process_t *owner;
    
    /* Operations */
    struct socket_ops *ops;
    
    /* Lock */
    spinlock_t lock;
    
    /* Reference Count */
    atomic_t refcount;
    
} socket_t;

/* Socket Operations */
typedef struct socket_ops {
    int (*connect)(socket_t *sk, sockaddr_t *addr, int addrlen);
    int (*disconnect)(socket_t *sk);
    int (*accept)(socket_t *sk, socket_t **newsock, sockaddr_t *addr);
    int (*listen)(socket_t *sk, int backlog);
    int (*bind)(socket_t *sk, sockaddr_t *addr, int addrlen);
    ssize_t (*sendmsg)(socket_t *sk, const void *buf, size_t len, int flags);
    ssize_t (*recvmsg)(socket_t *sk, void *buf, size_t len, int flags);
    int (*shutdown)(socket_t *sk, int how);
    int (*setsockopt)(socket_t *sk, int level, int optname, 
                      const void *optval, int optlen);
    int (*getsockopt)(socket_t *sk, int level, int optname,
                      void *optval, int *optlen);
} socket_ops_t;

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                          GLOBAL STATE                                     */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Network Devices */
static LIST_HEAD(netdev_list);
static spinlock_t netdev_lock = {0};
static u32 netdev_count = 0;

/* Routing Table */
typedef struct route_entry {
    u32 dest;
    u32 netmask;
    u32 gateway;
    net_device_t *dev;
    u32 metric;
    struct list_head list;
} route_entry_t;

static LIST_HEAD(route_table);
static rwlock_t route_lock = {0};

/* ARP Cache */
typedef struct arp_entry {
    u32 ip_addr;
    u8 mac_addr[6];
    u64 timestamp;
    struct list_head list;
} arp_entry_t;

static LIST_HEAD(arp_cache);
static spinlock_t arp_lock = {0};

/* TCP/UDP Port Binding */
typedef struct port_binding {
    u16 port;
    socket_t *socket;
    struct rb_node rb_node;
} port_binding_t;

static struct rb_root tcp_ports = { NULL };
static struct rb_root udp_ports = { NULL };
static spinlock_t port_lock = {0};

/* Socket Buffer Pool */
static struct kmem_cache *skb_cache = NULL;

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                       SOCKET BUFFER (SKB)                                 */
/*===========================================================================*/

sk_buff_t *skb_alloc(u32 size)
{
    sk_buff_t *skb = kmem_cache_alloc(skb_cache);
    if (!skb) return NULL;
    
    memset(skb, 0, sizeof(sk_buff_t));
    
    /* Allocate Data Buffer */
    skb->head = kmalloc(size + 256);  /* Extra for headers */
    if (!skb->head) {
        kmem_cache_free(skb_cache, skb);
        return NULL;
    }
    
    skb->data = skb->head + 128;  /* Leave room for headers */
    skb->tail = skb->data;
    skb->end = skb->head + size + 256;
    skb->len = 0;
    
    INIT_LIST_HEAD(&skb->list);
    atomic_set(&skb->refcount, 1);
    
    return skb;
}

void skb_free(sk_buff_t *skb)
{
    if (!skb) return;
    
    if (atomic_dec_and_test(&skb->refcount)) {
        kfree(skb->head);
        kmem_cache_free(skb_cache, skb);
    }
}

u8 *skb_push(sk_buff_t *skb, u32 len)
{
    skb->data -= len;
    skb->len += len;
    return skb->data;
}

u8 *skb_pull(sk_buff_t *skb, u32 len)
{
    skb->data += len;
    skb->len -= len;
    return skb->data;
}

u8 *skb_put(sk_buff_t *skb, u32 len)
{
    u8 *tmp = skb->tail;
    skb->tail += len;
    skb->len += len;
    return tmp;
}

void skb_reserve(sk_buff_t *skb, u32 len)
{
    skb->data += len;
    skb->tail += len;
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                       NETWORK DEVICE                                      */
/*===========================================================================*/

net_device_t *netdev_alloc(const char *name, struct net_device_ops *ops)
{
    net_device_t *dev = kzalloc(sizeof(net_device_t));
    if (!dev) return NULL;
    
    strncpy(dev->name, name, sizeof(dev->name) - 1);
    dev->ops = ops;
    dev->mtu = 1500;
    
    INIT_LIST_HEAD(&dev->tx_queue);
    INIT_LIST_HEAD(&dev->rx_queue);
    spin_lock_init(&dev->tx_lock);
    spin_lock_init(&dev->rx_lock);
    INIT_LIST_HEAD(&dev->list);
    
    return dev;
}

int netdev_register(net_device_t *dev)
{
    spin_lock(&netdev_lock);
    dev->index = netdev_count++;
    list_add_tail(&dev->list, &netdev_list);
    spin_unlock(&netdev_lock);
    
    pr_info("NET: Registered device '%s' (index %d)\n", dev->name, dev->index);
    return NEXUS_OK;
}

void netdev_unregister(net_device_t *dev)
{
    spin_lock(&netdev_lock);
    list_del(&dev->list);
    spin_unlock(&netdev_lock);
}

net_device_t *netdev_get_by_name(const char *name)
{
    net_device_t *dev;
    
    spin_lock(&netdev_lock);
    list_for_each_entry(dev, &netdev_list, list) {
        if (strcmp(dev->name, name) == 0) {
            spin_unlock(&netdev_lock);
            return dev;
        }
    }
    spin_unlock(&netdev_lock);
    
    return NULL;
}

int netdev_open(net_device_t *dev)
{
    if (dev->ops && dev->ops->open) {
        int ret = dev->ops->open(dev);
        if (ret == 0) {
            dev->flags |= NETDEV_UP | NETDEV_RUNNING;
        }
        return ret;
    }
    return NEXUS_OK;
}

int netdev_transmit(sk_buff_t *skb, net_device_t *dev)
{
    if (!dev || !(dev->flags & NETDEV_RUNNING)) {
        skb_free(skb);
        return NEXUS_ENODEV;
    }
    
    if (dev->ops && dev->ops->start_xmit) {
        int ret = dev->ops->start_xmit(skb, dev);
        if (ret == 0) {
            dev->tx_packets++;
            dev->tx_bytes += skb->len;
        } else {
            dev->tx_errors++;
        }
        return ret;
    }
    
    skb_free(skb);
    return NEXUS_ENOTSUPP;
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                        PACKET RECEPTION                                   */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Called by Driver on Packet Reception */
void netif_rx(sk_buff_t *skb)
{
    net_device_t *dev = skb->dev;
    
    dev->rx_packets++;
    dev->rx_bytes += skb->len;
    
    /* Process Ethernet Header */
    eth_header_t *eth = (eth_header_t *)skb->data;
    skb->mac.eth = eth;
    skb_pull(skb, sizeof(eth_header_t));
    
    u16 ethertype = ntohs(eth->type);
    
    switch (ethertype) {
    case ETH_TYPE_IP:
        ip_rcv(skb);
        break;
    case ETH_TYPE_ARP:
        arp_rcv(skb);
        break;
    case ETH_TYPE_IPV6:
        /* TODO: IPv6 */
        skb_free(skb);
        break;
    default:
        skb_free(skb);
        break;
    }
}

/* IP Receive */
void ip_rcv(sk_buff_t *skb)
{
    ip_header_t *ip = (ip_header_t *)skb->data;
    skb->network.ip = ip;
    
    /* Validate Checksum */
    if (ip_checksum(ip, sizeof(ip_header_t)) != 0) {
        skb_free(skb);
        return;
    }
    
    /* Check Destination */
    net_device_t *dev = skb->dev;
    if (ip->dst_addr != dev->ip_addr && 
        ip->dst_addr != 0xFFFFFFFF &&   /*
# NEXUS OS - Continued Implementation (Part 2)

## 9.1 Network Core - Continued (net/core/network.c)

```c
/* IP Receive - Continued */
void ip_rcv(sk_buff_t *skb)
{
    ip_header_t *ip = (ip_header_t *)skb->data;
    skb->network.ip = ip;
    
    /* Validate Checksum */
    if (ip_checksum(ip, sizeof(ip_header_t)) != 0) {
        skb_free(skb);
        return;
    }
    
    /* Check Destination */
    net_device_t *dev = skb->dev;
    if (ip->dst_addr != dev->ip_addr && 
        ip->dst_addr != 0xFFFFFFFF &&       /* Broadcast */
        (ip->dst_addr & 0xF0000000) != 0xE0000000) {  /* Multicast */
        /* Not for us - forward if routing enabled */
        skb_free(skb);
        return;
    }
    
    /* Get Header Length */
    u8 ihl = (ip->version_ihl & 0x0F) * 4;
    skb_pull(skb, ihl);
    
    /* Dispatch to Protocol Handler */
    switch (ip->protocol) {
    case IP_PROTO_ICMP:
        icmp_rcv(skb);
        break;
    case IP_PROTO_TCP:
        tcp_rcv(skb);
        break;
    case IP_PROTO_UDP:
        udp_rcv(skb);
        break;
    default:
        skb_free(skb);
        break;
    }
}

/* Calculate IP Checksum */
static u16 ip_checksum(void *data, u32 len)
{
    u32 sum = 0;
    u16 *ptr = (u16 *)data;
    
    while (len > 1) {
        sum += *ptr++;
        len -= 2;
    }
    
    if (len == 1) {
        sum += *(u8 *)ptr;
    }
    
    while (sum >> 16) {
        sum = (sum & 0xFFFF) + (sum >> 16);
    }
    
    return ~sum;
}

/* ICMP Receive */
void icmp_rcv(sk_buff_t *skb)
{
    typedef struct {
        u8 type;
        u8 code;
        u16 checksum;
        u16 id;
        u16 seq;
    } __packed icmp_header_t;
    
    icmp_header_t *icmp = (icmp_header_t *)skb->data;
    
    #define ICMP_ECHO_REQUEST  8
    #define ICMP_ECHO_REPLY    0
    
    if (icmp->type == ICMP_ECHO_REQUEST) {
        /* Send Echo Reply */
        icmp_send_reply(skb);
    } else {
        skb_free(skb);
    }
}

/* Send ICMP Reply */
static void icmp_send_reply(sk_buff_t *skb)
{
    ip_header_t *orig_ip = skb->network.ip;
    
    /* Swap Source and Dest */
    u32 tmp = orig_ip->src_addr;
    orig_ip->src_addr = orig_ip->dst_addr;
    orig_ip->dst_addr = tmp;
    
    /* Change ICMP Type to Reply */
    u8 *icmp_type = skb->data;
    *icmp_type = ICMP_ECHO_REPLY;
    
    /* Recalculate Checksums */
    u16 *icmp_checksum = (u16 *)(skb->data + 2);
    *icmp_checksum = 0;
    *icmp_checksum = ip_checksum(skb->data, skb->len);
    
    orig_ip->checksum = 0;
    orig_ip->checksum = ip_checksum(orig_ip, sizeof(ip_header_t));
    
    /* Send */
    skb_push(skb, sizeof(ip_header_t));
    ip_output(skb);
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                            TCP STACK                                      */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* TCP Receive */
void tcp_rcv(sk_buff_t *skb)
{
    tcp_header_t *tcp = (tcp_header_t *)skb->data;
    skb->transport.tcp = tcp;
    
    u16 src_port = ntohs(tcp->src_port);
    u16 dst_port = ntohs(tcp->dst_port);
    
    /* Find Socket */
    socket_t *sk = tcp_find_socket(skb->network.ip->dst_addr, dst_port,
                                    skb->network.ip->src_addr, src_port);
    
    if (!sk) {
        /* No socket - send RST */
        tcp_send_rst(skb);
        skb_free(skb);
        return;
    }
    
    skb->sk = sk;
    
    /* Process Based on State */
    spin_lock(&sk->lock);
    
    switch (sk->tcp.state) {
    case TCP_STATE_LISTEN:
        tcp_rcv_listen(sk, skb);
        break;
    case TCP_STATE_SYN_SENT:
        tcp_rcv_syn_sent(sk, skb);
        break;
    case TCP_STATE_SYN_RECEIVED:
        tcp_rcv_syn_received(sk, skb);
        break;
    case TCP_STATE_ESTABLISHED:
        tcp_rcv_established(sk, skb);
        break;
    case TCP_STATE_FIN_WAIT_1:
    case TCP_STATE_FIN_WAIT_2:
    case TCP_STATE_CLOSE_WAIT:
    case TCP_STATE_CLOSING:
    case TCP_STATE_LAST_ACK:
    case TCP_STATE_TIME_WAIT:
        tcp_rcv_closing(sk, skb);
        break;
    default:
        skb_free(skb);
        break;
    }
    
    spin_unlock(&sk->lock);
}

/* TCP Receive in LISTEN State */
static void tcp_rcv_listen(socket_t *sk, sk_buff_t *skb)
{
    tcp_header_t *tcp = skb->transport.tcp;
    
    if (!(tcp->flags & TCP_FLAG_SYN)) {
        skb_free(skb);
        return;
    }
    
    /* Create New Socket for Connection */
    socket_t *newsk = tcp_create_child(sk);
    if (!newsk) {
        skb_free(skb);
        return;
    }
    
    /* Set Remote Address */
    newsk->remote_addr.addr = skb->network.ip->src_addr;
    newsk->remote_addr.port = ntohs(tcp->src_port);
    
    /* Initialize TCP State */
    newsk->tcp.ack = ntohl(tcp->seq_num) + 1;
    newsk->tcp.seq = get_random_u32();
    newsk->tcp.state = TCP_STATE_SYN_RECEIVED;
    newsk->tcp.window = ntohs(tcp->window);
    
    /* Send SYN+ACK */
    tcp_send_synack(newsk);
    
    skb_free(skb);
}

/* TCP Receive in ESTABLISHED State */
static void tcp_rcv_established(socket_t *sk, sk_buff_t *skb)
{
    tcp_header_t *tcp = skb->transport.tcp;
    u32 seq = ntohl(tcp->seq_num);
    u32 ack = ntohl(tcp->ack_num);
    u8 data_offset = (tcp->data_offset >> 4) * 4;
    u32 data_len = skb->len - data_offset;
    
    /* Check Sequence Number */
    if (seq != sk->tcp.ack) {
        /* Out of order - handle or drop */
        if (seq > sk->tcp.ack) {
            /* Future packet - queue */
            tcp_queue_ooo(sk, skb);
            return;
        } else {
            /* Old packet - drop and ACK */
            tcp_send_ack(sk);
            skb_free(skb);
            return;
        }
    }
    
    /* Process ACK */
    if (tcp->flags & TCP_FLAG_ACK) {
        tcp_process_ack(sk, ack);
    }
    
    /* Process Data */
    if (data_len > 0) {
        skb_pull(skb, data_offset);
        
        /* Add to Receive Queue */
        list_add_tail(&skb->list, &sk->recv_queue);
        sk->tcp.ack += data_len;
        
        /* Wake Up Reader */
        wake_up(&sk->recv_wait);
        
        /* Send ACK */
        tcp_send_ack(sk);
    } else {
        skb_free(skb);
    }
    
    /* Process FIN */
    if (tcp->flags & TCP_FLAG_FIN) {
        sk->tcp.ack++;
        sk->tcp.state = TCP_STATE_CLOSE_WAIT;
        tcp_send_ack(sk);
        wake_up(&sk->recv_wait);
    }
}

/* TCP Connect */
int tcp_connect(socket_t *sk, sockaddr_in_t *addr)
{
    spin_lock(&sk->lock);
    
    if (sk->tcp.state != TCP_STATE_CLOSED) {
        spin_unlock(&sk->lock);
        return NEXUS_EINVAL;
    }
    
    /* Set Remote Address */
    sk->remote_addr = *addr;
    
    /* Allocate Local Port if Not Bound */
    if (sk->local_addr.port == 0) {
        sk->local_addr.port = tcp_alloc_port();
    }
    
    /* Initialize Sequence Number */
    sk->tcp.seq = get_random_u32();
    sk->tcp.state = TCP_STATE_SYN_SENT;
    
    spin_unlock(&sk->lock);
    
    /* Send SYN */
    tcp_send_syn(sk);
    
    /* Wait for Connection */
    int ret = wait_event_timeout(&sk->send_wait,
                                  sk->tcp.state == TCP_STATE_ESTABLISHED ||
                                  sk->tcp.state == TCP_STATE_CLOSED,
                                  30000);  /* 30 second timeout */
    
    if (ret == 0) {
        /* Timeout */
        spin_lock(&sk->lock);
        sk->tcp.state = TCP_STATE_CLOSED;
        spin_unlock(&sk->lock);
        return NEXUS_ETIMEDOUT;
    }
    
    if (sk->tcp.state != TCP_STATE_ESTABLISHED) {
        return NEXUS_ECONNREFUSED;
    }
    
    return NEXUS_OK;
}

/* TCP Send */
ssize_t tcp_send(socket_t *sk, const void *buf, size_t len, int flags)
{
    if (sk->tcp.state != TCP_STATE_ESTABLISHED) {
        return -NEXUS_ENOTCONN;
    }
    
    size_t sent = 0;
    const u8 *data = buf;
    
    while (sent < len) {
        /* Calculate Segment Size */
        size_t segment_size = MIN(len - sent, sk->tcp.mss);
        
        /* Wait for Window Space */
        while (tcp_send_window(sk) < segment_size) {
            if (flags & MSG_DONTWAIT) {
                if (sent > 0) return sent;
                return -NEXUS_EAGAIN;
            }
            
            int ret = wait_event_interruptible(&sk->send_wait,
                                               tcp_send_window(sk) >= segment_size);
            if (ret != 0) {
                if (sent > 0) return sent;
                return -NEXUS_EINTR;
            }
        }
        
        /* Build and Send Segment */
        sk_buff_t *skb = tcp_build_segment(sk, data + sent, segment_size,
                                            TCP_FLAG_ACK | TCP_FLAG_PSH);
        if (!skb) {
            if (sent > 0) return sent;
            return -NEXUS_ENOMEM;
        }
        
        /* Add to Retransmit Queue */
        tcp_add_to_retransmit(sk, skb);
        
        /* Send */
        ip_output(skb);
        
        sent += segment_size;
        sk->tcp.seq += segment_size;
    }
    
    return sent;
}

/* TCP Receive */
ssize_t tcp_recv(socket_t *sk, void *buf, size_t len, int flags)
{
    size_t received = 0;
    u8 *data = buf;
    
    spin_lock(&sk->lock);
    
    while (received < len) {
        /* Check for Data */
        if (list_empty(&sk->recv_queue)) {
            if (sk->tcp.state != TCP_STATE_ESTABLISHED &&
                sk->tcp.state != TCP_STATE_FIN_WAIT_1 &&
                sk->tcp.state != TCP_STATE_FIN_WAIT_2) {
                /* Connection Closed */
                spin_unlock(&sk->lock);
                return received > 0 ? received : 0;
            }
            
            if (received > 0) {
                spin_unlock(&sk->lock);
                return received;
            }
            
            if (flags & MSG_DONTWAIT) {
                spin_unlock(&sk->lock);
                return -NEXUS_EAGAIN;
            }
            
            /* Wait for Data */
            spin_unlock(&sk->lock);
            int ret = wait_event_interruptible(&sk->recv_wait,
                                               !list_empty(&sk->recv_queue) ||
                                               sk->tcp.state == TCP_STATE_CLOSE_WAIT);
            if (ret != 0) {
                return -NEXUS_EINTR;
            }
            spin_lock(&sk->lock);
            continue;
        }
        
        /* Get Data from Queue */
        sk_buff_t *skb = list_first_entry(&sk->recv_queue, sk_buff_t, list);
        size_t copy = MIN(len - received, skb->len);
        
        memcpy(data + received, skb->data, copy);
        received += copy;
        
        if (copy < skb->len) {
            skb_pull(skb, copy);
        } else {
            list_del(&skb->list);
            skb_free(skb);
        }
    }
    
    spin_unlock(&sk->lock);
    return received;
}

/* TCP Send SYN */
static void tcp_send_syn(socket_t *sk)
{
    sk_buff_t *skb = tcp_build_segment(sk, NULL, 0, TCP_FLAG_SYN);
    if (skb) {
        ip_output(skb);
    }
}

/* TCP Send SYN+ACK */
static void tcp_send_synack(socket_t *sk)
{
    sk_buff_t *skb = tcp_build_segment(sk, NULL, 0, TCP_FLAG_SYN | TCP_FLAG_ACK);
    if (skb) {
        ip_output(skb);
    }
}

/* TCP Send ACK */
static void tcp_send_ack(socket_t *sk)
{
    sk_buff_t *skb = tcp_build_segment(sk, NULL, 0, TCP_FLAG_ACK);
    if (skb) {
        ip_output(skb);
    }
}

/* Build TCP Segment */
static sk_buff_t *tcp_build_segment(socket_t *sk, const void *data, 
                                     size_t len, u8 flags)
{
    sk_buff_t *skb = skb_alloc(len + 128);
    if (!skb) return NULL;
    
    skb_reserve(skb, 64);  /* Room for headers */
    
    /* Add Data */
    if (data && len > 0) {
        memcpy(skb_put(skb, len), data, len);
    }
    
    /* Add TCP Header */
    tcp_header_t *tcp = (tcp_header_t *)skb_push(skb, sizeof(tcp_header_t));
    tcp->src_port = htons(sk->local_addr.port);
    tcp->dst_port = htons(sk->remote_addr.port);
    tcp->seq_num = htonl(sk->tcp.seq);
    tcp->ack_num = htonl(sk->tcp.ack);
    tcp->data_offset = (sizeof(tcp_header_t) / 4) << 4;
    tcp->flags = flags;
    tcp->window = htons(sk->tcp.window);
    tcp->urgent_ptr = 0;
    
    /* Calculate Checksum */
    tcp->checksum = 0;
    tcp->checksum = tcp_checksum(sk, tcp, sizeof(tcp_header_t) + len);
    
    skb->transport.tcp = tcp;
    
    return skb;
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                            UDP STACK                                      */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* UDP Receive */
void udp_rcv(sk_buff_t *skb)
{
    udp_header_t *udp = (udp_header_t *)skb->data;
    skb->transport.udp = udp;
    
    u16 dst_port = ntohs(udp->dst_port);
    
    /* Find Socket */
    socket_t *sk = udp_find_socket(skb->network.ip->dst_addr, dst_port);
    
    if (!sk) {
        /* No socket - send ICMP Port Unreachable */
        skb_free(skb);
        return;
    }
    
    /* Remove UDP Header */
    skb_pull(skb, sizeof(udp_header_t));
    
    /* Add to Receive Queue */
    spin_lock(&sk->lock);
    list_add_tail(&skb->list, &sk->recv_queue);
    spin_unlock(&sk->lock);
    
    /* Wake Up Reader */
    wake_up(&sk->recv_wait);
}

/* UDP Send */
ssize_t udp_send(socket_t *sk, const void *buf, size_t len, 
                  sockaddr_in_t *dest)
{
    sk_buff_t *skb = skb_alloc(len + 128);
    if (!skb) return -NEXUS_ENOMEM;
    
    skb_reserve(skb, 64);
    
    /* Add Data */
    memcpy(skb_put(skb, len), buf, len);
    
    /* Add UDP Header */
    udp_header_t *udp = (udp_header_t *)skb_push(skb, sizeof(udp_header_t));
    udp->src_port = htons(sk->local_addr.port);
    udp->dst_port = htons(dest->port);
    udp->length = htons(sizeof(udp_header_t) + len);
    udp->checksum = 0;  /* Optional for UDP */
    
    skb->transport.udp = udp;
    
    /* Add IP Header */
    ip_header_t *ip = (ip_header_t *)skb_push(skb, sizeof(ip_header_t));
    ip->version_ihl = 0x45;
    ip->tos = 0;
    ip->total_length = htons(skb->len);
    ip->id = htons(get_random_u16());
    ip->flags_fragment = 0;
    ip->ttl = 64;
    ip->protocol = IP_PROTO_UDP;
    ip->src_addr = sk->local_addr.addr;
    ip->dst_addr = dest->addr;
    ip->checksum = 0;
    ip->checksum = ip_checksum(ip, sizeof(ip_header_t));
    
    skb->network.ip = ip;
    
    /* Send */
    ip_output(skb);
    
    return len;
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                          IP OUTPUT                                        */
/*===========================================================================*/

int ip_output(sk_buff_t *skb)
{
    ip_header_t *ip = skb->network.ip;
    
    /* If no IP header yet, add one */
    if (!ip) {
        ip = (ip_header_t *)skb_push(skb, sizeof(ip_header_t));
        skb->network.ip = ip;
        
        ip->version_ihl = 0x45;
        ip->tos = 0;
        ip->total_length = htons(skb->len);
        ip->id = htons(get_random_u16());
        ip->flags_fragment = 0;
        ip->ttl = 64;
        ip->checksum = 0;
    }
    
    /* Route Lookup */
    net_device_t *dev;
    u32 next_hop;
    
    int ret = route_lookup(ip->dst_addr, &dev, &next_hop);
    if (ret != NEXUS_OK) {
        skb_free(skb);
        return ret;
    }
    
    /* Set Source Address if Not Set */
    if (ip->src_addr == 0) {
        ip->src_addr = dev->ip_addr;
    }
    
    /* Recalculate Checksum */
    ip->checksum = 0;
    ip->checksum = ip_checksum(ip, sizeof(ip_header_t));
    
    /* Resolve MAC Address */
    u8 dest_mac[6];
    ret = arp_resolve(next_hop, dest_mac, dev);
    if (ret != NEXUS_OK) {
        /* ARP Not Resolved - Queue Packet */
        arp_queue_packet(skb, next_hop, dev);
        return NEXUS_OK;
    }
    
    /* Add Ethernet Header */
    eth_header_t *eth = (eth_header_t *)skb_push(skb, sizeof(eth_header_t));
    memcpy(eth->dest, dest_mac, 6);
    memcpy(eth->src, dev->mac_addr, 6);
    eth->type = htons(ETH_TYPE_IP);
    
    skb->mac.eth = eth;
    skb->dev = dev;
    
    /* Transmit */
    return netdev_transmit(skb, dev);
}

/* Route Lookup */
static int route_lookup(u32 dest, net_device_t **dev, u32 *next_hop)
{
    route_entry_t *best = NULL;
    u32 best_mask = 0;
    
    read_lock(&route_lock);
    
    route_entry_t *entry;
    list_for_each_entry(entry, &route_table, list) {
        if ((dest & entry->netmask) == entry->dest) {
            if (entry->netmask >= best_mask) {
                best = entry;
                best_mask = entry->netmask;
            }
        }
    }
    
    if (!best) {
        read_unlock(&route_lock);
        return NEXUS_ENOENT;
    }
    
    *dev = best->dev;
    *next_hop = best->gateway ? best->gateway : dest;
    
    read_unlock(&route_lock);
    return NEXUS_OK;
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                          ARP PROTOCOL                                     */
/*===========================================================================*/

typedef struct arp_packet {
    u16 hw_type;
    u16 proto_type;
    u8 hw_len;
    u8 proto_len;
    u16 opcode;
    u8 sender_mac[6];
    u32 sender_ip;
    u8 target_mac[6];
    u32 target_ip;
} __packed arp_packet_t;

#define ARP_OP_REQUEST  1
#define ARP_OP_REPLY    2

/* ARP Receive */
void arp_rcv(sk_buff_t *skb)
{
    arp_packet_t *arp = (arp_packet_t *)skb->data;
    net_device_t *dev = skb->dev;
    
    /* Update ARP Cache */
    arp_cache_update(arp->sender_ip, arp->sender_mac);
    
    if (ntohs(arp->opcode) == ARP_OP_REQUEST) {
        /* Check if Target is Us */
        if (arp->target_ip == dev->ip_addr) {
            arp_send_reply(dev, arp->sender_ip, arp->sender_mac);
        }
    }
    
    skb_free(skb);
}

/* ARP Resolve */
static int arp_resolve(u32 ip, u8 *mac, net_device_t *dev)
{
    /* Check Broadcast */
    if (ip == 0xFFFFFFFF || (ip & ~dev->netmask) == ~dev->netmask) {
        memset(mac, 0xFF, 6);
        return NEXUS_OK;
    }
    
    /* Check Cache */
    spin_lock(&arp_lock);
    
    arp_entry_t *entry;
    list_for_each_entry(entry, &arp_cache, list) {
        if (entry->ip_addr == ip) {
            memcpy(mac, entry->mac_addr, 6);
            spin_unlock(&arp_lock);
            return NEXUS_OK;
        }
    }
    
    spin_unlock(&arp_lock);
    
    /* Send ARP Request */
    arp_send_request(dev, ip);
    
    return NEXUS_EAGAIN;
}

/* ARP Send Request */
static void arp_send_request(net_device_t *dev, u32 target_ip)
{
    sk_buff_t *skb = skb_alloc(sizeof(arp_packet_t) + sizeof(eth_header_t) + 64);
    if (!skb) return;
    
    skb_reserve(skb, 32);
    
    /* ARP Packet */
    arp_packet_t *arp = (arp_packet_t *)skb_put(skb, sizeof(arp_packet_t));
    arp->hw_type = htons(1);  /* Ethernet */
    arp->proto_type = htons(ETH_TYPE_IP);
    arp->hw_len = 6;
    arp->proto_len = 4;
    arp->opcode = htons(ARP_OP_REQUEST);
    memcpy(arp->sender_mac, dev->mac_addr, 6);
    arp->sender_ip = dev->ip_addr;
    memset(arp->target_mac, 0, 6);
    arp->target_ip = target_ip;
    
    /* Ethernet Header */
    eth_header_t *eth = (eth_header_t *)skb_push(skb, sizeof(eth_header_t));
    memset(eth->dest, 0xFF, 6);  /* Broadcast */
    memcpy(eth->src, dev->mac_addr, 6);
    eth->type = htons(ETH_TYPE_ARP);
    
    skb->dev = dev;
    netdev_transmit(skb, dev);
}

/* ARP Cache Update */
static void arp_cache_update(u32 ip, u8 *mac)
{
    spin_lock(&arp_lock);
    
    /* Check if Exists */
    arp_entry_t *entry;
    list_for_each_entry(entry, &arp_cache, list) {
        if (entry->ip_addr == ip) {
            memcpy(entry->mac_addr, mac, 6);
            entry->timestamp = get_time_ms();
            spin_unlock(&arp_lock);
            return;
        }
    }
    
    /* Create New Entry */
    entry = kmalloc(sizeof(arp_entry_t));
    if (entry) {
        entry->ip_addr = ip;
        memcpy(entry->mac_addr, mac, 6);
        entry->timestamp = get_time_ms();
        list_add(&entry->list, &arp_cache);
    }
    
    spin_unlock(&arp_lock);
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                      SOCKET INTERFACE                                     */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Create Socket */
socket_t *socket_create(int domain, int type, int protocol)
{
    socket_t *sk = kzalloc(sizeof(socket_t));
    if (!sk) return NULL;
    
    sk->type = type;
    sk->protocol = protocol;
    sk->state = SOCK_STATE_UNCONNECTED;
    sk->owner = current_proc;
    
    INIT_LIST_HEAD(&sk->recv_queue);
    INIT_LIST_HEAD(&sk->send_queue);
    INIT_LIST_HEAD(&sk->accept_queue);
    
    init_waitqueue_head(&sk->recv_wait);
    init_waitqueue_head(&sk->send_wait);
    init_waitqueue_head(&sk->accept_wait);
    
    spin_lock_init(&sk->lock);
    atomic_set(&sk->refcount, 1);
    
    /* Set Default Buffer Sizes */
    sk->recv_buf_size = 65536;
    sk->send_buf_size = 65536;
    
    /* Protocol-Specific Setup */
    if (type == SOCK_STREAM) {
        sk->tcp.state = TCP_STATE_CLOSED;
        sk->tcp.mss = 1460;
        sk->tcp.window = 65535;
    }
    
    return sk;
}

/* Close Socket */
int socket_close(socket_t *sk)
{
    if (!sk) return NEXUS_EINVAL;
    
    spin_lock(&sk->lock);
    
    if (sk->type == SOCK_STREAM && sk->tcp.state == TCP_STATE_ESTABLISHED) {
        /* Initiate Graceful Close */
        sk->tcp.state = TCP_STATE_FIN_WAIT_1;
        tcp_send_fin(sk);
        spin_unlock(&sk->lock);
        
        /* Wait for Close */
        wait_event_timeout(&sk->send_wait,
                           sk->tcp.state == TCP_STATE_CLOSED ||
                           sk->tcp.state == TCP_STATE_TIME_WAIT,
                           5000);
    } else {
        spin_unlock(&sk->lock);
    }
    
    /* Free Queued Data */
    sk_buff_t *skb, *tmp;
    list_for_each_entry_safe(skb, tmp, &sk->recv_queue, list) {
        list_del(&skb->list);
        skb_free(skb);
    }
    
    /* Release Port */
    if (sk->local_addr.port) {
        if (sk->type == SOCK_STREAM) {
            tcp_release_port(sk->local_addr.port);
        } else {
            udp_release_port(sk->local_addr.port);
        }
    }
    
    kfree(sk);
    return NEXUS_OK;
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                      NETWORK INITIALIZATION                               */
/*===========================================================================*/

int network_init(void)
{
    pr_info("Initializing network stack...\n");
    
    /* Initialize Locks */
    spin_lock_init(&netdev_lock);
    spin_lock_init(&arp_lock);
    spin_lock_init(&port_lock);
    rwlock_init(&route_lock);
    
    /* Create SKB Cache */
    skb_cache = kmem_cache_create("skb_cache", sizeof(sk_buff_t), 0);
    
    /* Initialize Loopback */
    net_device_t *lo = netdev_alloc("lo", &loopback_ops);
    lo->ip_addr = 0x7F000001;  /* 127.0.0.1 */
    lo->netmask = 0xFF000000;
    lo->flags = NETDEV_UP | NETDEV_RUNNING;
    memset(lo->mac_addr, 0, 6);
    netdev_register(lo);
    
    /* Add Default Route */
    route_entry_t *default_route = kzalloc(sizeof(route_entry_t));
    default_route->dest = 0;
    default_route->netmask = 0;
    default_route->gateway = 0;  /* Will be set by DHCP */
    default_route->dev = lo;
    default_route->metric = 100;
    list_add_tail(&default_route->list, &route_table);
    
    pr_info("Network stack initialized.\n");
    return NEXUS_OK;
}

int tcp_init(void)
{
    pr_info("Initializing TCP...\n");
    return NEXUS_OK;
}

int udp_init(void)
{
    pr_info("Initializing UDP...\n");
    return NEXUS_OK;
}
```

---

# 10. GUI FRAMEWORK

## 10.1 Compositor (gui/compositor/compositor.c)

```c
/*
 * NEXUS OS - GUI Compositor
 * gui/compositor/compositor.c
 */

#include <kernel.h>
#include <gui/compositor.h>
#include <gui/renderer.h>
#include <drivers/graphics.h>

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                       COMPOSITOR STRUCTURES                               */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Color Formats */
typedef enum {
    PIXEL_FORMAT_ARGB8888,
    PIXEL_FORMAT_XRGB8888,
    PIXEL_FORMAT_RGB888,
    PIXEL_FORMAT_RGB565,
} pixel_format_t;

/* Rectangle */
typedef struct rect {
    s32 x, y;
    s32 width, height;
} rect_t;

/* Point */
typedef struct point {
    s32 x, y;
} point_t;

/* Surface */
typedef struct surface {
    u32 id;
    
    /* Geometry */
    s32 x, y;
    s32 width, height;
    
    /* Buffer */
    void *buffer;
    size_t buffer_size;
    u32 stride;
    pixel_format_t format;
    
    /* State */
    bool visible;
    bool dirty;
    u8 opacity;
    
    /* Damage Region */
    rect_t damage;
    
    /* Owner */
    struct window *window;
    
    /* List */
    struct list_head list;
    
    /* Lock */
    spinlock_t lock;
    
} surface_t;

/* Window */
typedef struct window {
    u32 id;
    char title[256];
    
    /* Geometry */
    s32 x, y;
    s32 width, height;
    
    /* State */
    enum {
        WINDOW_STATE_NORMAL,
        WINDOW_STATE_MAXIMIZED,
        WINDOW_STATE_MINIMIZED,
        WINDOW_STATE_FULLSCREEN,
    } state;
    
    /* Decorations */
    bool decorated;
    s32 border_width;
    s32 titlebar_height;
    
    /* Surfaces */
    surface_t *content;
    surface_t *frame;
    
    /* Focus */
    bool focused;
    bool active;
    
    /* Input */
    bool keyboard_focus;
    bool pointer_focus;
    
    /* Owner */
    process_t *owner;
    
    /* Z-Order */
    s32 z_order;
    
    /* Parent/Children */
    struct window *parent;
    struct list_head children;
    struct list_head sibling;
    
    /* List */
    struct list_head list;
    struct rb_node rb_node;
    
    /* Event Queue */
    struct list_head event_queue;
    wait_queue_t event_wait;
    
    /* Lock */
    spinlock_t lock;
    
} window_t;

/* Compositor */
typedef struct compositor {
    /* Display */
    struct {
        u32 width;
        u32 height;
        u32 refresh_rate;
        pixel_format_t format;
    } display;
    
    /* Framebuffers */
    surface_t *front_buffer;
    surface_t *back_buffer;
    
    /* Windows */
    struct list_head window_list;
    struct rb_root window_tree;
    u32 next_window_id;
    
    /* Focus */
    window_t *focused_window;
    window_t *active_window;
    
    /* Cursor */
    struct {
        s32 x, y;
        surface_t *sprite;
        bool visible;
    } cursor;
    
    /* Wallpaper */
    surface_t *wallpaper;
    
    /* Damage Tracking */
    struct list_head damage_list;
    
    /* State */
    bool running;
    bool needs_repaint;
    
    /* Rendering Thread */
    thread_t *render_thread;
    
    /* VSync */
    bool vsync_enabled;
    wait_queue_t vsync_wait;
    
    /* Statistics */
    u64 frames_rendered;
    u64 last_frame_time;
    u32 fps;
    
    /* Lock */
    rwlock_t lock;
    
} compositor_t;

/* GUI Event */
typedef struct gui_event {
    enum {
        GUI_EVENT_KEY_PRESS,
        GUI_EVENT_KEY_RELEASE,
        GUI_EVENT_MOUSE_MOVE,
        GUI_EVENT_MOUSE_BUTTON,
        GUI_EVENT_MOUSE_SCROLL,
        GUI_EVENT_WINDOW_RESIZE,
        GUI_EVENT_WINDOW_CLOSE,
        GUI_EVENT_WINDOW_FOCUS,
        GUI_EVENT_PAINT,
    } type;
    
    union {
        struct {
            u32 keycode;
            u32 modifiers;
            char character;
        } key;
        
        struct {
            s32 x, y;
            s32 dx, dy;
            u32 buttons;
        } mouse;
        
        struct {
            s32 width, height;
        } resize;
    } data;
    
    u64 timestamp;
    struct list_head list;
    
} gui_event_t;

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                          GLOBAL STATE                                     */
/*===========================================================================*/

static compositor_t compositor = {0};
static struct kmem_cache *window_cache = NULL;
static struct kmem_cache *surface_cache = NULL;
static struct kmem_cache *event_cache = NULL;

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                       SURFACE OPERATIONS                                  */
/*===========================================================================*/

surface_t *surface_create(u32 width, u32 height, pixel_format_t format)
{
    surface_t *surface = kmem_cache_alloc(surface_cache);
    if (!surface) return NULL;
    
    memset(surface, 0, sizeof(surface_t));
    
    surface->width = width;
    surface->height = height;
    surface->format = format;
    surface->opacity = 255;
    surface->visible = true;
    
    /* Calculate Stride and Size */
    u32 bpp = 4;  /* Assume 32-bit */
    surface->stride = width * bpp;
    surface->buffer_size = surface->stride * height;
    
    /* Allocate Buffer */
    surface->buffer = vmalloc(surface->buffer_size);
    if (!surface->buffer) {
        kmem_cache_free(surface_cache, surface);
        return NULL;
    }
    
    memset(surface->buffer, 0, surface->buffer_size);
    
    INIT_LIST_HEAD(&surface->list);
    spin_lock_init(&surface->lock);
    
    return surface;
}

void surface_destroy(surface_t *surface)
{
    if (!surface) return;
    
    if (surface->buffer) {
        vfree(surface->buffer);
    }
    
    kmem_cache_free(surface_cache, surface);
}

void surface_damage(surface_t *surface, rect_t *rect)
{
    spin_lock(&surface->lock);
    
    if (rect) {
        /* Union with Existing Damage */
        if (surface->dirty) {
            s32 x1 = MIN(surface->damage.x, rect->x);
            s32 y1 = MIN(surface->damage.y, rect->y);
            s32 x2 = MAX(surface->damage.x + surface->damage.width,
                         rect->x + rect->width);
            s32 y2 = MAX(surface->damage.y + surface->damage.height,
                         rect->y + rect->height);
            
            surface->damage.x = x1;
            surface->damage.y = y1;
            surface->damage.width = x2 - x1;
            surface->damage.height = y2 - y1;
        } else {
            surface->damage = *rect;
        }
    } else {
        /* Full Surface Damage */
        surface->damage.x = 0;
        surface->damage.y = 0;
        surface->damage.width = surface->width;
        surface->damage.height = surface->height;
    }
    
    surface->dirty = true;
    
    spin_unlock(&surface->lock);
    
    compositor.needs_repaint = true;
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                       WINDOW OPERATIONS                                   */
/*===========================================================================*/

window_t *window_create(process_t *owner, const char *title,
                        s32 x, s32 y, s32 width, s32 height, u32 flags)
{
    window_t *window = kmem_cache_alloc(window_cache);
    if (!window) return NULL;
    
    memset(window, 0, sizeof(window_t));
    
    write_lock(&compositor.lock);
    window->id = compositor.next_window_id++;
    write_unlock(&compositor.lock);
    
    strncpy(window->title, title, sizeof(window->title) - 1);
    window->x = x;
    window->y = y;
    window->width = width;
    window->height = height;
    window->state = WINDOW_STATE_NORMAL;
    window->owner = owner;
    window->decorated = !(flags & WINDOW_FLAG_UNDECORATED);
    window->border_width = 1;
    window->titlebar_height = 30;
    
    /* Create Content Surface */
    window->content = surface_create(width, height, PIXEL_FORMAT_ARGB8888);
    if (!window->content) {
        kmem_cache_free(window_cache, window);
        return NULL;
    }
    window->content->window = window;
    
    /* Create Frame Surface if Decorated */
    if (window->decorated) {
        s32 frame_width = width + 2 * window->border_width;
        s32 frame_height = height + window->titlebar_height + window->border_width;
        
        window->frame = surface_create(frame_width, frame_height, 
                                        PIXEL_FORMAT_ARGB8888);
        if (window->frame) {
            window->frame->window = window;
            window_draw_frame(window);
        }
    }
    
    INIT_LIST_HEAD(&window->children);
    INIT_LIST_HEAD(&window->sibling);
    INIT_LIST_HEAD(&window->event_queue);
    init_waitqueue_head(&window->event_wait);
    spin_lock_init(&window->lock);
    
    /* Add to Compositor */
    write_lock(&compositor.lock);
    list_add(&window->list, &compositor.window_list);
    window->z_order = 0;
    write_unlock(&compositor.lock);
    
    /* Mark for Repaint */
    compositor.needs_repaint = true;
    
    pr_debug("Created window %d '%s' at (%d, %d) %dx%d\n",
             window->id, window->title, x, y, width, height);
    
    return window;
}

void window_destroy(window_t *window)
{
    if (!window) return;
    
    /* Remove from Compositor */
    write_lock(&compositor.lock);
    list_del(&window->list);
    
    if (compositor.focused_window == window) {
        compositor.focused_window = NULL;
    }
    if (compositor.active_window == window) {
        compositor.active_window = NULL;
    }
    write_unlock(&compositor.lock);
    
    /* Destroy Surfaces */
    if (window->content) {
        surface_destroy(window->content);
    }
    if (window->frame) {
        surface_destroy(window->frame);
    }
    
    /* Free Events */
    gui_event_t *event, *tmp;
    list_for_each_entry_safe(event, tmp, &window->event_queue, list) {
        list_del(&event->list);
        kmem_cache_free(event_cache, event);
    }
    
    kmem_cache_free(window_cache, window);
    
    compositor.needs_repaint = true;
}

void window_move(window_t *window, s32 x, s32 y)
{
    spin_lock(&window->lock);
    window->x = x;
    window->y = y;
    spin_unlock(&window->lock);
    
    compositor.needs_repaint = true;
}

void window_resize(window_t *window, s32 width, s32 height)
{
    spin_lock(&window->lock);
    
    /* Resize Content Surface */
    surface_t *new_content = surface_create(width, height, PIXEL_FORMAT_ARGB8888);
    if (new_content) {
        /* Copy Old Content */
        s32 copy_width = MIN(width, window->width);
        s32 copy_height = MIN(height, window->height);
        
        for (s32 y = 0; y < copy_height; y++) {
            memcpy((u8*)new_content->buffer + y * new_content->stride,
                   (u8*)window->content->buffer + y * window->content->stride,
                   copy_width * 4);
        }
        
        surface_destroy(window->content);
        window->content = new_content;
        new_content->window = window;
    }
    
    window->width = width;
    window->height = height;
    
    /* Resize Frame */
    if (window->decorated && window->frame) {
        surface_destroy(window->frame);
        
        s32 frame_width = width + 2 * window->border_width;
        s32 frame_height = height + window->titlebar_height + window->border_width;
        
        window->frame = surface_create(frame_width, frame_height,
                                        PIXEL_FORMAT_ARGB8888);
        if (window->frame) {
            window->frame->window = window;
            window_draw_frame(window);
        }
    }
    
    spin_unlock(&window->lock);
    
    /* Send Resize Event */
    gui_event_t *event = kmem_cache_alloc(event_cache);
    if (event) {
        event->type = GUI_EVENT_WINDOW_RESIZE;
        event->data.resize.width = width;
        event->data.resize.height = height;
        event->timestamp = get_time_ms();
        
        list_add_tail(&event->list, &window->event_queue);
        wake_up(&window->event_wait);
    }
    
    compositor.needs_repaint = true;
}

void window_set_focus(window_t *window)
{
    write_lock(&compositor.lock);
    
    if (compositor.focused_window) {
        compositor.focused_window->focused = false;
    }
    
    compositor.focused_window = window;
    
    if (window) {
        window->focused = true;
        
        /* Bring to Front */
        list_del(&window->list);
        list_add(&window->list, &compositor.window_list);
    }
    
    write_unlock(&compositor.lock);
    
    compositor.needs_repaint = true;
}

static void window_draw_frame(window_t *window)
{
    if (!window->frame) return;
    
    u32 *pixels = (u32 *)window->frame->buffer;
    s32 w = window->frame->width;
    s32 h = window->frame->height;
    
    /* Frame Colors */
    u32 border_color = window->focused ? 0xFF4488FF : 0xFF888888;
    u32 titlebar_color = window->focused ? 0xFF3366CC : 0xFF666666;
    u32 title_color = 0xFFFFFFFF;
    
    /* Draw Border */
    for (s32 y = 0; y < h; y++) {
        for (s32 x = 0; x < w; x++) {
            if (x < window->border_width || x >= w - window->border_width ||
                y < window->border_width || y >= h - window->border_width) {
                pixels[y * w + x] = border_color;
            } else if (y < window->titlebar_height) {
                pixels[y * w + x] = titlebar_color;
            } else {
                pixels[y * w + x] = 0;  /* Transparent Content Area */
            }
        }
    }
    
    /* Draw Title Text */
    render_text(window->frame, window->title,
                window->border_width + 8,
                (window->titlebar_height - 16) / 2,
                title_color);
    
    /* Draw Close Button */
    s32 btn_size = 20;
    s32 btn_x = w - window->border_width - btn_size - 4;
    s32 btn_y = (window->titlebar_height - btn_size) / 2;
    
    for (s32 y = btn_y; y < btn_y + btn_size; y++) {
        for (s32 x = btn_x; x < btn_x + btn_size; x++) {
            pixels[y * w + x] = 0xFFCC4444;
        }
    }
    
    surface_damage(window->frame, NULL);
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                        INPUT HANDLING                                     */
/*===========================================================================*/

void compositor_handle_mouse(s32 x, s32 y, u32 buttons)
{
    /* Update Cursor Position */
    s32 old_x = compositor.cursor.x;
    s32 old_y = compositor.cursor.y;
    
    compositor.cursor.x = CLAMP(x, 0, (s32)compositor.display.width - 1);
    compositor.cursor.y = CLAMP(y, 0, (s32)compositor.display.height - 1);
    
    /* Find Window Under Cursor */
    window_t *target = NULL;
    
    read_lock(&compositor.lock);
    
    window_t *window;
    list_for_each_entry(window, &compositor.window_list, list) {
        s32 wx = window->x;
        s32 wy = window->y;
        s32 ww = window->width;
        s32 wh = window->height;
        
        if (window->decorated) {
            wx -= window->border_width;
            wy -= window->titlebar_height;
            ww += 2 * window->border_width;
            wh += window->titlebar_height + window->border_width;
        }
        
        if (compositor.cursor.x >= wx && compositor.cursor.x < wx + ww &&
            compositor.cursor.y >= wy && compositor.cursor.y < wy + wh) {
            target = window;
            break;
        }
    }
    
    read_unlock(&compositor.lock);
    
    /* Handle Click */
    static u32 last_buttons = 0;
    u32 pressed = buttons & ~last_buttons;
    u32 released = last_buttons & ~buttons;
    
    if (pressed & 1) {  /* Left Button Pressed */
        if (target && target != compositor.focused_window) {
            window_set_focus(target);
        }
        
        /* Check Titlebar Click */
        if (target && target->decorated) {
            s32 local_y = compositor.cursor.y - target->y + target->titlebar_height;
            if (local_y < target->titlebar_height) {
                /* Start Window Drag */
                /* TODO: Implement dragging */
            }
        }
    }
    
    last_buttons = buttons;
    
    /* Send Mouse Event to Window */
    if (target) {
        gui_event_t *event = kmem_cache_alloc(event_cache);
        if (event) {
            event->type = GUI_EVENT_MOUSE_MOVE;
            event->data.mouse.x = compositor.cursor.x - target->x;
            event->data.mouse.y = compositor.cursor.y - target->y;
            event->data.mouse.dx = compositor.cursor.x - old_x;
            event->data.mouse.dy = compositor.cursor.y - old_y;
            event->data.mouse.buttons = buttons;
            event->timestamp = get_time_ms();
            
            spin_lock(&target->lock);
            list_add_tail(&event->list, &target->event_queue);
            spin_unlock(&target->lock);
            
            wake_up(&target->event_wait);
        }
    }
    
    compositor.needs_repaint = true;
}

void compositor_handle_keyboard(u32 keycode, bool pressed, u32 modifiers)
{
    window_t *target = compositor.focused_window;
    
    if (!target) return;
    
    gui_event_t *event = kmem_cache_alloc(event_cache);
    if (!event) return;
    
    event->type = pressed ? GUI_EVENT_KEY_PRESS : GUI_EVENT_KEY_RELEASE;
    event->data.key.keycode = keycode;
    event->data.key.modifiers = modifiers;
    event->data.key.character = keycode_to_char(keycode, modifiers);
    event->timestamp = get_time_ms();
    
    spin_lock(&target->lock);
    list_add_tail(&event->list, &target->event_queue);
    spin_unlock(&target->lock);
    
    wake_up(&target->event_wait);
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                          RENDERING                                        */
/*===========================================================================*/

static void compositor_render_frame(void)
{
    surface_t *target = compositor.back_buffer;
    
    /* Clear Background */
    if (compositor.wallpaper) {
        /* Copy Wallpaper */
        memcpy(target->buffer, compositor.wallpaper->buffer,
               MIN(target->buffer_size, compositor.wallpaper->buffer_size));
    } else {
        /* Solid Color Background */
        u32 *pixels = (u32 *)target->buffer;
        u32 bg_color = 0xFF204060;
        
        for (u32 i = 0; i < target->buffer_size / 4; i++) {
            pixels[i] = bg_color;
        }
    }
    
    /* Render Windows (Back to Front) */
    read_lock(&compositor.lock);
    
    window_t *window;
    list_for_each_entry_reverse(window, &compositor.window_list, list) {
        if (window->state == WINDOW_STATE_MINIMIZED) continue;
        
        /* Calculate Window Position */
        s32 wx = window->x;
        s32 wy = window->y;
        
        if (window->decorated) {
            wx -= window->border_width;
            wy -= window->titlebar_height;
        }
        
        /* Render Frame */
        if (window->frame && window->decorated) {
            compositor_blit(target, window->frame, wx, wy, window->opacity);
        }
        
        /* Render Content */
        if (window->content) {
            s32 cx = window->x;
            s32 cy = window->y;
            compositor_blit(target, window->content, cx, cy, window->opacity);
        }
    }
    
    read_unlock(&compositor.lock);
    
    /* Render Cursor */
    if (compositor.cursor.visible && compositor.cursor.sprite) {
        compositor_blit(target, compositor.cursor.sprite,
                        compositor.cursor.x, compositor.cursor.y, 255);
    }
    
    /* Swap Buffers */
    surface_t *tmp = compositor.front_buffer;
    compositor.front_buffer = compositor.back_buffer;
    compositor.back_buffer = tmp;
    
    /* Update Display */
    display_update(compositor.front_buffer->buffer);
    
    /* Statistics */
    compositor.frames_rendered++;
    u64 now = get_time_ms();
    u64 frame_time = now - compositor.last_frame_time;
    compositor.last_frame_time = now;
    
    if (frame_time > 0) {
        compositor.fps = 1000 / frame_time;
    }
}

/* Blit Surface to Target with Alpha Blending */
static void compositor_blit(surface_t *dst, surface_t *src,
                            s32 x, s32 y, u8 opacity)
{
    /* Clip to Destination */
    s32 sx = 0, sy = 0;
    s32 sw = src->width;
    s32 sh = src->height;
    
    if (x < 0) { sx = -x; sw += x; x = 0; }
    if (y < 0) { sy = -y; sh += y; y = 0; }
    if (x + sw > dst->width) sw = dst->width - x;
    if (y + sh > dst->height) sh = dst->height - y;
    
    if (sw <= 0 || sh <= 0) return;
    
    u32 *dst_pixels = (u32 *)dst->buffer;
    u32 *src_pixels = (u32 *)src->buffer;
    
    for (s32 row = 0; row < sh; row++) {
        u32 *dst_row = &dst_pixels[(y + row) * dst->width + x];
        u32 *src_row = &src_pixels[(sy + row) * src->width + sx];
        
        for (s32 col = 0; col < sw; col++) {
            u32 sp = src_row[col];
            u32 dp = dst_row[col];
            
            u8 sa = ((sp >> 24) & 0xFF) * opacity / 255;
            
            if (sa == 255) {
                dst_row[col] = sp;
            } else if (sa > 0) {
                /* Alpha Blend */
                u8 da = 255 - sa;
                
                u8 sr = (sp >> 16) & 0xFF;
                u8 sg = (sp >> 8) & 0xFF;
                u8 sb = sp & 0xFF;
                
                u8 dr = (dp >> 16) & 0xFF;
                u8 dg = (dp >> 8) & 0xFF;
                u8 db = dp & 0xFF;
                
                u8 r = (sr * sa + dr * da) / 255;
                u8 g = (sg * sa + dg * da) / 255;
                u8 b = (sb * sa + db * da) / 255;
                
                dst_row[col] = 0xFF000000 | (r << 16) | (g << 8) | b;
            }
        }
    }
}

/* Render Thread */
static void compositor_render_thread(void *arg)
{
    pr_info("Compositor render thread started.\n");
    
    while (compositor.running) {
        /* Wait for VSync or Damage */
        if (compositor.vsync_enabled) {
            wait_event(&compositor.vsync_wait, compositor.needs_repaint);
        } else if (!compositor.needs_repaint) {
            thread_sleep(16);  /* ~60 FPS */
            continue;
        }
        
        compositor.needs_repaint = false;
        
        /* Render Frame */
        compositor_render_frame();
    }
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                    COMPOSITOR INITIALIZATION                              */
/*===========================================================================*/

int compositor_init(void)
{
    pr_info("Initializing compositor...\n");
    
    /* Initialize Display */
    display_info_t display_info;
    if (display_get_info(&display_info) != NEXUS_OK) {
        pr_err("Failed to get display info!\n");
        return NEXUS_ERROR;
    }
    
    compositor.display.width = display_info.width;
    compositor.display.height = display_info.height;
    compositor.display.refresh_rate = display_info.refresh_rate;
    compositor.display.format = PIXEL_FORMAT_ARGB8888;
    
    pr_info("  Display: %dx%d @ %d Hz\n",
            compositor.display.width,
            compositor.display.height,
            compositor.display.refresh_rate);
    
    /* Create Caches */
    window_cache = kmem_cache_create("window_cache", sizeof(window_t), 0);
    surface_cache = kmem_cache_create("surface_cache", sizeof(surface_t), 0);
