# 1. ADVANCED SCHEDULER

## 1.1 CFS Scheduler (kernel/sched/cfs.c)

```c
/*
 * NEXUS OS - Completely Fair Scheduler (CFS)
 * kernel/sched/cfs.c
 */

#include <kernel.h>
#include <sched/scheduler.h>
#include <sched/cfs.h>

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                         CFS CONSTANTS                                     */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Scheduling Latency - Target for one scheduling period */
#define SCHED_LATENCY_NS            6000000ULL      /* 6ms */
#define SCHED_MIN_GRANULARITY_NS    750000ULL       /* 0.75ms */
#define SCHED_WAKEUP_GRANULARITY_NS 1000000ULL      /* 1ms */

/* Nice Value Range */
#define NICE_TO_PRIO(nice)          ((nice) + 20)
#define PRIO_TO_NICE(prio)          ((prio) - 20)
#define MIN_NICE                    -20
#define MAX_NICE                    19
#define DEFAULT_NICE                0

/* Weight Table (indexed by nice + 20) */
static const u32 sched_prio_to_weight[40] = {
    /* -20 */     88761,     71755,     56483,     46273,     36291,
    /* -15 */     29154,     23254,     18705,     14949,     11916,
    /* -10 */      9548,      7620,      6100,      4904,      3906,
    /*  -5 */      3121,      2501,      1991,      1586,      1277,
    /*   0 */      1024,       820,       655,       526,       423,
    /*   5 */       335,       272,       215,       172,       137,
    /*  10 */       110,        87,        70,        56,        45,
    /*  15 */        36,        29,        23,        18,        15,
};

/* Inverse Weight Table (for multiplication instead of division) */
static const u32 sched_prio_to_wmult[40] = {
    /* -20 */     48388,     59856,     76040,     92818,    118348,
    /* -15 */    147320,    184698,    229616,    287308,    360437,
    /* -10 */    449829,    563644,    704093,    875809,   1099582,
    /*  -5 */   1376151,   1717300,   2157191,   2708050,   3363326,
    /*   0 */   4194304,   5237765,   6557202,   8165337,  10153587,
    /*   5 */  12820798,  15790321,  19976592,  24970740,  31350126,
    /*  10 */  39045157,  49367440,  61356676,  76695844,  95443717,
    /*  15 */ 119304647, 148102320, 186737708, 238609294, 286331153,
};

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                         CFS STRUCTURES                                    */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Scheduling Entity */
typedef struct sched_entity {
    /* Load Weight */
    struct {
        u32 weight;
        u32 inv_weight;
    } load;
    
    /* RB-Tree Node for Run Queue */
    struct rb_node run_node;
    
    /* List for Group */
    struct list_head group_node;
    
    /* State */
    bool on_rq;
    
    /* Virtual Runtime */
    u64 vruntime;
    
    /* Execution Statistics */
    u64 sum_exec_runtime;
    u64 prev_sum_exec_runtime;
    
    /* Start Time of Current Execution */
    u64 exec_start;
    
    /* Slice Statistics */
    u64 nr_migrations;
    u64 nr_wakeups;
    u64 nr_wakeups_sync;
    u64 nr_wakeups_migrate;
    
    /* Parent Entity (for group scheduling) */
    struct sched_entity *parent;
    
    /* CFS Run Queue */
    struct cfs_rq *cfs_rq;
    struct cfs_rq *my_q;  /* For group scheduling */
    
    /* Depth in Hierarchy */
    int depth;
    
} sched_entity_t;

/* CFS Run Queue */
typedef struct cfs_rq {
    /* Load Tracking */
    struct {
        u64 weight;
        u64 runnable_weight;
        u64 blocked_weight;
    } load;
    
    /* Number of Running Tasks */
    u32 nr_running;
    u32 h_nr_running;  /* Hierarchical */
    
    /* Current Running Entity */
    sched_entity_t *curr;
    sched_entity_t *next;
    sched_entity_t *last;
    sched_entity_t *skip;
    
    /* RB-Tree of Runnable Entities */
    struct rb_root_cached tasks_timeline;
    
    /* Minimum vruntime */
    u64 min_vruntime;
    
    /* Clock */
    u64 exec_clock;
    
    /* CPU */
    int cpu;
    struct rq *rq;
    
    /* Throttle */
    bool throttled;
    s64 runtime_remaining;
    
    /* Group Scheduling */
    struct task_group *tg;
    struct sched_entity *se;
    
    /* Statistics */
    u64 nr_spread_over;
    
} cfs_rq_t;

/* Task Group (for cgroup integration) */
typedef struct task_group {
    /* Parent Group */
    struct task_group *parent;
    
    /* Children */
    struct list_head children;
    struct list_head siblings;
    
    /* Scheduling Entity per CPU */
    sched_entity_t **se;
    
    /* CFS Run Queue per CPU */
    cfs_rq_t **cfs_rq;
    
    /* Shares (weight) */
    unsigned long shares;
    
    /* Bandwidth Control */
    struct {
        u64 quota;
        u64 period;
        u64 runtime;
        bool throttled;
        timer_t period_timer;
        timer_t slack_timer;
    } cfs_bandwidth;
    
    /* Cgroup */
    struct cgroup *css_cgroup;
    
} task_group_t;

/* Per-CPU Run Queue */
typedef struct rq {
    /* Lock */
    spinlock_t lock;
    
    /* Number of Running Tasks */
    u32 nr_running;
    
    /* CPU Load */
    u64 cpu_load[5];
    u64 last_load_update;
    
    /* CFS Run Queue */
    cfs_rq_t cfs;
    
    /* Real-Time Run Queue */
    struct rt_rq rt;
    
    /* Deadline Run Queue */
    struct dl_rq dl;
    
    /* Current Task */
    thread_t *curr;
    thread_t *idle;
    
    /* Clock */
    u64 clock;
    u64 clock_task;
    u64 clock_pelt;
    
    /* Context Switches */
    u64 nr_switches;
    
    /* CPU ID */
    int cpu;
    bool online;
    
    /* Idle Statistics */
    u64 idle_stamp;
    u64 avg_idle;
    u64 max_idle_balance_cost;
    
    /* Push/Pull */
    bool overloaded;
    bool push_busy;
    struct list_head push_tasks;
    
    /* Migration */
    int active_balance;
    int push_cpu;
    thread_t *migration_thread;
    
    /* Scheduling Domain */
    struct sched_domain *sd;
    
    /* NUMA */
    int numa_preferred_nid;
    
} rq_t;

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                          GLOBAL STATE                                     */
/*===========================================================================*/

static DEFINE_PER_CPU(rq_t, runqueues);
static task_group_t root_task_group;

#define cpu_rq(cpu)         (&per_cpu(runqueues, cpu))
#define this_rq()           (&per_cpu(runqueues, get_cpu_id()))
#define task_rq(task)       cpu_rq((task)->cpu)
#define rq_clock(rq)        ((rq)->clock)

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                        HELPER FUNCTIONS                                   */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Calculate Time Slice */
static u64 calc_delta_fair(u64 delta, sched_entity_t *se)
{
    if (unlikely(se->load.weight != NICE_0_LOAD)) {
        delta = (delta * NICE_0_LOAD) / se->load.weight;
    }
    return delta;
}

/* Calculate vruntime delta */
static u64 calc_delta_vruntime(u64 delta, sched_entity_t *se)
{
    /* vruntime = delta * NICE_0_WEIGHT / weight */
    if (se->load.weight != 1024) {
        u64 fact = 1024;
        u32 inv = se->load.inv_weight;
        
        delta = (delta * fact * inv) >> 32;
    }
    return delta;
}

/* Get Scheduling Period */
static u64 sched_period(u32 nr_running)
{
    if (nr_running > 8) {
        return nr_running * SCHED_MIN_GRANULARITY_NS;
    }
    return SCHED_LATENCY_NS;
}

/* Calculate Time Slice for Entity */
static u64 sched_slice(cfs_rq_t *cfs_rq, sched_entity_t *se)
{
    u64 slice = sched_period(cfs_rq->nr_running + !se->on_rq);
    
    /* Weighted Fair Share */
    if (cfs_rq->load.weight > 0) {
        slice = (slice * se->load.weight) / cfs_rq->load.weight;
    }
    
    return MAX(slice, SCHED_MIN_GRANULARITY_NS);
}

/* Update Entity Load */
static void set_load_weight(sched_entity_t *se, int nice)
{
    int prio = NICE_TO_PRIO(nice);
    
    se->load.weight = sched_prio_to_weight[prio];
    se->load.inv_weight = sched_prio_to_wmult[prio];
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                      RB-TREE OPERATIONS                                   */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Insert Entity into RB-Tree */
static void enqueue_entity_rb(cfs_rq_t *cfs_rq, sched_entity_t *se)
{
    struct rb_node **link = &cfs_rq->tasks_timeline.rb_root.rb_node;
    struct rb_node *parent = NULL;
    bool leftmost = true;
    
    while (*link) {
        parent = *link;
        sched_entity_t *entry = rb_entry(parent, sched_entity_t, run_node);
        
        if (se->vruntime < entry->vruntime) {
            link = &parent->rb_left;
        } else {
            link = &parent->rb_right;
            leftmost = false;
        }
    }
    
    rb_link_node(&se->run_node, parent, link);
    rb_insert_color_cached(&se->run_node, &cfs_rq->tasks_timeline, leftmost);
}

/* Remove Entity from RB-Tree */
static void dequeue_entity_rb(cfs_rq_t *cfs_rq, sched_entity_t *se)
{
    rb_erase_cached(&se->run_node, &cfs_rq->tasks_timeline);
}

/* Get Leftmost (Minimum vruntime) Entity */
static sched_entity_t *pick_first_entity(cfs_rq_t *cfs_rq)
{
    struct rb_node *left = rb_first_cached(&cfs_rq->tasks_timeline);
    
    if (!left) return NULL;
    
    return rb_entry(left, sched_entity_t, run_node);
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                     VRUNTIME MANAGEMENT                                   */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Update Minimum vruntime */
static void update_min_vruntime(cfs_rq_t *cfs_rq)
{
    sched_entity_t *curr = cfs_rq->curr;
    sched_entity_t *first = pick_first_entity(cfs_rq);
    
    u64 vruntime = cfs_rq->min_vruntime;
    
    if (curr) {
        if (curr->on_rq) {
            vruntime = curr->vruntime;
        } else {
            curr = NULL;
        }
    }
    
    if (first) {
        if (!curr) {
            vruntime = first->vruntime;
        } else {
            vruntime = MIN(vruntime, first->vruntime);
        }
    }
    
    /* Ensure min_vruntime is monotonically increasing */
    cfs_rq->min_vruntime = MAX(cfs_rq->min_vruntime, vruntime);
}

/* Update Entity vruntime */
static void update_curr(cfs_rq_t *cfs_rq)
{
    sched_entity_t *curr = cfs_rq->curr;
    u64 now = rq_clock(cfs_rq->rq);
    u64 delta_exec;
    
    if (!curr) return;
    
    delta_exec = now - curr->exec_start;
    if (delta_exec <= 0) return;
    
    curr->exec_start = now;
    curr->sum_exec_runtime += delta_exec;
    
    /* Add Weighted Time to vruntime */
    curr->vruntime += calc_delta_vruntime(delta_exec, curr);
    
    update_min_vruntime(cfs_rq);
}

/* Place Entity on Enqueue */
static void place_entity(cfs_rq_t *cfs_rq, sched_entity_t *se, int initial)
{
    u64 vruntime = cfs_rq->min_vruntime;
    
    if (initial) {
        /* New Task - Start with Target Latency Penalty */
        vruntime += sched_slice(cfs_rq, se) / 2;
    } else {
        /* Waking Task - Give Some Boost */
        u64 thresh = SCHED_LATENCY_NS;
        
        if (se->vruntime + thresh < vruntime) {
            se->vruntime = vruntime - thresh;
        }
    }
    
    se->vruntime = MAX(se->vruntime, vruntime);
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                      ENQUEUE/DEQUEUE                                      */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Enqueue Entity */
static void enqueue_entity(cfs_rq_t *cfs_rq, sched_entity_t *se, int flags)
{
    bool renorm = !(flags & ENQUEUE_WAKEUP);
    bool curr = cfs_rq->curr == se;
    
    if (renorm) {
        se->vruntime += cfs_rq->min_vruntime;
    }
    
    update_curr(cfs_rq);
    
    if (flags & ENQUEUE_WAKEUP) {
        place_entity(cfs_rq, se, 0);
    }
    
    /* Update Load */
    cfs_rq->load.weight += se->load.weight;
    cfs_rq->nr_running++;
    
    if (!curr) {
        enqueue_entity_rb(cfs_rq, se);
    }
    
    se->on_rq = true;
}

/* Dequeue Entity */
static void dequeue_entity(cfs_rq_t *cfs_rq, sched_entity_t *se, int flags)
{
    update_curr(cfs_rq);
    
    if (se != cfs_rq->curr) {
        dequeue_entity_rb(cfs_rq, se);
    }
    
    se->on_rq = false;
    
    /* Update Load */
    cfs_rq->load.weight -= se->load.weight;
    cfs_rq->nr_running--;
    
    /* Normalize vruntime for Later Re-enqueue */
    if (!(flags & DEQUEUE_SLEEP)) {
        se->vruntime -= cfs_rq->min_vruntime;
    }
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                       TASK PICKING                                        */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Check Preemption */
static void check_preempt_tick(cfs_rq_t *cfs_rq, sched_entity_t *curr)
{
    u64 ideal_runtime, delta_exec;
    sched_entity_t *se;
    s64 delta;
    
    ideal_runtime = sched_slice(cfs_rq, curr);
    delta_exec = curr->sum_exec_runtime - curr->prev_sum_exec_runtime;
    
    if (delta_exec > ideal_runtime) {
        /* Exceeded Time Slice */
        set_tsk_need_resched(current);
        return;
    }
    
    if (delta_exec < SCHED_MIN_GRANULARITY_NS) {
        return;
    }
    
    se = pick_first_entity(cfs_rq);
    
    if (!se) return;
    
    delta = curr->vruntime - se->vruntime;
    
    if (delta > (s64)ideal_runtime) {
        set_tsk_need_resched(current);
    }
}

/* Check Wakeup Preemption */
static void check_preempt_wakeup(rq_t *rq, thread_t *p)
{
    sched_entity_t *se = &current->se;
    sched_entity_t *pse = &p->se;
    s64 delta;
    
    if (se == pse) return;
    
    update_curr(&rq->cfs);
    
    delta = se->vruntime - pse->vruntime;
    
    if (delta > (s64)SCHED_WAKEUP_GRANULARITY_NS) {
        set_tsk_need_resched(current);
    }
}

/* Pick Next Entity */
static sched_entity_t *pick_next_entity(cfs_rq_t *cfs_rq)
{
    sched_entity_t *se = pick_first_entity(cfs_rq);
    
    /* Handle Skip/Next Hints */
    if (cfs_rq->skip) {
        if (cfs_rq->skip == se) {
            sched_entity_t *second = rb_entry(rb_next(&se->run_node),
                                               sched_entity_t, run_node);
            if (second) se = second;
        }
    }
    
    if (cfs_rq->next && cfs_rq->next->on_rq) {
        se = cfs_rq->next;
    }
    
    return se;
}

/* Set Current Entity */
static void set_next_entity(cfs_rq_t *cfs_rq, sched_entity_t *se)
{
    if (se->on_rq) {
        dequeue_entity_rb(cfs_rq, se);
    }
    
    se->exec_start = rq_clock(cfs_rq->rq);
    se->prev_sum_exec_runtime = se->sum_exec_runtime;
    
    cfs_rq->curr = se;
}

/* Put Previous Entity */
static void put_prev_entity(cfs_rq_t *cfs_rq, sched_entity_t *prev)
{
    if (prev->on_rq) {
        update_curr(cfs_rq);
        enqueue_entity_rb(cfs_rq, prev);
    }
    
    cfs_rq->curr = NULL;
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                     MAIN CFS INTERFACE                                    */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Enqueue Task */
void cfs_enqueue_task(rq_t *rq, thread_t *p, int flags)
{
    sched_entity_t *se = &p->se;
    cfs_rq_t *cfs_rq = &rq->cfs;
    
    enqueue_entity(cfs_rq, se, flags);
    
    rq->nr_running++;
}

/* Dequeue Task */
void cfs_dequeue_task(rq_t *rq, thread_t *p, int flags)
{
    sched_entity_t *se = &p->se;
    cfs_rq_t *cfs_rq = &rq->cfs;
    
    dequeue_entity(cfs_rq, se, flags);
    
    rq->nr_running--;
}

/* Yield Task */
void cfs_yield_task(rq_t *rq)
{
    cfs_rq_t *cfs_rq = &rq->cfs;
    sched_entity_t *curr = cfs_rq->curr;
    sched_entity_t *rightmost;
    
    if (!curr || cfs_rq->nr_running < 2) {
        return;
    }
    
    update_curr(cfs_rq);
    
    /* Move to Rightmost Position */
    rightmost = rb_entry(rb_last(&cfs_rq->tasks_timeline.rb_root),
                         sched_entity_t, run_node);
    
    if (rightmost) {
        curr->vruntime = rightmost->vruntime + 1;
    }
    
    set_tsk_need_resched(current);
}

/* Pick Next Task */
thread_t *cfs_pick_next_task(rq_t *rq)
{
    cfs_rq_t *cfs_rq = &rq->cfs;
    sched_entity_t *se;
    
    if (!cfs_rq->nr_running) {
        return NULL;
    }
    
    /* Put Previous */
    if (cfs_rq->curr) {
        put_prev_entity(cfs_rq, cfs_rq->curr);
    }
    
    /* Pick Next */
    se = pick_next_entity(cfs_rq);
    
    if (!se) {
        return NULL;
    }
    
    set_next_entity(cfs_rq, se);
    
    return container_of(se, thread_t, se);
}

/* Scheduler Tick */
void cfs_task_tick(rq_t *rq, thread_t *curr)
{
    cfs_rq_t *cfs_rq = &rq->cfs;
    sched_entity_t *se = &curr->se;
    
    /* Update Runtime */
    update_curr(cfs_rq);
    
    /* Check Preemption */
    if (cfs_rq->nr_running > 1) {
        check_preempt_tick(cfs_rq, se);
    }
}

/* Task Fork */
void cfs_task_fork(thread_t *p)
{
    rq_t *rq = this_rq();
    cfs_rq_t *cfs_rq = &rq->cfs;
    sched_entity_t *se = &p->se;
    sched_entity_t *curr = cfs_rq->curr;
    
    spin_lock(&rq->lock);
    
    update_curr(cfs_rq);
    
    if (curr) {
        se->vruntime = curr->vruntime;
    }
    
    place_entity(cfs_rq, se, 1);
    
    spin_unlock(&rq->lock);
}

/* Set Nice Value */
void cfs_set_nice(thread_t *p, int nice)
{
    rq_t *rq = task_rq(p);
    sched_entity_t *se = &p->se;
    cfs_rq_t *cfs_rq = &rq->cfs;
    int old_nice = PRIO_TO_NICE(p->static_prio);
    s64 delta;
    
    nice = CLAMP(nice, MIN_NICE, MAX_NICE);
    
    if (nice == old_nice) return;
    
    spin_lock(&rq->lock);
    
    if (se->on_rq) {
        dequeue_entity(cfs_rq, se, 0);
    }
    
    /* Adjust vruntime for Weight Change */
    delta = se->vruntime - cfs_rq->min_vruntime;
    delta = (delta * se->load.weight) / sched_prio_to_weight[NICE_TO_PRIO(nice)];
    se->vruntime = cfs_rq->min_vruntime + delta;
    
    p->static_prio = NICE_TO_PRIO(nice);
    set_load_weight(se, nice);
    
    if (se->on_rq) {
        enqueue_entity(cfs_rq, se, 0);
    }
    
    spin_unlock(&rq->lock);
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                     CFS INITIALIZATION                                    */
/*===========================================================================*/

void cfs_rq_init(cfs_rq_t *cfs_rq, rq_t *rq)
{
    cfs_rq->tasks_timeline = RB_ROOT_CACHED;
    cfs_rq->min_vruntime = (u64)(-(1LL << 20));
    cfs_rq->nr_running = 0;
    cfs_rq->load.weight = 0;
    cfs_rq->curr = NULL;
    cfs_rq->next = NULL;
    cfs_rq->last = NULL;
    cfs_rq->skip = NULL;
    cfs_rq->rq = rq;
    cfs_rq->cpu = rq->cpu;
}

void cfs_init(void)
{
    pr_info("Initializing CFS scheduler...\n");
    
    /* Initialize Per-CPU Run Queues */
    for (int cpu = 0; cpu < get_num_cpus(); cpu++) {
        rq_t *rq = cpu_rq(cpu);
        
        spin_lock_init(&rq->lock);
        rq->nr_running = 0;
        rq->cpu = cpu;
        rq->online = true;
        
        cfs_rq_init(&rq->cfs, rq);
    }
    
    pr_info("CFS scheduler initialized.\n");
}
```

## 1.2 Real-Time Scheduler (kernel/sched/rt.c)

```c
/*
 * NEXUS OS - Real-Time Scheduler
 * kernel/sched/rt.c
 */

#include <kernel.h>
#include <sched/scheduler.h>
#include <sched/rt.h>

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                      RT SCHEDULER STRUCTURES                              */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* RT Priority Range */
#define RT_PRIO_MIN         1
#define RT_PRIO_MAX         99
#define MAX_RT_PRIO         100

/* RT Scheduling Policies */
#define SCHED_FIFO          1
#define SCHED_RR            2
#define SCHED_DEADLINE      6

/* RT Run Queue */
typedef struct rt_rq {
    /* Priority Queue (Array of Lists) */
    struct rt_prio_array {
        DECLARE_BITMAP(bitmap, MAX_RT_PRIO);
        struct list_head queue[MAX_RT_PRIO];
    } active;
    
    /* Number of Running RT Tasks */
    u32 rt_nr_running;
    u32 rr_nr_running;
    
    /* Total Weight */
    u64 rt_runtime;
    
    /* Throttle */
    bool rt_throttled;
    u64 rt_time;
    u64 rt_runtime_limit;
    
    /* Round Robin Time Slice */
    u64 rr_time_slice;
    
    /* Highest Priority */
    int highest_prio;
    
    /* Current RT Task */
    struct rt_sched_entity *curr;
    
    /* CPU */
    int cpu;
    struct rq *rq;
    
    /* Push/Pull */
    int overloaded;
    struct list_head pushable_tasks;
    
} rt_rq_t;

/* RT Scheduling Entity */
typedef struct rt_sched_entity {
    /* Priority List */
    struct list_head run_list;
    
    /* Timeout for SCHED_RR */
    u64 timeout;
    u64 time_slice;
    
    /* Watchdog */
    u64 watchdog_stamp;
    
    /* Priority */
    int prio;
    
    /* Policy */
    int policy;
    
    /* State */
    bool on_rq;
    bool on_list;
    
    /* Parent */
    struct rt_sched_entity *parent;
    struct rt_rq *rt_rq;
    struct rt_rq *my_q;
    
    /* Pushable Tasks */
    struct list_head pushable_list;
    
} rt_sched_entity_t;

/* Deadline Entity */
typedef struct dl_sched_entity {
    /* RB-Tree for Deadline Sorting */
    struct rb_node rb_node;
    
    /* Deadline Parameters */
    u64 dl_runtime;     /* Maximum Runtime per Period */
    u64 dl_deadline;    /* Relative Deadline */
    u64 dl_period;      /* Period */
    u64 dl_bw;          /* Bandwidth = runtime / period */
    u64 dl_density;     /* Density = runtime / deadline */
    
    /* Absolute Deadlines */
    u64 deadline;       /* Absolute Deadline */
    u64 runtime;        /* Remaining Runtime */
    
    /* State */
    enum {
        DL_TASK_IDLE,
        DL_TASK_RUNNING,
        DL_TASK_ACTIVE,
    } state;
    
    /* Flags */
    bool dl_throttled;
    bool dl_boosted;
    bool dl_yielded;
    bool dl_non_contending;
    
    /* Timer for Replenishment */
    timer_t dl_timer;
    
    /* Statistics */
    u64 dl_overrun;
    
} dl_sched_entity_t;

/* Deadline Run Queue */
typedef struct dl_rq {
    /* RB-Tree of Deadline Tasks */
    struct rb_root_cached root;
    
    /* Running Stats */
    u32 dl_nr_running;
    
    /* Earliest Deadline */
    sched_entity_t *earliest;
    u64 earliest_dl;
    
    /* Bandwidth */
    u64 running_bw;
    u64 this_bw;
    u64 total_bw;
    
    /* Pushable Tasks */
    struct rb_root_cached pushable_dl_tasks;
    
    /* CPU */
    int cpu;
    struct rq *rq;
    
} dl_rq_t;

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                      RT QUEUE OPERATIONS                                  */
/*===========================================================================*/

static void rt_rq_init(rt_rq_t *rt_rq, rq_t *rq)
{
    /* Initialize Priority Array */
    for (int i = 0; i < MAX_RT_PRIO; i++) {
        INIT_LIST_HEAD(&rt_rq->active.queue[i]);
    }
    bitmap_zero(rt_rq->active.bitmap, MAX_RT_PRIO);
    
    rt_rq->rt_nr_running = 0;
    rt_rq->highest_prio = MAX_RT_PRIO;
    rt_rq->rt_throttled = false;
    rt_rq->rt_time = 0;
    rt_rq->rt_runtime_limit = 950000000ULL;  /* 950ms per second */
    rt_rq->rr_time_slice = 100000000ULL;     /* 100ms */
    rt_rq->curr = NULL;
    rt_rq->rq = rq;
    rt_rq->cpu = rq->cpu;
    
    INIT_LIST_HEAD(&rt_rq->pushable_tasks);
}

/* Find First Set Bit */
static int find_highest_prio(rt_rq_t *rt_rq)
{
    int idx = find_first_bit(rt_rq->active.bitmap, MAX_RT_PRIO);
    
    if (idx >= MAX_RT_PRIO) {
        return MAX_RT_PRIO;
    }
    
    return idx;
}

/* Update Highest Priority */
static void update_rt_highest_prio(rt_rq_t *rt_rq, int prio)
{
    if (prio < rt_rq->highest_prio) {
        rt_rq->highest_prio = prio;
    }
}

/* Recompute Highest Priority */
static void recompute_rt_highest_prio(rt_rq_t *rt_rq)
{
    rt_rq->highest_prio = find_highest_prio(rt_rq);
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                      RT ENQUEUE/DEQUEUE                                   */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Enqueue RT Task */
static void enqueue_rt_entity(rt_rq_t *rt_rq, rt_sched_entity_t *rt_se, int flags)
{
    struct list_head *queue = &rt_rq->active.queue[rt_se->prio];
    
    if (flags & ENQUEUE_HEAD) {
        list_add(&rt_se->run_list, queue);
    } else {
        list_add_tail(&rt_se->run_list, queue);
    }
    
    __set_bit(rt_se->prio, rt_rq->active.bitmap);
    
    rt_se->on_rq = true;
    rt_se->on_list = true;
    
    rt_rq->rt_nr_running++;
    
    update_rt_highest_prio(rt_rq, rt_se->prio);
}

/* Dequeue RT Task */
static void dequeue_rt_entity(rt_rq_t *rt_rq, rt_sched_entity_t *rt_se)
{
    list_del_init(&rt_se->run_list);
    
    if (list_empty(&rt_rq->active.queue[rt_se->prio])) {
        __clear_bit(rt_se->prio, rt_rq->active.bitmap);
    }
    
    rt_se->on_rq = false;
    rt_se->on_list = false;
    
    rt_rq->rt_nr_running--;
    
    if (rt_se->prio == rt_rq->highest_prio) {
        recompute_rt_highest_prio(rt_rq);
    }
}

/* Requeue RT Task (for Round Robin) */
static void requeue_rt_entity(rt_rq_t *rt_rq, rt_sched_entity_t *rt_se)
{
    if (rt_se->on_rq) {
        struct list_head *queue = &rt_rq->active.queue[rt_se->prio];
        list_move_tail(&rt_se->run_list, queue);
    }
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                      RT TASK PICKING                                      */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Pick Highest Priority RT Task */
static rt_sched_entity_t *pick_next_rt_entity(rt_rq_t *rt_rq)
{
    int prio = rt_rq->highest_prio;
    
    if (prio >= MAX_RT_PRIO) {
        return NULL;
    }
    
    struct list_head *queue = &rt_rq->active.queue[prio];
    
    if (list_empty(queue)) {
        return NULL;
    }
    
    return list_first_entry(queue, rt_sched_entity_t, run_list);
}

/* Set Current RT Entity */
static void set_next_rt_entity(rt_rq_t *rt_rq, rt_sched_entity_t *rt_se)
{
    rt_rq->curr = rt_se;
    
    if (rt_se->policy == SCHED_RR) {
        rt_se->time_slice = rt_rq->rr_time_slice;
    }
}

/* Put Previous RT Entity */
static void put_prev_rt_entity(rt_rq_t *rt_rq, rt_sched_entity_t *rt_se)
{
    rt_rq->curr = NULL;
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                      RT SCHEDULER TICK                                    */
/*===========================================================================*/

static void rt_task_tick(rq_t *rq, thread_t *curr)
{
    rt_rq_t *rt_rq = &rq->rt;
    rt_sched_entity_t *rt_se = &curr->rt;
    
    /* Update Runtime */
    rt_rq->rt_time += TICK_NSEC;
    
    /* Check Throttle */
    if (rt_rq->rt_time >= rt_rq->rt_runtime_limit) {
        rt_rq->rt_throttled = true;
        set_tsk_need_resched(curr);
        return;
    }
    
    /* SCHED_FIFO Never Preempts on Tick */
    if (rt_se->policy == SCHED_FIFO) {
        return;
    }
    
    /* SCHED_RR Time Slice */
    if (rt_se->policy == SCHED_RR) {
        if (rt_se->time_slice > TICK_NSEC) {
            rt_se->time_slice -= TICK_NSEC;
            return;
        }
        
        /* Time Slice Expired */
        rt_se->time_slice = rt_rq->rr_time_slice;
        
        /* Requeue to End of Priority Queue */
        requeue_rt_entity(rt_rq, rt_se);
        
        set_tsk_need_resched(curr);
    }
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                      RT PUBLIC INTERFACE                                  */
/*===========================================================================*/

void rt_enqueue_task(rq_t *rq, thread_t *p, int flags)
{
    rt_rq_t *rt_rq = &rq->rt;
    rt_sched_entity_t *rt_se = &p->rt;
    
    enqueue_rt_entity(rt_rq, rt_se, flags);
    
    rq->nr_running++;
}

void rt_dequeue_task(rq_t *rq, thread_t *p, int flags)
{
    rt_rq_t *rt_rq = &rq->rt;
    rt_sched_entity_t *rt_se = &p->rt;
    
    dequeue_rt_entity(rt_rq, rt_se);
    
    rq->nr_running--;
}

thread_t *rt_pick_next_task(rq_t *rq)
{
    rt_rq_t *rt_rq = &rq->rt;
    rt_sched_entity_t *rt_se;
    
    /* Check Throttle */
    if (rt_rq->rt_throttled) {
        return NULL;
    }
    
    rt_se = pick_next_rt_entity(rt_rq);
    
    if (!rt_se) {
        return NULL;
    }
    
    if (rt_rq->curr) {
        put_prev_rt_entity(rt_rq, rt_rq->curr);
    }
    
    set_next_rt_entity(rt_rq, rt_se);
    
    return container_of(rt_se, thread_t, rt);
}

void rt_check_preempt(rq_t *rq, thread_t *p)
{
    rt_rq_t *rt_rq = &rq->rt;
    rt_sched_entity_t *curr = rt_rq->curr;
    rt_sched_entity_t *rt_se = &p->rt;
    
    if (!curr) {
        set_tsk_need_resched(rq->curr);
        return;
    }
    
    /* Higher Priority (Lower Number) Preempts */
    if (rt_se->prio < curr->prio) {
        set_tsk_need_resched(rq->curr);
    }
}

/* Set RT Priority */
int rt_set_priority(thread_t *p, int policy, int prio)
{
    rq_t *rq;
    rt_sched_entity_t *rt_se = &p->rt;
    bool queued, running;
    
    if (prio < RT_PRIO_MIN || prio > RT_PRIO_MAX) {
        return -NEXUS_EINVAL;
    }
    
    if (policy != SCHED_FIFO && policy != SCHED_RR) {
        return -NEXUS_EINVAL;
    }
    
    rq = task_rq_lock(p);
    
    queued = rt_se->on_rq;
    running = (rq->curr == p);
    
    if (queued) {
        dequeue_rt_entity(&rq->rt, rt_se);
    }
    
    rt_se->prio = prio;
    rt_se->policy = policy;
    
    if (queued) {
        enqueue_rt_entity(&rq->rt, rt_se, 0);
    }
    
    task_rq_unlock(rq);
    
    return NEXUS_OK;
}

void rt_init(void)
{
    pr_info("Initializing RT scheduler...\n");
    
    for (int cpu = 0; cpu < get_num_cpus(); cpu++) {
        rq_t *rq = cpu_rq(cpu);
        rt_rq_init(&rq->rt, rq);
    }
    
    pr_info("RT scheduler initialized.\n");
}
```

# 2. USB STACK

## 2.1 USB Core (drivers/usb/usb_core.c)

```c
/*
 * NEXUS OS - USB Core
 * drivers/usb/usb_core.c
 */

#include <kernel.h>
#include <drivers/usb.h>
#include <drivers/pci.h>

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                         USB CONSTANTS                                     */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* USB Speeds */
#define USB_SPEED_LOW           1       /* 1.5 Mbps */
#define USB_SPEED_FULL          2       /* 12 Mbps */
#define USB_SPEED_HIGH          3       /* 480 Mbps */
#define USB_SPEED_SUPER         4       /* 5 Gbps */
#define USB_SPEED_SUPER_PLUS    5       /* 10 Gbps */

/* USB Descriptor Types */
#define USB_DT_DEVICE           0x01
#define USB_DT_CONFIG           0x02
#define USB_DT_STRING           0x03
#define USB_DT_INTERFACE        0x04
#define USB_DT_ENDPOINT         0x05
#define USB_DT_HID              0x21
#define USB_DT_HUB              0x29
#define USB_DT_SS_HUB           0x2A

/* USB Request Types */
#define USB_DIR_OUT             0x00
#define USB_DIR_IN              0x80
#define USB_TYPE_STANDARD       0x00
#define USB_TYPE_CLASS          0x20
#define USB_TYPE_VENDOR         0x40
#define USB_RECIP_DEVICE        0x00
#define USB_RECIP_INTERFACE     0x01
#define USB_RECIP_ENDPOINT      0x02
#define USB_RECIP_OTHER         0x03

/* USB Standard Requests */
#define USB_REQ_GET_STATUS          0x00
#define USB_REQ_CLEAR_FEATURE       0x01
#define USB_REQ_SET_FEATURE         0x03
#define USB_REQ_SET_ADDRESS         0x05
#define USB_REQ_GET_DESCRIPTOR      0x06
#define USB_REQ_SET_DESCRIPTOR      0x07
#define USB_REQ_GET_CONFIGURATION   0x08
#define USB_REQ_SET_CONFIGURATION   0x09
#define USB_REQ_GET_INTERFACE       0x0A
#define USB_REQ_SET_INTERFACE       0x0B

/* USB Device Classes */
#define USB_CLASS_PER_INTERFACE     0x00
#define USB_CLASS_AUDIO             0x01
#define USB_CLASS_COMM              0x02
#define USB_CLASS_HID               0x03
#define USB_CLASS_PHYSICAL          0x05
#define USB_CLASS_IMAGE             0x06
#define USB_CLASS_PRINTER           0x07
#define USB_CLASS_MASS_STORAGE      0x08
#define USB_CLASS_HUB               0x09
#define USB_CLASS_CDC_DATA          0x0A
#define USB_CLASS_VIDEO             0x0E
#define USB_CLASS_WIRELESS          0xE0
#define USB_CLASS_VENDOR_SPEC       0xFF

/* Endpoint Types */
#define USB_ENDPOINT_XFER_CONTROL   0x00
#define USB_ENDPOINT_XFER_ISOC      0x01
#define USB_ENDPOINT_XFER_BULK      0x02
#define USB_ENDPOINT_XFER_INT       0x03

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                         USB STRUCTURES                                    */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* USB Setup Packet */
typedef struct usb_setup_packet {
    u8 bmRequestType;
    u8 bRequest;
    u16 wValue;
    u16 wIndex;
    u16 wLength;
} __packed usb_setup_packet_t;

/* USB Device Descriptor */
typedef struct usb_device_descriptor {
    u8 bLength;
    u8 bDescriptorType;
    u16 bcdUSB;
    u8 bDeviceClass;
    u8 bDeviceSubClass;
    u8 bDeviceProtocol;
    u8 bMaxPacketSize0;
    u16 idVendor;
    u16 idProduct;
    u16 bcdDevice;
    u8 iManufacturer;
    u8 iProduct;
    u8 iSerialNumber;
    u8 bNumConfigurations;
} __packed usb_device_descriptor_t;

/* USB Configuration Descriptor */
typedef struct usb_config_descriptor {
    u8 bLength;
    u8 bDescriptorType;
    u16 wTotalLength;
    u8 bNumInterfaces;
    u8 bConfigurationValue;
    u8 iConfiguration;
    u8 bmAttributes;
    u8 bMaxPower;
} __packed usb_config_descriptor_t;

/* USB Interface Descriptor */
typedef struct usb_interface_descriptor {
    u8 bLength;
    u8 bDescriptorType;
    u8 bInterfaceNumber;
    u8 bAlternateSetting;
    u8 bNumEndpoints;
    u8 bInterfaceClass;
    u8 bInterfaceSubClass;
    u8 bInterfaceProtocol;
    u8 iInterface;
} __packed usb_interface_descriptor_t;

/* USB Endpoint Descriptor */
typedef struct usb_endpoint_descriptor {
    u8 bLength;
    u8 bDescriptorType;
    u8 bEndpointAddress;
    u8 bmAttributes;
    u16 wMaxPacketSize;
    u8 bInterval;
} __packed usb_endpoint_descriptor_t;

/* USB URB (USB Request Block) */
typedef struct usb_urb {
    /* Device */
    struct usb_device *dev;
    
    /* Endpoint */
    u8 endpoint;
    u8 direction;
    u8 type;
    
    /* Transfer */
    void *transfer_buffer;
    dma_addr_t transfer_dma;
    u32 transfer_buffer_length;
    u32 actual_length;
    
    /* Setup Packet (for Control) */
    usb_setup_packet_t *setup_packet;
    dma_addr_t setup_dma;
    
    /* Status */
    int status;
    int error_count;
    
    /* Flags */
    u32 flags;
    #define URB_SHORT_NOT_OK    BIT(0)
    #define URB_ISO_ASAP        BIT(1)
    #define URB_NO_TRANSFER_DMA BIT(2)
    #define URB_ZERO_PACKET     BIT(3)
    
    /* Completion */
    void (*complete)(struct usb_urb *urb);
    void *context;
    
    /* Isochronous */
    int number_of_packets;
    int interval;
    int start_frame;
    
    struct {
        u32 offset;
        u32 length;
        u32 actual_length;
        int status;
    } iso_frame_desc[0];
    
    /* Internal */
    struct list_head urb_list;
    struct list_head anchor_list;
    spinlock_t lock;
    atomic_t use_count;
    
} usb_urb_t;

/* USB Endpoint */
typedef struct usb_endpoint {
    usb_endpoint_descriptor_t desc;
    
    /* URB List */
    struct list_head urb_list;
    
    /* State */
    bool enabled;
    bool halted;
    
    /* Statistics */
    u64 bytes_transferred;
    u32 errors;
    
} usb_endpoint_t;

/* USB Interface */
typedef struct usb_interface {
    usb_interface_descriptor_t *cur_altsetting;
    usb_interface_descriptor_t *altsettings;
    u32 num_altsetting;
    
    /* Endpoints */
    usb_endpoint_t *endpoints;
    u32 num_endpoints;
    
    /* Driver */
    struct usb_driver *driver;
    void *driver_data;
    
    /* Device */
    struct usb_device *dev;
    
    /* State */
    bool claimed;
    
} usb_interface_t;

/* USB Device */
typedef struct usb_device {
    /* Device Info */
    u32 devnum;
    char devpath[16];
    
    /* Descriptors */
    usb_device_descriptor_t descriptor;
    usb_config_descriptor_t *config;
    usb_interface_t *interfaces;
    u32 num_interfaces;
    
    /* Strings */
    char manufacturer[64];
    char product[64];
    char serial[64];
    
    /* Speed */
    u8 speed;
    
    /* Endpoints */
    usb_endpoint_t ep0_in;
    usb_endpoint_t ep0_out;
    usb_endpoint_t *endpoints[32];
    
    /* State */
    enum {
        USB_STATE_NOTATTACHED,
        USB_STATE_ATTACHED,
        USB_STATE_POWERED,
        USB_STATE_RECONNECTING,
        USB_STATE_UNAUTHENTICATED,
        USB_STATE_DEFAULT,
        USB_STATE_ADDRESS,
        USB_STATE_CONFIGURED,
        USB_STATE_SUSPENDED,
    } state;
    
    /* Parent Hub */
    struct usb_device *parent;
    struct usb_hub *hub;
    u8 port_num;
    
    /* Host Controller */
    struct usb_hcd *hcd;
    
    /* Reference Count */
    atomic_t refcount;
    
    /* Lock */
    struct mutex dev_mutex;
    
    /* List */
    struct list_head dev_list;
    
} usb_device_t;

/* USB Driver */
typedef struct usb_driver {
    const char *name;
    
    /* Probe/Disconnect */
    int (*probe)(usb_interface_t *intf, const struct usb_device_id *id);
    void (*disconnect)(usb_interface_t *intf);
    
    /* Power Management */
    int (*suspend)(usb_interface_t *intf, u32 message);
    int (*resume)(usb_interface_t *intf);
    int (*reset_resume)(usb_interface_t *intf);
    
    /* URB Callbacks */
    int (*pre_reset)(usb_interface_t *intf);
    int (*post_reset)(usb_interface_t *intf);
    
    /* ID Table */
    const struct usb_device_id *id_table;
    
    /* Dynamic ID Support */
    struct list_head dynids;
    spinlock_t dynids_lock;
    
    /* Driver Model */
    struct device_driver driver;
    
    /* List */
    struct list_head driver_list;
    
} usb_driver_t;

/* USB Device ID */
struct usb_device_id {
    u16 match_flags;
    #define USB_DEVICE_ID_MATCH_VENDOR      BIT(0)
    #define USB_DEVICE_ID_MATCH_PRODUCT     BIT(1)
    #define USB_DEVICE_ID_MATCH_DEV_CLASS   BIT(2)
    #define USB_DEVICE_ID_MATCH_INT_CLASS   BIT(3)
    
    u16 idVendor;
    u16 idProduct;
    u16 bcdDevice_lo;
    u16 bcdDevice_hi;
    
    u8 bDeviceClass;
    u8 bDeviceSubClass;
    u8 bDeviceProtocol;
    
    u8 bInterfaceClass;
    u8 bInterfaceSubClass;
    u8 bInterfaceProtocol;
    
    void *driver_info;
};

/* USB Host Controller Driver */
typedef struct usb_hcd {
    /* Controller Info */
    const char *product_desc;
    const char *driver_name;
    
    /* Resources */
    void __iomem *regs;
    phys_addr_t rsrc_start;
    size_t rsrc_len;
    u32 irq;
    
    /* Root Hub */
    usb_device_t *root_hub;
    
    /* Device Pool */
    struct list_head device_list;
    u32 next_devnum;
    
    /* URB Processing */
    struct list_head urb_list;
    spinlock_t urb_lock;
    
    /* State */
    bool rh_registered;
    bool dead;
    
    /* Operations */
    struct hc_driver *driver;
    
    /* DMA */
    struct dma_pool *pool[4];
    
    /* Private Data */
    void *hcd_priv[0];
    
} usb_hcd_t;

/* Host Controller Operations */
typedef struct hc_driver {
    const char *description;
    const char *product_desc;
    size_t hcd_priv_size;
    
    u32 flags;
    #define HCD_MEMORY      BIT(0)
    #define HCD_USB11       BIT(1)
    #define HCD_USB2        BIT(2)
    #define HCD_USB3        BIT(3)
    #define HCD_MASK        0x0070
    
    /* Lifecycle */
    int (*reset)(usb_hcd_t *hcd);
    int (*start)(usb_hcd_t *hcd);
    void (*stop)(usb_hcd_t *hcd);
    void (*shutdown)(usb_hcd_t *hcd);
    
    /* URB Handling */
    int (*urb_enqueue)(usb_hcd_t *hcd, usb_urb_t *urb, gfp_t flags);
    int (*urb_dequeue)(usb_hcd_t *hcd, usb_urb_t *urb, int status);
    
    /* Endpoint */
    void (*endpoint_disable)(usb_hcd_t *hcd, usb_endpoint_t *ep);
    void (*endpoint_reset)(usb_hcd_t *hcd, usb_endpoint_t *ep);
    
    /* Root Hub */
    int (*hub_status_data)(usb_hcd_t *hcd, char *buf);
    int (*hub_control)(usb_hcd_t *hcd, u16 typeReq, u16 wValue,
                       u16 wIndex, char *buf, u16 wLength);
    
    /* Power Management */
    int (*bus_suspend)(usb_hcd_t *hcd);
    int (*bus_resume)(usb_hcd_t *hcd);
    
    /* Device Management */
    int (*alloc_dev)(usb_hcd_t *hcd, usb_device_t *udev);
    void (*free_dev)(usb_hcd_t *hcd, usb_device_t *udev);
    int (*address_device)(usb_hcd_t *hcd, usb_device_t *udev);
    int (*enable_device)(usb_hcd_t *hcd, usb_device_t *udev);
    
} hc_driver_t;

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                          GLOBAL STATE                                     */
/*===========================================================================*/

static struct {
    /* Host Controllers */
    struct list_head hcd_list;
    spinlock_t hcd_lock;
    
    /* Drivers */
    struct list_head driver_list;
    spinlock_t driver_lock;
    
    /* Devices */
    struct list_head device_list;
    spinlock_t device_lock;
    u32 next_devnum;
    
    /* Workqueue */
    struct workqueue_struct *hub_wq;
    
} usb_core = {
    .hcd_list = LIST_HEAD_INIT(usb_core.hcd_list),
    .driver_list = LIST_HEAD_INIT(usb_core.driver_list),
    .device_list = LIST_HEAD_INIT(usb_core.device_list),
    .next_devnum = 1,
};

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                         URB OPERATIONS                                    */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Allocate URB */
usb_urb_t *usb_alloc_urb(int iso_packets, gfp_t flags)
{
    size_t size = sizeof(usb_urb_t);
    
    if (iso_packets > 0) {
        size += iso_packets * sizeof(struct {
            u32 offset;
            u32 length;
            u32 actual_length;
            int status;
        });
    }
    
    usb_urb_t *urb = kzalloc(size);
    if (!urb) return NULL;
    
    INIT_LIST_HEAD(&urb->urb_list);
    INIT_LIST_HEAD(&urb->anchor_list);
    spin_lock_init(&urb->lock);
    atomic_set(&urb->use_count, 1);
    urb->number_of_packets = iso_packets;
    
    return urb;
}

/* Free URB */
void usb_free_urb(usb_urb_t *urb)
{
    if (urb && atomic_dec_and_test(&urb->use_count)) {
        kfree(urb);
    }
}

/* Get URB Reference */
usb_urb_t *usb_get_urb(usb_urb_t *urb)
{
    if (urb) {
        atomic_inc(&urb->use_count);
    }
    return urb;
}

/* Initialize Control URB */
void usb_fill_control_urb(usb_urb_t *urb, usb_device_t *dev,
                          u8 endpoint, usb_setup_packet_t *setup,
                          void *data, int len,
                          void (*complete)(usb_urb_t *), void *context)
{
    urb->dev = dev;
    urb->endpoint = endpoint;
    urb->direction = setup->bmRequestType & USB_DIR_IN;
    urb->type = USB_ENDPOINT_XFER_CONTROL;
    urb->setup_packet = setup;
    urb->transfer_buffer = data;
    urb->transfer_buffer_length = len;
    urb->complete = complete;
    urb->context = context;
}

/* Initialize Bulk URB */
void usb_fill_bulk_urb(usb_urb_t *urb, usb_device_t *dev,
                       u8 endpoint, void *data, int len,
                       void (*complete)(usb_urb_t *), void *context)
{
    urb->dev = dev;
    urb->endpoint = endpoint & 0x0F;
    urb->direction = endpoint & USB_DIR_IN;
    urb->type = USB_ENDPOINT_XFER_BULK;
    urb->transfer_buffer = data;
    urb->transfer_buffer_length = len;
    urb->complete = complete;
    urb->context = context;
}

/* Initialize Interrupt URB */
void usb_fill_int_urb(usb_urb_t *urb, usb_device_t *dev,
                      u8 endpoint, void *data, int len,
                      void (*complete)(usb_urb_t *), void *context,
                      int interval)
{
    urb->dev = dev;
    urb->endpoint = endpoint & 0x0F;
    urb->direction = endpoint & USB_DIR_IN;
    urb->type = USB_ENDPOINT_XFER_INT;
    urb->transfer_buffer = data;
    urb->transfer_buffer_length = len;
    urb->complete = complete;
    urb->context = context;
    urb->interval = interval;
}

/* Submit URB */
int usb_submit_urb(usb_urb_t *urb, gfp_t flags)
{
    if (!urb || !urb->dev || !urb->dev->hcd) {
        return -NEXUS_EINVAL;
    }
    
    usb_hcd_t *hcd = urb->dev->hcd;
    
    if (hcd->dead) {
        return -NEXUS_ENODEV;
    }
    
    /* Add to URB List */
    spin_lock(&hcd->urb_lock);
    list_add_tail(&urb->urb_list, &hcd->urb_list);
    spin_unlock(&hcd->urb_lock);
    
    /* Submit to HCD */
    int ret = hcd->driver->urb_enqueue(hcd, urb, flags);
    
    if (ret != 0) {
        spin_lock(&hcd->urb_lock);
        list_del(&urb->urb_list);
        spin_unlock(&hcd->urb_lock);
    }
    
    return ret;
}

/* Cancel URB */
int usb_unlink_urb(usb_urb_t *urb)
{
    if (!urb || !urb->dev || !urb->dev->hcd) {
        return -NEXUS_EINVAL;
    }
    
    usb_hcd_t *hcd = urb->dev->hcd;
    
    return hcd->driver->urb_dequeue(hcd, urb, -NEXUS_ECONNRESET);
}

/* URB Completion (called by HCD) */
void usb_hcd_giveback_urb(usb_hcd_t *hcd, usb_urb_t *urb, int status)
{
    /* Remove from List */
    spin_lock(&hcd->urb_lock);
    list_del(&urb->urb_list);
    spin_unlock(&hcd->urb_lock);
    
    urb->status = status;
    
    /* Call Completion Handler */
    if (urb->complete) {
        urb->complete(urb);
    }
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                      CONTROL TRANSFERS                                    */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Synchronous Control Transfer */
int usb_control_msg(usb_device_t *dev, u8 request, u8 requesttype,
                    u16 value, u16 index, void *data, u16 size,
                    int timeout)
{
    usb_setup_packet_t *setup = kzalloc(sizeof(usb_setup_packet_t));
    if (!setup) return -NEXUS_ENOMEM;
    
    setup->bmRequestType = requesttype;
    setup->bRequest = request;
    setup->wValue = cpu_to_le16(value);
    setup->wIndex = cpu_to_le16(index);
    setup->wLength = cpu_to_le16(size);
    
    usb_urb_t *urb = usb_alloc_urb(0, GFP_KERNEL);
    if (!urb) {
        kfree(setup);
        return -NEXUS_ENOMEM;
    }
    
    /* Setup Completion */
    DECLARE_COMPLETION_ONSTACK(done);
    
    usb_fill_control_urb(urb, dev, 0, setup, data, size,
                         usb_control_msg_complete, &done);
    
    /* Submit */
    int ret = usb_submit_urb(urb, GFP_KERNEL);
    
    if (ret == 0) {
        /* Wait for Completion */
        if (!wait_for_completion_timeout(&done, ms_to_jiffies(timeout))) {
            usb_unlink_urb(urb);
            ret = -NEXUS_ETIMEDOUT;
        } else {
            ret = urb->status;
            if (ret == 0) {
                ret = urb->actual_length;
            }
        }
    }
    
    usb_free_urb(urb);
    kfree(setup);
    
    return ret;
}

static void usb_control_msg_complete(usb_urb_t *urb)
{
    complete((struct completion *)urb->context);
}

/* Get Descriptor */
int usb_get_descriptor(usb_device_t *dev, u8 type, u8 index,
                       void *buf, int size)
{
    return usb_control_msg(dev, USB_REQ_GET_DESCRIPTOR,
                           USB_DIR_IN | USB_TYPE_STANDARD | USB_RECIP_DEVICE,
                           (type << 8) | index, 0, buf, size, 5000);
}

/* Set Configuration */
int usb_set_configuration(usb_device_t *dev, int configuration)
{
    int ret = usb_control_msg(dev, USB_REQ_SET_CONFIGURATION,
                              USB_DIR_OUT | USB_TYPE_STANDARD | USB_RECIP_DEVICE,
                              configuration, 0, NULL, 0, 5000);
    
    if (ret == 0) {
        dev->state = USB_STATE_CONFIGURED;
    }
    
    return ret;
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                      DEVICE ENUMERATION                                   */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Enumerate New Device */
int usb_enumerate_device(usb_device_t *dev)
{
    int ret;
    
    pr_info("USB: Enumerating device on port %d\n", dev->port_num);
    
    /* Get Device Descriptor (first 8 bytes for max packet size) */
    usb_device_descriptor_t desc;
    
    ret = usb_get_descriptor(dev, USB_DT_DEVICE, 0, &desc, 8);
    if (ret < 8) {
        pr_err("USB: Failed to get device descriptor\n");
        return -NEXUS_EIO;
    }
    
    /* Set Address */
    spin_lock(&usb_core.device_lock);
    dev->devnum = usb_core.next_devnum++;
    spin_unlock(&usb_core.device_lock);
    
    ret = usb_control_msg(dev, USB_REQ_SET_ADDRESS,
                          USB_DIR_OUT | USB_TYPE_STANDARD | USB_RECIP_DEVICE,
                          dev->devnum, 0, NULL, 0, 5000);
    if (ret < 0) {
        pr_err("USB: Failed to set address\n");
        return ret;
    }
    
    dev->state = USB_STATE_ADDRESS;
    
    /* Wait for Device */
    thread_sleep(10);
    
    /* Get Full Device Descriptor */
    ret = usb_get_descriptor(dev, USB_DT_DEVICE, 0, &dev->descriptor,
                             sizeof(usb_device_descriptor_t));
    if (ret < sizeof(usb_device_descriptor_t)) {
        pr_err("USB: Failed to get full device descriptor\n");
        return -NEXUS_EIO;
    }
    
    pr_info("USB: Device %04x:%04x\n",
            le16_to_cpu(dev->descriptor.idVendor),
            le16_to_cpu(dev->descriptor.idProduct));
    
    /* Get Strings */
    if (dev->descriptor.iManufacturer) {
        usb_get_string(dev, dev->descriptor.iManufacturer,
                       dev->manufacturer, sizeof(dev->manufacturer));
    }
    
    if (dev->descriptor.iProduct) {
        usb_get_string(dev, dev->descriptor.iProduct,
                       dev->product, sizeof(dev->product));
    }
    
    if (dev->descriptor.iSerialNumber) {
        usb_get_string(dev, dev->descriptor.iSerialNumber,
                       dev->serial, sizeof(dev->serial));
    }
    
    pr_info("USB: %s %s (S/N: %s)\n",
            dev->manufacturer, dev->product, dev->serial);
    
    /* Get Configuration */
    ret = usb_get_configuration(dev);
    if (ret < 0) {
        pr_err("USB: Failed to get configuration\n");
        return ret;
    }
    
    /* Set Configuration */
    ret = usb_set_configuration(dev, dev->config->bConfigurationValue);
    if (ret < 0) {
        pr_err("USB: Failed to set configuration\n");
        return ret;
    }
    
    /* Add to Device List */
    spin_lock(&usb_core.device_lock);
    list_add_tail(&dev->dev_list, &usb_core.device_list);
    spin_unlock(&usb_core.device_lock);
    
    /* Probe Drivers */
    usb_probe_device(dev);
    
    return NEXUS_OK;
}

/* Probe Device Against Drivers */
static void usb_probe_device(usb_device_t *dev)
{
    usb_driver_t *driver;
    
    spin_lock(&usb_core.driver_lock);
    
    list_for_each_entry(driver, &usb_core.driver_list, driver_list) {
        for (int i = 0; i < dev->num_interfaces; i++) {
            usb_interface_t *intf = &dev->interfaces[i];
            
            if (intf->claimed) continue;
            
            /* Check ID Table */
            if (usb_match_id(intf, driver->id_table)) {
                spin_unlock(&usb_core.driver_lock);
                
                /* Probe */
                if (driver->probe(intf, usb_match_id(intf, driver->id_table)) == 0) {
                    intf->driver = driver;
                    intf->claimed = true;
                }
                
                spin_lock(&usb_core.driver_lock);
            }
        }
    }
    
    spin_unlock(&usb_core.driver_lock);
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                      DRIVER REGISTRATION                                  */
/*===========================================================================*/

/* Register USB Driver */
int usb_register_driver(usb_driver_t *driver)
{
    spin_lock(&usb_core.driver_lock);
    list_add_tail(&driver->driver_list, &usb_core.driver_list);
    spin_unlock(&usb_core.driver_lock);
    
    pr_info("USB: Registered driver '%s'\n", driver->name);
    
    /* Probe Existing Devices */
    usb_device_t *dev;
    spin_lock(&usb_core.device_lock);
    
    list_for_each_entry(dev, &usb_core.device_list, dev_list) {
        spin_unlock(&usb_core.device_lock);
        usb_probe_device(dev);
        spin_lock(&usb_core.device_lock);
    }
    
    spin_unlock(&usb_core.device_lock);
    
    return NEXUS_OK;
}

/* Unregister USB Driver */
void usb_deregister(usb_driver_t *driver)
{
    /* Disconnect All Devices */
    usb_device_t *dev;
    
    spin_lock(&usb_core.device_lock);
    
    list_for_each_entry(dev, &usb_core.device_list, dev_list) {
        for (int i = 0; i < dev->num_interfaces; i++) {
            usb_interface_t *intf = &dev->interfaces[i];
            
            if (intf->driver == driver) {
                spin_unlock(&usb_core.device_lock);
                
                if (driver->disconnect) {
                    driver->disconnect(intf);
                }
                
                intf->driver = NULL;
                intf->claimed = false;
                
                spin_lock(&usb_core.device_lock);
            }
        }
    }
    
    spin_unlock(&usb_core.device_lock);
    
    /* Remove from List */
    spin_lock(&usb_core.driver_lock);
    list_del(&driver->driver_list);
    spin_unlock(&usb_core.driver_lock);
    
    pr_info("USB: Unregistered driver '%s'\n", driver->name);
}

/*===========================================================================*/
/*                      USB INITIALIZATION                                   */
/*===========================================================================*/

int usb_init(void)
{
    pr_info("Initializing USB subsystem...\n");
    
    spin_lock_init(&usb_core.hcd_lock);
    spin_lock_init(&usb_core.driver_lock);
    spin_lock_init(&usb_core.device_lock);
    
    /* Create Hub Workqueue */
    usb_core.hub_wq = create_workqueue("usb_hub_wq");
    
    /* Initialize XHCI Driver */
    xhci_init();
    
    pr_info("USB subsystem initialized.\n");
    return NEXUS_OK;
}
```

I'll continue with more components. Due to the length, I'll provide a summary of what else should be added and then continue with key implementations.
